 Michael dusted his pants himself and spoke "No, You didn't! You bothered me!" 
Tina stopped laughing. She put her hands on her hips of her jeans. 
She spoke "So? I scared you anyway!"  
She looked at the book Michael threw at her.
Rolling her eyes she asked "Mike, Are you still interested in this stuff about Native Americans? You know Mom won't approve you reading it."
She bent to pick the book up as Michael glared. Then he ran and snatched the book out of his sister Tina's hands and ran down the staircase slamming the door.
Tina sighed and said "Boys! Go figure!"  
When she heard a meow sounded from the Trio's cat Hocus. The Trio was Michael, his sister Tina and seventeen year old Samuel Benson. Tina spoke to the cat, "Oh Hocus, where you been?" 
 She stroked the black cat's fur coat. He meowed in reply and rubbed his head in her face before rubbing his tail across her nose. Tina laughed and picked up Hocus. Then she went downstairs of the apartment building. The Ryan family was mostly Mrs. Claire Ryan, Michael and Tina including a female mixed breed not identified despite claims of wolf/dog hybrid said in their faces soon after adopting her from the pound only answering to the name of Nanook and balking on answering to other names they gave her. They lived in the city suburbs in an apartment in Wolfville, Connecticut. Claire Ryan, the mother, was the cleaning lady of the small six story building called Burke's apartments. She was employed under the land owner Mrs. Billie Burke. Under Mrs. Burke's watchful eye, Michael, Tina, and Sam Benson the only kids in the building were the blame of things when their jokes and playing got too rowdy for the neighbors and residents living in the building. 

Walking down the stairs to the apartment Michael remembered that his Father Octaves Ryan walked out of the family in a fight with his Mother Claire Ryan leaving her with him and Tina. His Father later divorced her later, and died in a plane crash, leaving Claire as a widow and single Mother to Michael and his younger sister Tina. The three used to live in a house in a town in Connecticut but Claire fell on problems of bills and was laid out from her job as a bookseller that she had to sell the house. She packed her two children Michael who was thirteen years old and Tina ten years old, and drove them to Wolfville in another part of Connecticut while looking for a home. Arriving in Wolfville it was days before Claire found both a job and a home for her and her children. It took time for them to get used to the ways of Wolfville while living in the new century including the year of 2000 including a surprised adoption of Nanook by their Mother who always claimed she got her from the pound despite rumors among the city's folks overheard commenting about some loose dog wandering around the neighborhood that hadn't been found or seen since. It has been two years for the Ryan kids being the only kids in the building. Till one afternoon two years ago before the year 2000 arrived, when it was early September before schools would start in. Michael was age fifteen and Tina his younger sister was age twelve, bored sat on the steps leading to the apartment building. Tina sat on the steps wearing sneakers and pink sweats with a white turtleneck long sleeved shirt. She had a blue jacket on. Her long shoulder length brown hair was tied in a ponytail, swayed in the wind. Michael sat opposite from her. He had on blue faded jeans, sneakers and was wearing a red sweatshirt with a denim jacket slung on the banister as he sat bouncing and playing with a basketball. His short brown hair with streaks of blonde swayed in the wind. The traffic on the street was low, with few people mostly adults were walking by. It was a boring dearly life, living in a neighborhood with no kids around their age was beginning to be a drag, to them. Then suddenly a big green truck stopped at Burke's apartments. Men came out of the truck and started taking things out of the truck and were carrying them inside. A black car stopped in front of the truck and out came a red brown haired man in a suit. A red brown haired woman in some purple Sunday dress came out and behind her was a blonde haired boy with brown eyes about Michael’s age in faded blue jeans; tan hiking boots and a blue shirt. He was carrying a black cat. Michael looked up and saw what the commotion was. He nudged his sister Tina from reading a book. She looked up and scooted over to Michael in time. For there were some men carrying stuff up the stairs. The boy's parents went inside with the movers. The blonde haired boy was left outside. 
Carrying the cat he sat next to Tina and said "Hi! Sam Benson, The cat's name is Hocus and it's a he." 
This marked the beginning of a friendship between the three which were later called the Trio by the apartment building's natives.

Chapter two

They have been living in the apartment building having fun of thinking up jokes to play on Mrs. Burke, to get back at her for being a meanie and not having a good sense of humor to their jokes played onto her. 
One night around midnight sixteen year old Sam who was sleeping over in the Ryan apartment, dared sixteen year old Michael to go up into the attic. The boys also woke up Tina because they wanted her to share the fun. The three went into the hallway careful not to wake up Claire, armed with flashlights because it was dark. When the Trio got to the attic the flashlights died out. Then a white glowing figure with chains leaped at them. All three were suddenly grabbed from behind by people who dumped stuff like feathers on them. There were booms of laugher. Someone turned the lights on then there was a scream. The screamer was Claire who turned the light on and saw three people in feathery attire draped around them. The Trio was surprised as Claire to see everyone who was living in the building was there. The white figure took a mask he was wearing off.
The figure said "I hope it will teach you trio, not to play any jokes when we don't like it."
Michael groaned, for he recognized the voice belonging to Mrs. Burke. 
Mrs. Burke spoke in a serious voice "I have permission from the Bensons and Claire that you can play in the attic whenever you want. But" holding a finger up, like a Mother lecturing "Play your jokes onto each other in the attic period." 

Chapter three

For as many times they could, the Trio would sometimes go in the attic and look around, maybe to explore. That was when Michael opened box full of books. As he was looking through when he found a book and became in grossed reading when his sister Tina started him. Sam with Nanook was exploring stuff when the attic door slammed. He looked up in time to see Tina carrying Hocus go down the attic stairs. 
He yelled "Hey Tee Na! Wait for me! I'm coming!" 
He did a jump over some boxes and ran down the attic staircase with Nanook trailing at his heels yapping.

In the Ryan apartment, Claire Ryan was on the phone angrily. 
She was saying " What?! " pause "I've got two kids, to take care of and you have to dump Sam on me?" 
Then she slammed the phone down on the table so hard that it bounced off and fell off the table.
Michael who came in asked "Dump Sam on you?"
Claire looked at her son. She he saw ran a hand through her brown spiked hair.
Then she spoke "It was the Bensons, they dumped Sam on me."
She added to herself he overheard "Forcefully"
Then she spoke "I was told from Taylor Benson, Sam's mom. The Bensons were going to live here for Sam to make friends but because of her husband Alex's job, at the Briny Modeling Agency." 
She paused and then said "They have to travel to Europe to live and work for the company for half of the school year. Taylor explained to me that she doesn't want Sam to miss any school work and besides she didn't want Sam to go to a boarding school." 
His Mother Michael noticed seemed to sense Sam and Tina standing in the doorway silently next to him smiled said "Hi Sam! Your parents called on the phone, and we'll to take you in while their in Europe for your Father's job." 
She surprised them by saying after groans were heard "Anybody for pizza because I'm ordering." 
Tina sighed for relief, for her Mother was never a good cook.

Chapter four

Since the day Sam was joined as a member of the Ryan family. Life couldn't have been better without Sam's comedy routines using swear words such as “fuck and shit”. School was in Tina's liking but the boys complained. One day in June the Trio were home from school and were in the attic talking about the last day of school which was tomorrow when Claire came home early from her cleaning job.
She came up the attic stairs where she yelled "Boys! Tina! Get down here! I got news from Sam's parents in Europe!" 
There was a clatter of thudding of three pairs of feet along with yapping and meows from the pets. Claire was holding a piece of paper. 
She handed it to Sam saying "Here read it."
Sam noticing the look on her face that it wasn't good. 
He read out loud "Dear Sam, How are things going? Your Dad got a promotion. So it looks like, we will have to stay longer than I thought. We're coming home soon to get you. Your Father thinks you should stay with us, so when you get to Europe we'll take you on a tour of Europe then off to boarding school where you'll stay till you're eighteen. Is that fantastic? You will finally be with boys your age. Affectingly Mom Taylor Benson."
Sam crumpled the letter and said "Fuck it! I wish their plane would crash. They weren't my parents anyway."
Tina asked "Wait a minute! You’re adopted?"
Sam answered, "Yup, since I was a baby I never knew my parents. My name used to be some name called Wilson something but Taylor insisted I change my name to Samuel Benson"
At the sound of the name Wilson, Claire stiffened unnoticed.
Claire got her pocket book and said "Come on guys! Anyone for Italian food, a going away celebration for Sam."
A weak chorus of “All Rights!” was heard by Claire who sighed. It would hurt that Sam was going away after a lengthy friendship. The four left the apartment. 

Chapter five

It was long after dark when they came back home. After eating at an Italian restaurant, they went to an arcade where the boys played games with Tina sometimes. 
Claire opened the apartment door and spoke "Tina, boys it's time for bed school is tomorrow and you don't want to miss it."
Sighing and yawning Tina managed to carry the cat Hocus and went into her bedroom. The boys dawdled before Claire rushed them into their bedroom. An hour later of watching the news Claire yawned and went to bed. Up on the roof of the apartment building in the dark sat a figure. The figure was a man in ripped blue jeans and a blue ripped T-shirt. His hair was long blonde perm and a little spiked. Silently he jumped off the building to the fire escape. His form changed to a wolf as he ran down the fire escape. 
He ran out of the city suburbs to the forest on the edge of the city till he reached a figure in black with features hidden in a hood stood spoke in a muffled voice, "Report Daniel."
Daniel answered the figure "I have sighted the male under the name Michael Ryan that can be another candidate."
The figure in black person spoke "Time to wait and see if Michael will join us."
Daniel spoke "If he tries to refuse?"
"He won't for you'll choose for him” said the figure in black.
Daniel hearing that nodded his head in agreement. 

Chapter six

It was early in the morning when Claire roused the kids. The boys groaned and moaned as they woke up and dressed. Tina woke up immediately and dressed. The boys came into the kitchen to eat. Sam fed the cat while Tina gave Nanook her unusual dog chow.
Claire yelled "Kids you’re going to have to get alarm clocks! Hurry up and eat and get ready for school!"
As the Trio ate Claire cleaned the living room with the vacuum cleaner. 
Looking at the clock Claire yelled "Kids get ready and wait at the bus stop!"
The Trio left the apartment and went outside of the building. The streets were busy with morning time activity. It took a while to get to the school bus stop at the end of their street. They stood waiting till a minivan came up to them by the curb where they were waiting with a school bus sign on it. Michael recognized the driver to be Mrs. Cynthia Watts, Tina’s driver to school. 
She opened the car door of her green minivan and spoke "Tina! Thanks for waiting. Get in I'll drive you to school. Boys you two will have to take the bus to high school."
When Tina got in and closed the door Mrs. Watts drove off. 
Sam spoke "Lucky! She gets to go to school with Mrs. Watts instead of a wicky old school bus. Humph!" 
 Michael spoke "Chill out Sam. She'll be going to high school next year so Tina will be taking the wicky bus."
The boys didn't have to wait long for the school bus to the high school pulled up. It was a yellow dirty color like it hadn't been cleaned. It rattled and shook as it slowed to stop. The bus driver a lady of forties' sat impatiently as Michael and Sam got on.
A boy yelled "Hurry up Ryans! I wanna ged oud of dis bus!"  
Michael laughed recognizing the voice belonging to foreign exchanged student Vladimir Kystov. Still laughing Michael sat down with Sam. The bus roared and went into the busy streets to school. 

At the high school, both boys, were practically in the same classes except gym and history. In the last class, history, Michael sat bored in the second row of the third seat. The lecture his history teacher Mr. Duke was talking about summer school was putting him to sleep. Michael almost daydreamed when Mr. Duke mentioned that they could ask him any questions which got him wide eyed and awake. Michael bravely raised his hand. 
Mr. Duke called on him “Yes Michael?”
Michael asked “What do you know of skin walkers?”
Mr. Duke sputtered and stammered out “Their Native American Legend that people could change their skin as an animal or something like that.” 
Then suddenly the bell rang loudly ending school over for the summer vacation. Michael gathered his stuff. Kids joyously ran out of their classes to their lockers. It was chaos of teenagers at their lockers frantically trying to clean it out in a hurry with mobs of teenagers running out of the school, to start their vacations. Michael ran through the crowd looking for Sam. He spotted the familiar blonde head in the crowd. Edging over to him Michael tapped him on the shoulder. 
Sam turned around and said "Where have you been Mike?"
Michael glared and dragged him to their bus. 
Michael complained "I really can't wait to get a motorbike it's ridiculous to ride home by bus."
Sam spoke "So? Quit complaining!" 

At the middle school Tina sat in the back of the room of Mrs. Pollack's resource class her last class of the school year. Some kids were talking about what they were going to do during the summer time. Penny Worthington, a blond haired girl was blabbering to anyone about spending the summer in Spain. Tina was half listening to Penny's chatter. She was thinking of having to spend the summer in that hot smoggy city suburbs in an apartment. Soon she would have to get a job working at Mr. Lu's big grocery store. She would be the third person of the Trio to get a job at the grocery store.  
She was so busy thinking when Penny spoke "Tina! Tina! Yoo hoo!"
Penny waved a hand in front of Tina's face. 
Startled Tina asked Penny "What?"
Penny giggled and said " Lucky you! Your Mom has come to take you home!"
Tina smiled and hugged her good bye then stood up and gathered her books. She left with her blue skirt swishing. Outside the school Claire sat in the family's red car waiting for her daughter to come. Claire was bursting with news but it had to wait. At last Tina came wearing a short mid length red and white shirt with a blue skirt and tennis shoes came hurrying with her brown hair swinging. She opened the car door and got in closing the car door behind her and put her seat belt on. 
When she was settled she spoke "Hey Mom thanks for picking me up early."
Claire laughed and said "I got some great and bad news. So I wanted to share it when all three are together." 
Tina nodded and opened one of her books and started reading. Claire started the car and drove on to the streets of the city suburbs to their home.

It took thirty minutes to drive through the busy streets of the traffic to get home to the apartment building. On the front steps waiting were Sam and Michael. Nanook slept in the sun on the stairwell. Hocus was seen on the window of the Ryan apartment looking out. Claire drove up and parked the car then she and Tina got out. 
Michael spoke "Mom what's new?" 
Sam spoke “Yo! What's going on? "
Claire answered them "The news I have are in these envelopes."
She held them up. She handed one to Sam who tore it open in a hurry. He skimmed it for a few minutes before crumpling it up and threw it down. 
Michael asked " Sam what's wrong?" 
Sam answered "I got my fucking wish. It's my adoptive parents; they died in a plane crash coming home." 
He paused and then he was about to say something before running inside. 
Michael tried to follow but Claire put a hand on his arm and said "I think Sam needs some time alone." 
Tina asked "Mom what's the other news?"  
Claire handed the other envelope to Tina. She pulled out the letter and read it with Michael looking over her shoulder.
Then the two yelled "All right!" 
While giving each other high fives, as Michael couldn't help doing some dancing, on the side walk. 
Claire spoke "We better find Sam and share it with him" as they darted in side.

Chapter seven

It was late in the afternoon when Michael after a while of searching found Sam with help from the dog Nanook sitting in the corner in the attic. Sam looked up to see Michael walk over to him. He sat down on the bare floor next to where Sam was sitting. 
Michael spoke "I know how you feel. We lost our Father in a plane crash after he divorced our Mother."
He paused and sighed then he said "How are you doing?"
Sam spoke not looking at Michael "Fine what the fuck do you want?" 
Michael shrugged and spoke "To tell you the other news."
Sam looked at him and said "I suppose it was fucking good news?
Michael answered him "Yep. It's from our Grandfather, Mom's Father George Patricoly. He invited all of us including you to stay at his home in Port Monaco, Connecticut."
He pause waiting for Sam to say something then he spoke "Do ya wanna come along?"
Sam spoke "Can Nanook and Hocus come?” 
Michael smiled and punched him playfully in the arm "Yep the animals are coming. So are you coming down to eat dinner?" 
Smiling Sam got up with Michael behind him they went downstairs to the Ryan apartment. Inside was a going away party host by Mrs. Burke and several of the residents were there partying.

The following days following the party were hectic of Claire turning the apartment upside down to find useful stuff to pack. The furniture was staying for they were extras, belonged to Mrs. Burke. Sam packed most of his things, clothes, comic books, and the cat's bowls and toys. He managed to fit this in one big suitcase. Michael packed two suitcases and Tina used one suitcase for her stuff and the other suitcase for Nanook's dishes and dog chows and treats. Claire packed a total of three suitcases which made eight suitcases. It was Tina who discovered that Claire's car was too small and didn't have enough room for all of the suitcases and the trio including the animals. Mrs. Burke saved the day by lending her big white station wagon and got Claire's car in return. Then they finished packing and some last minute preparations loaded up the station wagon. Then after lunching with Mrs. Burke they bid good bye and left on their way to Port Monaco. 
But before they left Sam made a sign that read "From Hell to Port Monaco or bust". 
On the back of the car a fact unknown to Claire who found out later on the trip. 

Chapter eight

It took nearly hours to get to Port Monaco due to Nanook complaining of bathroom along with similar complaints from the Trio including stopping to let Hocus out of the car due to him appearing to try to go to the bathroom which the cat didn't complain to expelling once out of the car and watched heavily by Sam his owner. During the ride Nanook tried to chase Hocus the cat. They were running around the car and wouldn't stay put. It was so amusing to Sam and Tina but annoying to Claire. Michael wasn't interested for he was looking out the window. Claire stopped the car at a rest stop and she strapped Nanook tight in the back with a seat belt. The cat she put in his carrier and closed it enough for him to stick his nose out. Sam thought Hocus looked funny. Satisfied Claire got in the driver's seat and started the car on the road again ignoring people's requests for bathroom due to feeling fed up with stopping for that. Michael spent the trip staring out the window after getting the message that his Mother wasn't going to stop for another bathroom trip which his sister Tina wound up reading a book in response to their mother's ignoring their bathroom requests. Sam sat in the front bored with the cat in his carrier. 
When they were a few miles before the border to Port Monaco, Tina spoke "Look there's the beach and it's the lake!"
Sam peered behind him to noticed Michael watching a girl in a bikini rollerblading on the board walk. 
Sam spoke "Mrs. Ryan, Michael interested in that girl in a bikini rollerblading" 
Claire looked and spoke "Michael quit gawking at her!" 
Michael turned away from the window and glared at Sam. 
"Spoil sport" he mouthed. 
Sam laughed then resumed looking away.

A billboard of a house with trees, on the entrance to the tunnel wall said "Welcome to Port Monaco!"
Then the car went into a tunnel before coming out. The scenery was houses sitting in rows but some of them looked worn and old. 
A big sign with a picture of the lake and a port said "Port Monaco" 
As they passed Michael looked behind to see written in graffiti were words "Punk rock and roll town of the world!" 
Stores and restaurants sat in groups like an outdoor mall. On the beach was a big amusement park with all kinds of rides and roller coasters including venders and booths selling stuff. One of the booths caught Michael's interest. The booth was selling a motorbike at three hundred and sixty dollars. The motorbike was a little old with red on it. It brought Michael memories of riding a friends’ motorbike at the school parking lot while learning to get his license. 
Michael spoke "Mom can you stop the car? It's been a long time and I need to stretch." 
Claire parked the car and looked at Michael. 
She spoke "You got your eye on that motorbike? Well its fine with me, go buy it."
Michael darted out the car. He pulled out the five hundred dollars he had been saving from his pocket and thumbed out three hundred and sixty to the vender who wordlessly took the money and didn't seem to care that he was a teenager which he took the motorbike and started riding it around along with finding a gas station to fill up the tank fully of gas due to its sputtering noises was indicating it low of gas.
Claire spoke soon after Michael darted out "Sam, Tina would you two get the pets out? They might have to go. So go buy some thing. Stretch your legs." 
She got out from the car and went into the town hall building. Sam came out carrying Hocus and Tina had Nanook on a leash. Tina spotted a booth selling clothes and went to it. Sam stood by the car and looked around. He spotted a comic book booth and was walking to it. A girl with long blonde hair that was almost white came and bumped into Sam. 
She spoke angrily "Will you watch where you’re going you fucking punk!" 
She walked off in a huff and disappeared in the crowd. Sam stuck his middle finger at her form and went into the comic book booth.

Chapter nine

An hour later Michael, after buying the motorbike practiced driving it till he could control it. He stood leaning on the Ryan station wagon with the motorbike next to him. Sam came running up reading a thick comic book in one hand and the cat in the other hand. Then Tina came with two bags full in hand. Nanook was behind Tina on her leash. Tina put her bags down and weeded through it and pulled out black leather like jacket. 
Tina spoke "Here Michael for you to wear on your motorbike to look cool." 
She handed it to Michael who took it and put it on. The jacket fit him perfectly. 
"Thanks" He told his sister.
Claire came out from a booth with a shiny gray helmet in hand and a bag and came up to the Trio waving the helmet in Michael's face. 
She spoke "Michael the helmet is for reckless driving and is part of the Port Monaco ordinance." 
She put the helmet on Michael’s head who grumbled the word fuck loudly she ignored. She pulled out a pair of white high top sneakers and waved them in front of Sam.
Sam looked up and asked "Do I have to wear them? The hiking boots were from my real Father because they used to be his."
Claire spoke "Sam, wear which ever you want but I would like it if you wore them. I'm sick of hearing that thump noise coming from your boots." 
Sighing Sam took them and put them in the car. Tina put her bags in the car and got in as Michael sat on his bike waiting Claire pulled out a package and handed it to Tina. Claire then got in the drivers' seat as Sam sat next to Tina. Tina opened the package and was delighted to see several books on her favorite animal horses.
She spoke "Thanks Mom now I can do horse riding and read too.”
Claire smiled and started the car. She waved her arm out the window as a signal to start. Then she drove the car through the streets with Michael on his motorbike following behind.

As the car went through the busy streets there were people dressed in styles of leather, dyed hair, and paint on faces, cutoffs and tie dye clothes. 
Sam asked " Mrs. Ryan, What fad it that?" 
Claire answered "Sam, you may call me Claire and Port Monaco is mostly a punk rock and roll town including ex‑hippies. But don't worry it's my kind of town." 
Laughing she turned the car down the lane of trees and then she droved the car on the dirt driveway and stopped the car in one of the parking spaces. 
Claire got out and said "Well this is it. What do you think?"
Michael followed Claire by motorbike and parked it next to the Ryan car. 
Michael spoke uncaring if his Mother heard him "Great we’re living in an old fucking wreck.”
He meant the house’s forlorn shape and was apparently neglected. It was violet color and three stories high. The front door of the house opened and an old white haired man came out with a cane onto the porch. He had on a faded long sleeve shirt and faded denims. On his feet were moccasins decorated with beads. When Claire saw him she ran into his arms and the two hugged for he was her Father George Patricoly. Grandfather Patricoly came to the car with an arm around his daughter. His other hand was holding onto a cane. 
He spoke "Claire is you going to introduce your kids and the pets?" 
Michael came walking around the car. He had the helmet under his arm and he was still wearing the jacket. 
Claire spoke "This is my eldest son, Michael Octaves Ryan. The dog is a female named Nanook." 
When Sam opened the car door and Nanook jumped out with Tina. Sam came out with Hocus in hand. 
Grandfather Patricoly noticed Sam asked "Hey there! Who is this?" 
Claire answered "This is Samuel Benson. His parents trusted him in our care. So I'm keeping him." 
Grandfather Patricoly spoke "You can call me George, or Grandfather, whose cat is that?"
Claire spoke "When we got Sam, we got Hocus."
Grandfather noticed Tina, he spoke " Claire is that your daughter too?"
Claire spoke "Yes this is Natina Maria Ryan. She prefers to be called Tina." 
Grandfather spoke "Come on kids! What are we standing around for? Let's get your stuff inside!" 

Unpacking the car took awhile with so many stuff crammed in the car and on top. Grandfather despite Claire’s objections helped unload the car. When he and Claire were inside unpacking kitchen stuff the Trio was outside picking up their suitcases. 
Sam spoke "Natina is that your full name?" 
Tina glared and said " Yes and I resent being called by that fucking name so don't ever say it to me in my face or refer it to me period." 
Sam glared back and grabbed his suitcase and went into the large living room towards the stairs as he was walking by the double swinging doors of the kitchen when he heard voices. They were Grandfather and Claire. 
Grandfather was saying "Claire I wrote to you and invited you here for I was getting worried. That something might happen to either one of you." 
Claire spoke "What are you worried about? I've been living in Wolfville city suburbs for years and nothing happened to any of us." 
Grandfather spoke "There's been sightings of wolves in Wolfville."
Claire spoke "I'm shocked for I was never told of this." 
Grandfather spoke "There has been wolves’ murders and attacks in the Wolfville city suburbs so I had to get you to safety." 

Sam who had been busy eavesdropping with Michael and Tina felt himself being pushed in. The door swung open as the Trio fell hitting the wooden floor. Grandfather and Claire who were sitting at the table looked at the commotion.
Grandfather spoke "Jojo! Did you push them?"
Michael turned and gasped at Jojo. She appeared to be about his age, seventeen. She had long pale blonde hair to her waist with side bangs and blue eyes. She straightened her blue overalls that had dirt on them. Under her overalls was a white T-shirt top.
She spoke angrily "There! They must be the punks that have been prowling on your land."
Claire glared and said coolly "Excuse Me! But these three" pointing at them "Are my children"
Jojo held her hands up which had garden gloves on spoke "Well sorry I had no idea that they were George's grandchildren. But I don't think the blonde is one of yours. For I recall Mrs. Ryan had two children."
Sam spoke "I was taken under the care of Mrs. Ryan after my parents died in a plane crash."
Jojo spoke coolly "So it was you that rudely bumped into me at the fair."
Sam glared and said "Fuck off!" 
Jojo rebelled "Fuck you yourself!" 
Grandfather spoke "Jojo! Sam! Knock it off! Jojo you may take the rest of the day off." 
She they saw walked out of the kitchen slamming the double swing doors that it still swung. 
Tina asked "Who is that snob?”
Grandfather replied "She's Jojo Ioniel the daughter of the Ioniels family our nearest neighbors."
He paused and said "What are we waiting for get back to unpacking!" 

Chapter ten

Jojo left the house by the back door. She quickened her pace till she was almost running through the forest. She ran down a big hill till she reached the bottom. She looked around to see if she was being followed. Then she waited as a hooded figure in black walked from around a tree. 
The figure spoke muffled "Do you have any news to report Jojo?"
Jojo spoke "I saw candidate Michael Octaves Ryan there with his family."
The figure said "Good."
Jojo added "One more thing, there's an interference a dog named Nanook, a cat named Hocus and Sam Benson who Mrs. Ryan took under her care. I'm not sure if Tina Ryan, Michael's sister can interfere."
The figure spoke "Very well but invite Michael to visit your family. He will be another addition to the clan." 
The figure disappeared in the forest as Jojo left and hurried to the house. 

In the house Grandfather gave the trio to their rooms. Because of his health Grandfather slept in one of the extra bedrooms on the first floor. For the trio he let them pick whatever rooms they wanted upstairs on the second floor. He gave Claire the room next to his. She was worried about him for Grandfather looked frail enough to hurt himself seriously. Upstairs the trio was exploring the rooms. The trio saw that there was a bathroom at the end of the hallway and there were three rooms in a row on the left and three in a row on the right. The wall paper was old and yellow of pink small flowers on it. The doors were white with numbers in gold plate on them. 
Tina spoke "I'm going to take a look on the left." 
She opened door number three and looked in. The room was furnished with brown furniture and white curtains and a Native American styled oval rug, and attached to Number one was a room like Number three was another bathroom. Sam left his stuff in room number three. The trio inspected numbers four on the right. It was the same as room’s number one and three. Number five was an empty room that had miles of boxes in it. Number six was locked. Michael left his stuff in room number one. Tina did the same by picking room number four. The trio heard Grandfather call them down.

In the kitchen Jojo prepared lemonade in cups as refreshment. She set six cups and put them on a tray and carried them to the TV room which was where the stairway was to upstairs. The TV room was the biggest room in the house. It was furnished with brown panels and a stone fireplace. The furniture was old with covers of Native American designs on them. Jojo carried the tray on to the coffee table where she set it down. The Ryans were sitting near the fire place. They were talking about how things were going in the city suburbs and were still at it when Jojo came from the kitchen.
She spoke "Excuse me. I brought lemonade courtesy of the Ioniel fruit orchard farm."
She stood waiting. 
Grandfather spoke "Thank you Jojo."
He picked a cup of lemonade and drank. Claire did the same and so did Tina. 
Michael who was staring at her picked his cup and spoke "I suppose judging from your accent that you’re Romanian?" 
Jojo spoke "Yes my family is from Romania and nobody in our family is Native American." 
Michael stared questioningly. She pointed to Tina's book which the title indicating Native Americans was seen.
Grandfather spoke "Jojo would you mind getting Sam to get down here and try this lemonade?"
Jojo nodded and went upstairs. The family resumed talking but Michael went upstairs.
Tina asked "Grandfather, How did you hire Jojo?" 
Grandfather put down his cup and thought for a minute. 
He spoke "The Ioniels have been my neighbors for a long time since I first brought this house. When I injured myself the doctor told me to use a cane for walking and do limited activities which mean caring for the horses, fixing the fence and keeping this place neat. So the Ioniels sent Jojo help me for the rest of the summer till school."
Tina asked " Hey where's Sam?" 

Sam was exploring his room with the cat Hocus on his bed. It had an adjoining bathroom which connected his room and Michael's. First he explored the closet in his room, it was solid wall and its back was to the hallway. Disappointed he was expecting a secret door to a passage. He went out of his room and saw Michael on the stairs with Jojo. They were both talking. Sam picked up Hocus and inspected room number five where he explored every inch of it. Curiously he was looking in the boxes when he heard Hocus on the window still meow. Sam went to the window and saw a blonde haired figure in ripped attire walking away from the house. Sam figured he would have to ask about it later. Sam went out in the hallway. Jojo and Michael were still talking. He eavesdropped on them. They were saying:
Michael: “What do you know of skin walkers?”
Jojo: “That their Native American legend around here in Port Monaco.”.
Michael: “Oh. What do you know who owned the house before Grandpa?”
Jojo: “From what I know some family who died off and a last living relative sold it.” 

Sam came walking to the library room which was a loft with a computer and bookshelves on the sides. He stood watching Jojo and Michael talk. Jojo turned and glared at Sam. 
She spoke “Eavesdropping? I could hear you from the hallway.” 
Michael glared and spoke “Sam, you’re wanted downstairs.”
Sam sighed and walked down the stairs to the TV room. Claire and her Father sat with Tina talking. They stopped talking when Sam entered the room with Hocus the cat following. Nanook abruptly got up and barked and proceeded to chase Hocus around the room. Tina sighed and got up to grab Nanook by the collar and then hauled the dog outside. Sam sat and noticed Grandfather and Claire exchange looks. 
Sam asked “Well, what did I miss?” 
Grandfather cleared his throat and spoke “It’s about time for me to go to bed. It’s getting late.”
He gave Claire an affectionate pat on her head and got up limping with his cane to one of the bedrooms on the first floor of the house. Sam gave Claire a questioning look. 
Claire sighed and spoke “This house used to belong to the Morgan family for generations before several tragedies led to them selling it before you and the kids were born. From time to time I would see wolves in the forest of Port Monaco. There’s an old town legend about the Morgan family. It’s said that they were skin walkers’ people who could change their forms, mostly wolves. They were twin brothers, Luke and Mark and an older sister named Brittany Morgan. According to my father, Mark died here out there. This happened in the year 1977.” 
She gestured to the windows overlooking the back yard lawn towards the pool house. 
Then she continued “After Mark’s death Luke and his wife Ariana Nicholas and their daughter Cheyenne, Mark’s son, Mark Junior and another daughter named Claire disappeared never to be seen again. Local legend is that two wolves and three cubs were seen hanging around the house before Brittany Morgan sold the house and its grounds.”
Claire sighed. 
Sam asked “What happened next?”
Claire answered “Brittany Morgan later became a recluse and hasn’t been seen in town lately but she mostly hung around the house a few times when I was there, but I haven’t seen her since. No one in town knows where’s she is. They still have trouble finding her cabin till the present day it’s still a mystery where it is.”
The clock chimed ten times. 
Claire got up and spoke “I believe it’s your bedtime. Go.” 
Sam watched her go out the back door and stare at the sky. He went to the window as Tina came in. 
She grumbled “Fucking cat always torturing Nanook.” 
Noticing Sam staring out the window she spoke “What are you doing?” 
Sam looked at her and answered “Nothing”. 
He went up the stairs with a confused Tina following him. 

Outside Claire shivered in the cold. She could see a several grave stones lying in the yard under some forlorn trees. 
She went over to them and read the words "In loving memory: Christian Morgan and Cheyenne Wolf-Morgan." 
At that moment a wolf howled joined by several voices of the wolves howling. Claire shivered. Sighing she turned and went inside the house. 

Chapter eleven

Inside sleep didn’t come easily for Sam. He wondered about the story he was told. Hocus who was in his room meowed and he got up and looked out the window. A white wolf was sitting there staring at the window. Sam frowned and opened the window. The wolf ran away towards the forest. Sam watched it leave. He had a strange feeling like he knew that wolf wanted to tell him something. Sighing he went back to bed. He didn’t see Michael peering out the bathroom door adjoining their rooms watching him. Michael slowly closed the door and went to his room. He stood staring out the window in his room. Michael frowned about what Jojo told him about the wolves. She told him that they were frequent around the forests of the town of Port Monaco. She also told him that the locals treated the wolves like they were to be feared because of what happened to the Morgan family. Michael sighed and went back to bed. 

Morning came with her ray of sunshine on the forest near the forlorn house. Jojo stood in the corral brushing a horse. It was a brown chestnut mare who snickered softly and shook its head. 
Jojo was startled when she heard Michael say “Nice horse.” 
She looked at him leaning on the fence watching her. 
Jojo spoke “Out with it. What’s your purpose of being here this early?”
Michael replied “Me? I’m just checking out the grounds and seeing every thing. I haven’t been here before.” 
Jojo kept brushing the horse and said “Keep looking. There’s a barn down that way with other horses. Feel free to go horse back riding.” 
Michael spoke “I don’t know how to ride a horse.” 
As he admired Jojo wearing jeans that showed her curves and the t-shirt that hugged to her frame. He felt a feeling of a tug in him and stood leaning against the fence watching her. Jojo kept brushing the mare she named “Honeycomb”. Honeycomb snickered and stood. 
Soon Michael’s staring got the best of her and she protested “Enough! Michael, take yourself to the barn and stop staring at me. You’re upsetting the horse.”
Michael groaned and walked away towards the barn. He had to walk through the forest on a dirt driveway towards the red barn. As he neared it, a young man appearing to be about his age, wearing punk attire of ripped blue jeans with a blue ripped t-shirt at the sleeves came from around the tree. His hair was a long perm yellow color and a bit spiked at the top of his head. He stood in front of Michael. Michael froze staring at him. The punk’s eyes were a cold brown color bore into Michael’s hazel eyes. 
Michael asked “My name’s Michael. You are?” 
The punk answered “Daniel. Stay away from her. She’s mine, not yours.” 
Confused Michael asked “Who?” 
Instead of answering Daniel turned away and walked away. Michael jogged chasing after him. Daniel ran through some bushes and around trees losing Michael. Michael reached a tree and saw a black wolf there sitting there. He froze staring at the wolf in the eyes. The wolf sat then turned around and ran away. Michael frowned then walked further into the forest. He looked around feeling a little lost. He heard a sound of a horse neighing and followed the sound till he reached the dirt driveway where Jojo was leading the horse towards the barn. He followed with a confused look on his face. 
Jojo annoyingly told him “Are you going to follow me all day?”
Michael replied “No. I saw a guy who told me his name was Daniel. He told me to stay away from her. Who’s he?”
At the sound of the name Daniel, Jojo sniffed and frowned as she led Honeycomb down the path towards the barn. 
She replied to Michael’s question “He’s my boyfriend Daniel.” 
While noticing a flicker of jealously in Michael’s face then continued speaking “So stop following me.” 
Michael stood staring at her figure as she walked towards the barn. 
He yelled “Hey! Is your name Jojo, Romanian?” 
Jojo yelled back “It’s a nickname for Georgina!”
Then she kept walking towards the barn. Michael stood stewing and stormed back towards the house. 

Jojo kept walking towards the barn. She neared a tree and Daniel stepped out glaring at her. 
He spoke “I don’t appreciate that Human, being near you.” 
Jojo answered “He’s one of us and doesn’t know it yet but if time is right he’ll know soon enough.” 
Daniel glared again spoke “I hope your right.”
Then he kissed Jojo on the lips and strode into the forest. Jojo sighed and kept walking towards the barn. 

At the barn Tina stood playing with Nanook. She threw a thick blue ball and Nanook ran and chased it. Then Nanook brought it back to Tina who threw it again. She saw Jojo came in with Honeycomb the horse. Tina squealed of delight and forgetting Nanook and her ball walked towards the horse and gave the horse back a rub. 
Jojo smiled and spoke “Like her? Her name is Honeycomb and she’s one of the horses in the coral.” 
Tina sighed of delight and gave Honeycomb a hug and said “Ah heaven. I love horses because my favorite. I love to learn lots about them.” 
She looked at Jojo and asked “When can I ride her?” 
Jojo thought for a minute and spoke “Soon, she’s a little skitterish towards people riding her.” 
Tina followed Jojo leading Honeycomb towards the barn. She heard Nanook whining and looked at the dog. The ball was in her mouth and Nanook wagged her tail respectively. Tina took the ball and threw it into the forest with Nanook chasing after it. Tina followed Jojo into the barn. Jojo led Honeycomb towards a stall and gave her some hay to munch on. Tina stood watching her gave Honeycomb some carrots to eat when she heard growling. She looked towards her left to see a black wolf standing at the entrance to the barn growling at her. 
Jojo hearing the growling and went to stand next to Tina and whispered “Don’t move or make a sound.”
The wolf growled then Nanook came with her ball and the wolf ran away. Nanook dropped her ball and cocked her head as if saying a question. 
Tina asked “What? Was that a skin walker?”
Jojo stiffened but answered “I don’t know. Come on lets go back to the house. It’s not safe here.” 
Tina sighed and followed Jojo to the house. Nanook followed holding her ball in her mouth. 

Chapter twelve

At the house Michael sat in the living room staring at the fire place. His Grandfather George sat in an armchair asleep. Michael stormed outside towards the pool house. He noticed his Mother standing near something like a statue of a gray wolf. The wolf moved and stared at him and then ran away. Claire looked up to see Michael looking at them. She waved him over. 
He ran over and asked “What’s with the wolf?” 
Claire answered “I have no idea except I thought it was a statue at first but it moved and ran away. Take a look.” 
She gestured to the ground. Michael saw a headstone with the names Christian Morgan and Cheyenne Wolf-Morgan. Michael frowned staring at the headstone. On the ground in front of the head stone were two headstones with the two names and dates of their births and deaths. Michael noticed the date and saw it was before he was born. Tina came bounding out the door with a sleepy Sam. She skipped towards her brother and mother and noticed their sad expressions. Michael pointed and she saw where he pointed. On the ground were a large headstone and two small ones. Tina read the names and dates. Sam yawned and stared at the headstones. 
He grumbled out “Tina woke me up blathering about horses and you show me some headstones?” 
Michael told him “Take a look and read the names.” 
Sam read the names and spoke out loud “Christian Morgan and Cheyenne Wolf-Morgan. Oh the people of the local legend”
Claire said “No the parents of Brittany, and the twins Luke and Mark Morgan, the local legend.” 
Sam rubbed his eyes and yawned again. Nanook whined wagging her tail staring at the house. Michael noticed Jojo peering out the kitchen window as she busied herself in the kitchen helping her mother Raya Ioniel make lunch for George and family. 
Claire spoke “When my father brought the house the kitchen was on the small size and he did some renovations, including adding a barn for horses.” 
Michael asked “What about the pool house?”
Claire sighed and answered “The original pool house was burned down. The fire department suspect arson but the arsonist was never found. Your Grandfather built a new one in its spot.” 
Then they heard a bell ringing and looked towards the house. Out the porch was Jojo ringing a bell by the back door to the sun room. 
She yelled out “Lunch time! Come and get it!” 

Inside the gang met Raya Ioniel, Jojo’s Mother, a woman with white hair wearing a flowered cotton dress and sandals with a smiling face who stood over the stove cooking. Michael stared at the kitchen wondering why it was renovated. He slid himself onto the bench with Sam and Tina in the dining room. Claire sat at the head of the table with George opposite her at the other side of the table. Raya handed them steaming bowls of food and sat next to Claire with Jojo sitting besides her on the bench. Conversation was centered on the food which was Italian like cooked food dishes. Michael tasted different foods and found them good. Sam ate most of what was put on his plate. Tina being a finicky eater ate a little bit of food. 
Sam sighed and spoke “Good food Mrs. Ioniel.” 
Raya spoke “Thank you but please call me, Raya.”
Michael noticed Raya staring at him with pity. It made him uncomfortable that he shifted on the bench. 
Sam noticed it and spoke “Raya why do you look Michael with pity?”
Raya was startled at the question and said “Jojo told me how Michael was interested in her but she has a boyfriend.” 
Michael rudely spoke “Some boyfriend. He looks like a punk rocker with his ripped clothes.” 
Raya abruptly spoke in Romanian to Jojo “Georgina, I told you to tell Daniel to stop dressing like some rock and roll star.”
Jojo replied in Romanian “I did, but he won’t listen to me, told me it was his style and way to dress like that.” 
Tina curiously asked “What language are you two speaking in?”
Michael answered for Jojo “I think it’s Romanian by the accents like the customers at Mr. Lu’s store. Remember?”
Tina frowned and said “Oh I remember accents and Romanian language.” 
Sam at the moment was busy feeding Nanook some scraps when Claire said “Sam, stop feeding the dog scraps. I plan to go to town soon to check and make sure our mail reached this address.” 
Grandfather spoke “Why don’t you call the post office and have them deliver it here? That’s what I do lately if it wasn’t due to this bum leg. Humph.” 
Claire sighed and said “Father, I have to visit the town hall about adopting Sam as his legal guardian until he turns twenty one.”
Sam groaned as Michael asked “What about his birth parents and relatives of the Bensons?” 
Sam answered “There are no relatives of my adopted parents. My mother told me that my father’s name is Wilson. A last name or first name I don’t know. I also don’t know if he’s alive or dead.” 
At the name Wilson, Claire looked at Grandfather who was frowning with a glare at Sam. 
Claire gathered her plate and her Father’s and said “I’m going to town; anyone is welcome to come along.” 
She went to the kitchen and sighed thinking “Coyote Wilson fathered a son? I might want to check it out.” 
Raya came in the kitchen and spoke Romanian to Claire who understood her “Claire. Sam reminds me of Coyote Wilson. He’s the splitting image of him with his blond hair despite his eyes. I wonder how Sam got adopted in the first place.”
Claire spoke in Romanian “I plan to find out at the town hall today once I get there.”

In the dining room Grandfather sighed. 
Jojo spoke “Here George I’ll help you to your seat by the fire.” 
She got up and assisted him towards the huge living room. Michael followed them and watched Jojo assist his Grandfather settle in his favorite chair as Jojo flicked on the TV, which showed racing cars Grandfather’s favorite sport. Michael watched his Grandfather sit in the armchair with an amused expression on his face watching the car race on TV. Michael sighed and walked through the huge living room towards the small sun room and outside the back door. A car came up the drive with a sound of loud music. Sam went to investigate. He saw Jojo leave by the front door and he followed her out. Outside was a slick black Corvette and sitting in it was a guy with perm long yellow hair. 
Jojo walked up to him and gave him a kiss on the mouth which made Sam say “Bad hair day.” 
He watched as she talked to the guy and then the guy drove off. Jojo turned around to catch the disgust on Sam’s face. 
She put her hands on her hips and glared at Sam while saying “He’s not disgusting and he’s my boyfriend Daniel.” 
Sam answered her with sarcasm “Oh really? What do you see in a guy with a bad hair day?”
Laughing he ran inside the house. Jojo rolled her eyes and sighed then she followed Sam inside the house. 

Chapter thirteen

Claire left the house and got in her car. She couldn’t shake the uneasy feeling of being watched. As she drove down the dirt road towards the street she looked in her rearview mirror to see a wolf sitting in the road watching her. The wolf was gray with black markings on it. Claire sighed and kept driving. Then she looked in the review mirror again and gasped stopping the car on the brake. In the review mirror was a man with tan skin, with a Mohawk styled hair, a blue crew neck top, jeans and black shoes on. He had a sneer on his face. Claire abruptly turned around and looked. In place was a wolf that howled and ran away. Claire frowned shaken that she sat in her car for awhile. She didn’t notice her Father watching hidden from the trees with a glare on his face. Then he hobbled towards the house. A wolf bounded in his path and sat staring at him. 
Grandfather spoke “I know you and your intentions. Believe me I won’t go down without a fight.” 
The wolf growled with menace and stalked towards Grandfather. Then the front door opened and Sam came out on to the porch yelling with Nanook running out barking. The wolf turned its head and seeing Sam and Nanook it ran into the forest with Nanook in a chase. Grandfather sighed of relief. 
Sam angrily spoke “What the fuck's with that wolf and what’s going on?”
Grandfather answered “Nothing, just a wolf wanting me for its lunch.”
He hobbled towards the house with Sam glaring at him. 
In Sam’s mind he thought “Something’s fucking funny going on here and I’m going to find out what’s going on.”

Claire regained her composure and drove to the town hall. She parked the car and noticed some people glaring at her. She was used to it from living in the former Morgan house. The town people treated her Father and her with suspicion of accusing them of being skin walkers as it appeared to be by the glares aimed at her and her Father whenever in town. She ignored them glaring and entered the town hall which was a brick building with a metal door a former army fort building. 
Entering the building she reached some steps and walked up to a hallway to a door marked “Town records.” 
Inside was small room with a receptionist. 
The receptionist a woman with frizzy blonde hair and a brown suit sat at a desk with a lap top, with a name tag “Anita” spoke “May I help you?” 
It was obvious to Claire that she was new in town judging from her innocent expression on her face. Claire was at the end of her patience. 
Claire spoke a little annoyed “I would like to see the records on a family by the name Morgan who lived in this town.” 
Anita said frowning “I’m sorry but the records to the Morgan Family are sealed on the orders of Timothy Jones their lawyer of their estate. You’ll have to wait till Mr. Timothy Jones returns to town from a family trip, location unknown.” 
Claire glared and asked “What about the records for Coyote Wilson?” 
Anita again spoke “I’m sorry but the records to Coyote Wilson and family are sealed on the orders of Timothy Jones their lawyer who is on a family vacation. “
Seeing she was getting nowhere Claire again asked “What about the records on an Alex and Taylor Benson?” 
Anita frowned again and turned to her laptop computer and typed some keys. 
Words appeared on her screen as she spoke “It appears the Bensons lived here for two years before moving to Houston, Texas.”
Claire asked “Did they have any children?”
The receptionist typed some keys and spoke again “Appears they adopted a son from oh its personal can’t tell you-“
She was interrupted as Claire grabbed her laptop and read the name “Coyote Wilson” under “Biological Father.” 
Anita protested “That’s personal property! Its also personal information! Lady, give me back my laptop!” 
Claire set it down on Anita’s desk and spoke “Thanks for the information.”
Then she turned on her heel and left the room slamming the door. 
Anita sighed and grabbed her cell phone and dialed a number. 
A male electronic voice in it spoke “Hello? Anita, I told you not to call me on this number.”
Anita spoke “I’m sorry Silent Walker, but some woman came in asking about the Morgan family and Coyote Wilson. I did what you told me to but she asked about the Bensons' and I gave her the information on what you told me to but she was really nosy, grabbed my laptop and saw the information about Sam Benson.”
She paused and waited listening for a sound, nothing. 
She spoke “Hello?” 
Then the voice on the line spoke “Describe the woman.” 
Anita gave a description of Claire. 
She heard the voice speak “Ah Claire Patricoly, the daughter.” 
Anita asked “What am I supposed to do?” 
The voice answered “Download the files and personally sent them to a meeting spot yourself. And don’t forget to delete them.” 
Anita spoke “Okay.” 
As the line went dead Anita typed some keys and downloaded the information onto a small disk. Once the information was downloaded Anita typed the word “Delete”. 
Then she put the disk in her pocket and gathered her purse. She walked towards the door and put an “Out for lunch” sign on the door then locked it. She saw Claire come out of another office stewing. Anita flattened herself against the wall and waited as Claire stormed pass her and out of the town hall. Anita followed her out and watched as Claire entered a white station wagon with the license plate “Wolf-One” on it. Anita watched as Claire drove off. Sighing Anita got in a red sedan and drove away. She drove towards the town park with a forest bordering it. Anita was careful to look behind her to make sure she wasn’t being followed as she entered the forest. She tied the disk in a string purse held in her mouth and ran in the forest. Her skin became fur as her legs became paws. She got shorter and shorter as her face narrowed with ears poking out of the top of her head. She ran in the wolf form running into the forest. Anita’s wolf form was grey with black splotches on her fur. She ran to a stream and took a drink from it and ran through it following the stream. Anita reached a small waterfall and walked towards the bank. She howled and heard an answering howl of a Human voice. She sat in the wolf form as a hand took the disk off Anita. The hand gave Anita a steak and a pat on the head. Anita moaned of pleasure and chewed the steak with happiness. She didn’t notice the hand pulled out a knife from the waist of a scabbard and stabbed her in the heart killing her instantly on the side. 

Chapter fourteen

Outside the house Michael stewed stomping around. He liked Jojo but Daniel was bothering him. 
Michael wondered to himself “What does she see in a shitty jerk like Daniel?” 
He stewed and stomped towards the gravesite. He stood there frowning. 
A man’s voice spoke “Hello.”
Startling Michael who turned to see a man of Native American ancestry judging from his Native American clothes which were tan pants with a beaded trim, on his feet were moccasins and he wore a tan long sleeve top with colorful beads on it. His hair had streaks of gray in his black hair. 
The Native American again spoke “Hello.”
Michael stared at him with curiosity. 
He asked “Who are you?”
The Native American replied “I’m called Lone Eagle. You must be Michael, Claire’s son. You don’t remember me but I was chosen as your Godfather.” 
Michael stared at Lone Eagle and answered “Oh I don’t know if I remember you or not.” 
Lone Eagle sighed and spoke “I knew the Morgan family and I talked about them a lot.”
Michael frowned replying “What do you know about them?”
Lone Eagle spoke “That they had wolf blood in them along with the ability to change themselves into a wolf. That’s all I know.” 
He stiffened as Michael was about to say something when he heard Nanook’s barking. He turned around facing the forest and called out “Nanook! Nanook!”
He turned around and discovered that Lone Eagle had disappeared. 
Nanook came out of the forest barking with her tail wagging. Michael sighed and bent to rub Nanook’s flanks. She panted with excitement as he kneeled next to her. Nanook responded by giving him licks on the face. The back door opened and Sam came out angry. 
He yelled “Mike! It’s Grandfather!” 
Michael ran up the porch steps to Sam with Nanook and asked “What happened?” 
Sam answered “A wolf tried to attack Grandfather as he was coming in the house. Nanook saved his life by scaring the wolf away.” 
Michael spoke “Fuck it! How’s Grandfather doing?”
Sam replied “He’s holed up in his fucking room refusing to come out.”
Michael ran inside through the TV room; pass the front door to a hallway that lead to a series of two bedrooms. There was one on his right and one on his left. In front of him was a bathroom with the door open. 
He knocked on the bedroom on his right and heard his Grandfather’s voice saying “Go away I’m fine.”
Michael pounded on the door and yelled “It’s me, Michael! Are you alright? Sam told me what happened!”
The door opened and his Grandfather stared at Michael with a serious expression on his face. 
He spoke “Come in I have something to tell you.” 
Michael came in his room with Sam following along with Nanook. Inside his room was brown walls, a queen sized bed stood under a window in one corner. The TV was on with car racing in it. The dressers looked hand made out of wood. Grandfather closed the door and turned off the TV with a remote which he put on the table next to the bed. 
Michael stared at him and asked “What the hell happened?” 
Grandfather answered “It’s a skin walker. They have an interest in you, Michael. “
Michael gasped and spoke “Why?”
Grandfather went to his armchair in front of the TV and swiveled it around to face the boys. 
He spoke “Because you’re a skin walker.” 
Michael replied “Impossible! I have no ability to change into a wolf.” 
Grandfather sighed and spoke “Sure you do, but the ability stays dormant until it manifests whenever that is.” 
Sam asked “Why did that skin walker run away from Nanook?” 
Grandfather replied “Actually it was you who the wolf ran away from. Do you recall a man named Belen Morgan? Does he sound familiar?”
Michael and Sam both shook their heads as Nanook whined and put her head on Grandfather’s lap. 
Grandfather put a hand on her head and spoke “Here’s the story, The Morgan family had a curse on them that was passed. It passed to Belen Morgan. He was a wolf who tried to kill people but Luke Morgan stopped him several times. The only way to kill him with out the curse passing was by a destined Hunter. Coyote Wilson, a police officer was destined the Hunter. It was he who killed Belen Morgan stopping the curse. Now it appears he fathered a son just before he disappeared mysteriously. The son is you, Sam.” 
He paused to let Sam take shock of the words.
Sam spoke “Me? My father’s Coyote Wilson? It explains what I overheard when I was younger. One night I heard my adoptive parents’ arguing in the kitchen. I was in my bedroom of the apartment and had gotten up to get a drink of water just before I and my adoptive parents moved to Wolfville. They mentioned Coyote Wilson’s name and something about telling me about my biological father.” 
Michael spoke “How do I change into a wolf?” 
Grandfather answered “That fact is a mystery. It appears that there’s something to do with wolf DNA in your blood-“ 
At that moment he was interrupted with a knock on the door as Tina came in. 
She spoke with a serious expression on her face “The police just arrived. They want to see you.”
Grandfather got up and followed Tina to the front door with the boys behind him. A man with a crew cut and black hair in a police uniform stood with his partner a woman with red hair in a ponytail. 
His face was serious as he spoke “George Patricoly?” 
Grandfather replied “Yes that’s me. What happened?” 
The man sighed and spoke “Name’s Edward Larsen and this is my partner Ellie Jones. There’s no way to say it but your daughter Claire was in a car accident driving on her way here which is at the end of the driveway actually.” 
He paused to let Grandfather take stock of the news. 
Grandfather glared and spoke “Is she fine?”
Larsen sighed again and spoke “She’s in critical condition at the local General Hospital.”
Grandfather frowned again “There’s something you’re not telling me?” 
Larsen cleared his throat and spoke “Judging from the evidence on the road she was swerving and speeding as the car crashed into a tree.” 
Michael asked “Was she avoiding a wolf?” 
Larsen sighed again and answered “Uh evidence appears that she hit a woman named Anita McIntosh. Uh Anita didn’t survive the hit. There maybe charges against Claire Ryan.”
Grandfather interrupted with anger “Charges? What the hell are the charges for?”
Larsen frowned and answered “Charges for Manslaughter. Charges for driving while under the influence of alcohol. Her intake was above the legal limits of the state.”
Grandfather yelled “What? My daughter doesn’t drink and drive!” 
He waved his cane wildly. 
Jojo came from inside the house and pulled Grandfather away with a soothing tone “There, there, don’t get your blood pressure up.” 
She escorted him inside. 
Michael glared at the cop and spoke “Mom never told me she had a drinking problem.” 
Jones holding out a file with Claire’s name on it said, “She had Driving Underneath the Influence cases back as a teenager when she was your age along doing that repeatedly.” 
Michael grabbed the file and opened it. He read the report with a younger picture of his mother on it. Sam read over his shoulder as Tina peered over Michael’s other shoulder reading the contents. The file had a list of drinking and driving over a two year period when Claire was eighteen and nineteen. Michael crumbled the file and handed it back to Jones. He stormed inside the house. 
Sam glared at the officers and spoke “What happens now?” 
As Tina went inside crying, Larsen sighed with pity in his eyes and answered “It depends on Claire if she wakes up or not then we’ll see.” 
Sighing he turned and left with Jones to the car as Sam stood glaring at them. 

In the car on the way to the police station Jones spoke on the radio "Jones here" and a voice answered “Yes?” 
Jones spoke “Tell him we did what was asked.”
As Larsen drove the car to the police station, the voice spoke “Will do.” 

Chapter fifteen

Sam stood glaring as the police car drove away. His suspicions were on the rise. Some sense told him that there was something wrong with the accident. He walked inside and saw Michael going out the back door stumping away. Tina sat on a chair with tears in her eyes as she held Hocus the cat. Nanook came up to Sam whining to be petted. Sam sighed and gave Nanook a scratch on the head. He saw Jojo soothing a still angry Grandfather who sat fuming. Sam studied Jojo who was busy trying to calm Grandfather down. Sam went up the stairs to the loft where the computer was. He opened the computer and went online a search engine for police records for the public to check. He typed the name Anita McIntosh and read the contents. 
Then abruptly the computer screen flashed “Virus alert!” 
Sam typed some keys printing out the information as the computer began to shut down. He stared at the printer as it printed the information on Anita. He took the paper and walked downstairs. 

Downstairs Jojo saw him with a computer printout. 
She spoke “Oh the computer has a virus; don’t use it until I get a new Defense against Viruses computer ware.”

Jojo ran into the forest until she ran smack into Daniel. 
She spoke “Here give this to the Pack Leader to read.”

He yelled “Where the hell did you take the paper?”
Jojo sighed and instead of answering she ran into the house with Sam following. 

Inside Tina was sitting next to Grandfather watching TV. She saw Sam and Jojo come in.

Jojo denied “I don’t know what he was talking about. He followed me outside.” 
Sam glared at Jojo who had a face of innocence. 
Grandfather spoke sighing “Sam, what was on the paper?” 
Sam replied “Police files on Anita McIntosh for trespassing Government Lands and soliciting as a prostitute in Hartford.”
Grandfather groaned and spoke “I don’t know if that will hold up in court if they decide to charge Claire. Keep looking.” 
Sam spoke “I’m going to town. I got to check out the town.” 
Grandfather spoke “It’s a long walk but at least you’ll get some exercise but change your shoes. I don’t think you’ll get far in those shoes.” 
He meant Sam’s hiking boots. Sam went to the couch and pulled out some high top sneakers and changed his shoes. 
Jojo spoke “Good luck looking at the site of the accident.” 
Sam froze as he thought “How the hell did she know that?”
Grandfather spoke “Take Nanook for a walk for protection. Tina, give him Nanook’s leash.” 
Tina obeyed going in the sun room and grabbed Nanook’s least as Nanook joyously bounded besides her. She hooked the leash onto Nanook’s collar and handed it to Sam. Sam glared at Jojo then left the house slamming the door.

Chapter sixteen

The walk to the accident site didn’t take long. It was a short walk to the end of the driveway. A police car sat with people crawling all over the area. There were yellow police “Caution” tapes around an area. Sam saw Claire’s car a station wagon being hauled to a tow truck. Its front looked banged up along with windshield looking smashed up. Sam stood watching them tow the car. Nanook tugged on the leash. He followed her to a tree and she pawed the ground. Sam saw her bark at him and look towards the ground. He saw a bottle of wine sitting there with an animal print obviously not Nanook’s. Sam stared at it. Then a foot reached in his focus and stamped over the animal print. 
Sam looked up to stare at Daniel who grinned and shouted “Hey over here! The dog found a wine bottle!” 
Then he turned and left waving his hand. Sam heard Nanook growling at Daniel and had to restrain her as the male walked away. 
Sam glared at his back as a police officer came and spoke “Move your dog, Sam It’s wrecking the area.”
Sam recognized Officer Larsen and obeyed. He pulled Nanook away and stood on the dirt driveway watching them inspect the scene. Nanook tugged on the leash towards the tow truck. Sam let her tug him to the car. She put her paws on the passenger door of the car and barked. 
An officer came; opening the car door with force and he pulled out a grocery bag and spoke to Nanook, “Sorry doggie, evidence.” 
As he took the grocery bag away, Nanook whined and sat next to Sam cocking her head whining. Sam sighed and pulled Nanook with him towards the street lane. Several reporters crowded around taking pictures and reporting the scene. Sam ignored them and walked down the road with Nanook pulling the leash to town. He noticed people who were talking becoming silent as he neared them. He noticed some of them were glaring at him. Sam glared back at them too. Nanook pulled the leash and nearly dragged him towards a house. It was a two story house with a wrap around porch. Raya Ioniel stood on the porch sweeping with a broom. Sam heard her muttering something sounding like a chant as she swept with a broom. 
Nanook barked as Raya spoke “Hello Sam.” 
As she finished her sweeping and looked up, Sam studied the house, which the porch wrapped around the house in the front and the sides. There was a window on the house over the porch. He had a feeling of being watched. 
Nanook wagged her tail and panted as Sam spoke “You heard what happened to Claire?” 
Raya answered frowning “Yes I’ve heard. Poor Claire still can’t control her drinking habits.” 
Sam noticed her looking nervous as she said it. 
He asked “You look nervous why?”
Raya’s eyes widen as she thought “Ooh suspicious like his father Coyote Wilson.” 
She answered “Oh the car accident has me nervous.”
Sam asked “What made Claire drink in the first place?”
Raya replied “Oh it could be anything but I suspect it had to do something with her husband’s death. The anniversary is coming up soon.”
Sam spoke “Do you have a computer so I could look it up online?”
Raya sighed and spoke “Sorry don’t have a computer.” 
While looking more nervous as she waved at Sam and went inside the house. Sam led by Nanook walked away with suspicion on his face. Nanook abruptly barked and dragged the leash out of Sam’s hands. Sam had to jog while chasing the dog to behind the house as he saw a white wolf running away from the house. 
Sam yelled “Hey Nanook! Stop running from me!” 
The wolf kept running into the forest beyond. 
The back door opened and Raya yelled “Nanook! Stop!”
Nanook stopped running and went to Raya who grabbed the leash anger flashing in her eyes as she spoke “What is wrong with you, Nanook chasing after wolves? One of these days they’ll get the best of you. Michael and Tina would be upset with this.”
Saying this she went down the porch and handed the leash to Sam. Then she stormed into the house slamming the door. Sam crept up the stairs and peeked in the window. He could see her on the phone then he turned around and left the house. 

Inside the house Raya dialed a number and waited. 
A male electronic voice answered speaking “Hello? Raya-“
Raya cut off by angrily saying “Silent Walker, Sam came to visit with Nanook and he’s suspicious.” 
She heard the voice speaking “Calm down, Raya. He’s only a seventeen year old boy. Who’ll believe him if he finds out?”
Raya sighed and counted to ten and calmed down. 
She spoke “They saw a white wolf running from the house. Nanook gave chase but I stopped the poor dog.” 
The voice spoke “Don’t worry. The son of Coyote Wilson won’t cause us trouble.”
Then hung up as Raya stared at the phone, and hung up herself while speaking a chant a protection spell she learned from her mother. 

Chapter seventeen

Sam walked down the lane with Nanook ahead. It had a row of houses that looked old and forlorn. Sam passed the accident scene and walked to the horse corral. He found Jojo in the corral brushing a brown horse. She hummed as she brushed the horse’s rump and back sides. 
Sam startled her by asking “Was it you who left your family house?”
Jojo stiffened and turned to face him. 
She answered “No, I was here all day.” 
Sam turned and walked towards the house towing Nanook who followed behind him sniffing the plants and trees. Jojo sighed and turned back to the horse. She heard sounds of an ahem behind her and turned to look. 
She gasped and spoke “What are you doing here? You never came to the house and its grounds this close before.”
She watched as the brush was taken from her hand and then suddenly it was whipped across her face knocking her to the ground. Then the brush was dropped and Jojo painfully heard the person walking away in the forest. Jojo groaned and got up. She leaned against the horse and sighed. Then her eyes glowed gold as the bruise on her face went away healing her. Jojo groaned and sighs leaning onto the horse. She shook her head and felt a hand on her arm. Looking into the eyes of Daniel, who pulled her into a hug and kissed her on the lips then held her in a hug. 

Sam walked towards the house. He saw Grandfather sitting on the porch staring in space apparently thinking. 
Sam wandered up the stairs to sit next to Grandfather who spoke “You can let Nanook free of the leash now.” 
Sam obeyed and released Nanook who bounded down the stairs to the lawn. She came back with her ball her in mouth. She dropped it at Sam’s feet. Sam sighed and picked up the ball and threw it onto the lawn. Nanook joyously ran after it with her tongue out of her mouth. 
Grandfather spoke “Michael is in the back yard stewing away.” 
As Tina came out to sit next to them, Nanook came and dropped her ball at Tina’s feet. Tina threw it onto the yard as Nanook chased it. Sam went inside the front door and walked through the TV room to the sun room. He froze when he saw Michael standing in the yard talking to a man who was dressed like a Native American. Coming out of the back door onto the porch Sam saw them both look his direction and then the Native American jogged limping off. 
Sam wandered up to Michael and said “Who’s your friend?” 
Michael replied “His name’s Lone Eagle and he had to go. Sorry if he didn’t hung around for the introductions.” 
Sam spoke “That’s alright. So what were you talking about?”
Michael answered “Oh stuff about skin walking. I wanted to know what it feels like, makes me nervous if there’s pain.” 
Sam nodded in agreement. He knew of Michael’s fear of pain. Together the two of them walked inside the house. 

In the forest Lone Eagle stood watching them. He felt a tap on his shoulder and turned to look. 
“Oh it’s you” he said. “Did you know that Michael has a fear of pain?”
A hand reached towards his face and then reached back and slapped him. 
Lone Eagle stared and said “He deserved to know about his heritage and the wolf ability.” 
The hand turned to fist and punched him in the stomach. Lone Eagle glared as his eyes turned gold and his form shift towards a wolf. He turned into a gray wolf and bounded away passed a snarling white wolf. 

Chapter eighteen

Sam lay on his bed not sleeping with Hocus sitting in the window still. Sighing he got up and looked outside to see two wolves running towards each other and jumping around. To Sam they appeared to be fighting but from learning Nanook’s behavior and research online they were playing. The grey wolf was playing with wolf with white, grey and black splotches in patches on it. Sam watched them play dancing under the sky. Then both wolves ran into the forest. Sam felt a tap on his shoulder and turned to Michael who was peering over his shoulder. Sam saw a sense of longing on Michael’s face. 
He feeling irritate spoke “Knock the fuck off, Mike.”
Startling Michael who looked at Sam and spoke “Sorry but living in a city like Wolfville has me feeling trapped for years.”
Sam saw Hocus meow and scratch the door to his room. He heard Nanook barking from Tina’s room. 
Michael spoke “That’s funny. Nanook hardly barks when Tina is asleep.” 
Sam darted out of his room towards Tina’s room with Michael in tow. They could hear Nanook barking urgently. Inside they found Tina sitting on the floor crying. A bottle of pills were next to her. Sam grabbed the bottle as Michael gathered Tina in a hug. 
He asked her “How many pills did you take?”
As Sam opened the cover and spoke “None of them. It’s a new bottle of aspirin.”

Tina muttered “Why Mom why did you hide your drinking from us?”
Sam asked “Why did your Mom never told you about her drinking?”
Michael answered “I think she did in hints. She told me over and over never to drink and drive plus one night around our parents’ divorce, I caught her passed out on the bed with beer cans on the floor.”
Tina spoke crying “It explains their arguments. They were always yelling about something about drinking alcohol when the chips were down.”
“Uh” Sam said “I have a confession to make. I caught her one night staring at a can of beer like she was trying to decide on whether to drink it or not. I asked her right out if she was an alcoholic. At first she denied it and then she right out told me that she was an alcoholic when she was eighteen at Port Monaco a fact she hid from her Father-“
Tina interrupted “It explains why when Mike came home with beer cans and she made him pour them all out in the kitchen sink. Where the fuck did you get the beer cans anyway Mike?”
Michael answered “I got them from our fucking father’s apartment before it was sold along with several things too.”
Tina asked “What things?” 
Michael spoke “Their in the box room according to Mom.” 
As Tina fell asleep, he stared at Tina and then picked up his sister and placed her on the bed and pulled the blankets around her. Sam stood watching them. He went to the window and saw a white wolf sitting there. Michael joined him and saw the white wolf. The wolf sat staring at them then ran towards the forest and disappeared beyond. 
Sam spoke “That’s three times I’ve seen that wolf.”
Michael replied “There’s probably a bunch of white wolves around here.” 
Sam said “No I don’t think so.” 
Michael told him “I’m going to stay and sleep on the trundle bed in case Tina needs me.” 
He yawned and lied down on the trundle bed and fell asleep.
