Sam left the room and went to his room. He stood around staring at the bathroom door. Sensing an opportunity he walked through the bathroom to Michael’s room. It was similar to his. A bed in one corner with a dresser in another corner and they appeared to be hand made of old age with Native American designs on them. Sam went to the walls and lightly tapped them but they weren’t hollow. Sam sighed and walked out towards the door to the box room. Inside there were boxes of photo graphs of the Ryan family. There were pictures of Claire at a younger age with a younger looking George Patricoly. Sam sighed and kept looking. He found a black and white photo on the bottom of a box. In it were two men looking alike and a woman standing a bit taller than them with her arms around them. The two men had pants with beaded trim and vests with army shirts. The woman had sweatpants and an army tank top. Sam saw names scrawled next to them. It said the words Luke, Mark and Brittany Morgan on Army leave. Sam frowned and took the faded photo graph to Tina’s room. He roused Michael and Tina by turning on the over head light despite the window glowing of faded sunlight. Both Tina and Michael grumbled fuck words to being waked up. 
Sam excitedly spoke “Take a look at this.”
As he shoved the picture in Michael’s face. 
Michael grumbled “You woke me up to show a lousy fucking picture?”
Sam protested “It’s not a lousy fucking picture! It’s a picture of the Morgans!”
This got them wide awake as Tina sat up from the bed as Michael grabbed the photo and studied it. He sighed and handed it back to Sam. Tina got up from the bed and took the photo. She studied it for a minute looking at Michael and the photo. 
Michael asked “What the fuck are you implying?” 
Tina answered “Uh just checking to make sure if we resemble them but I don’t see it.” 
Sam asked “Is Grandfather up at this hour?” 
He gestured to the clock which showed five thirty on it. 
Michael sighed and spoke “I think we better show that photo to Grandfather.” 
Then they left the room and darted down stairs. 

Chapter nineteen

After a search with Nanook’s help they found Grandfather outside on the front porch sitting there apparently thinking. 
He spoke “Good Morning kids.” 
As they came up to him Sam handed him the photo. Grandfather studied it a moment. 
He spoke “The Morgan Legend. I believe Claire told you the story about them.” 
Sam asked “Why are they wearing Army tops and what's with the wording of army leave?”
Grandfather spoke “After their mother’s death and their father being put in a nursing home due to his mental health, they went to a military boarding school in some state. Alaska I think. Brittany studied everything about nature like a naturalist. As for Luke, he became a World Champion in some sport until he blew out his left knee in a fight and reportedly wound up with a limp. His brother, Mark got involved in a modeling business company working in offices of that business, became a vice president of a modeling company after working there shortly.”
Grandfather sighed then continued. 
“Their father fought in a war and they were honoring him on Brittany’s twenty first, birthday. She’ll be Claire’s age in her early forties wherever she is.” 
He studied the photo some more. The front door banged as Jojo came out with Daniel’s arm around her. Grandfather hid the photo in the pocket of his overalls. They stopped when they saw the Trio and Grandfather with somber faces. 
Jojo asked “What’s going on?”
Daniel looked concerned. 
Grandfather answered somberly “We were discussing the situation about Claire.”
Jojo spoke “Uh the hospital has called with an update. Claire is out of critical condition but she’s in a coma. The doctors are hoping she’ll wake up with the help of medicines.” 
Grandfather sighed and stared off at Nanook sniffing around the lawn. Michael watched as Jojo escorted Daniel to a sleek black Corvette and watched as the male got in and drove away. 
Jojo walked towards the Trio and spoke “My mother will be along shortly to cook breakfast for you all.” 
She sat next to Grandfather on a rocking chair. Soon they heard singing and chanting as Raya came up the dirt driveway singing in her Romanian language. She stopped singing when she saw them with somber faces. 
“Any news on Claire?” She asked. 
Jojo answered “She’s out of critical condition but is in a coma, which the doctors are trying to bring her out of.”
Raya spoke “I guess I better get breakfast cooking.” 
She went up the porch stairs to the front door and inside the house. 
Tina asked “What was she singing about?”
Jojo replied “Nothing just some chanting Mother habitually does.”
She got up and went inside. Michael sighed and went inside following her. Sam sat next to Tina watching Nanook sniffing around.
Sam spoke “Man that is odd, I saw a white wolf three times and Mike claims that it’s common around here.” 
Grandfather replied “Town legend says it’s Ghost the lone white wolf. No one has been able to capture that wolf. Some trackers claimed that the wolf was really a ghost and not real.” 
Sam answered “Hmm, I saw that wolf sitting outside my window twice and running away from Raya’s house, which Nanook gave chase.” 
Tina frowned and spoke “I had a dream of a white wolf that I was a skin walker and would die from that if I interfered with nature.”
Noticing Grandfather’s concerned look she added “It’s a fear of pain. I don’t like pain very well like Mike does. Please don’t tell Mike about my dream.” 
Grandfather abruptly got up and went inside slamming the door muttering “It’s none of my business and I should forget what I heard.” 
Sam asked “Well, what was your dream about Tina?”
Tina frowned and was about to say something when Nanook came bounding up with something in her mouth. She dropped it at Sam’s feet and he picked the item up. Sam saw it was a set of keys. 
Jojo came out and Sam hid the keys in his jean pocket. 
Jojo spoke “Breakfast is ready.” 
As she gave Sam a glaring look, while he tried to look innocent as then the three and the dog went inside. 

Chapter twenty 

Breakfast was a somber affair with the gang eating food silently. It was shattered by the phone shrilling. Raya got up from her seat and went to the wall where the phone was. Michael, Sam and Tina strained to hear what she said. Raya came out of the kitchen double doors with the cordless phone. 
“It’s for you, George.” She said. 
Grandfather took the phone she handed out and spoke “Hello, George Patricoly here.” 
Raya went and took the plates and went to the kitchen with Jojo following her. 
Michael, Sam and Tina sat staring at Grandfather who noticed them staring at him spoke “It’s the hospital. Claire is out of her coma but she appears to have suffered some sort of memory loss of the accident according to the doctors when they questioned her. ” 
He sounded angry when he said this. 
Michael asked “When can Mom come home?” 
Tina looked hopeful as Grandfather asked on the phone “Her children just asked me when their Mother can come home.” 
He frowned some more as he said “Uh huh oh ok.’ 
Then he disconnected the phone and spoke “The hospital says Claire, your Mother has suffered some kind of brain injury and she’s not responding to her memories properly. This might take awhile for they tell me that she says she doesn’t have any children.” 
Tina gasped as Michael frowned as Sam bravely asked “What do you mean she doesn’t have any children?” 
Grandfather replied “According to the doctors when they asked her about her life, she told them she’s a single woman in her twenties who isn’t married with children. What’s worse is she claims she lived in the forests as a wolf, oh hi Jojo.” 
The trio turned to look at Jojo standing at the doorway of the kitchen. 
A concerned look was on her face but she spoke “Sorry to eavesdrop but Mother wonders whether it’s a good idea to bring Michael and Tina to see Claire, in her car.” 
Grandfather spoke “The hospital told me it’s too soon to bring the kids to see her.” 
Saying this he got up and Jojo went to help him towards the TV room. Michael frowned and was about to say something when Sam pulled up a set of keys. 
Tina spoke “Nanook found those keys.”
Sam added “Jojo gave me a glaring look as I put the keys in my pocket.” 
He held them up for Michael to see while keeping an eye on the kitchen door. The Trio could hear Raya humming from the kitchen as she put the dishes in the dishwasher loudly. Michael took the keys and examined them. 
He spoke “The keys look old and have rust on them.”
Then he pocketed them as Jojo came in the dinning room. 
She spoke while giving Sam a glaring look “Are you going to sit there all day?”
Sam replied “No I want to explore the land and its boundaries.” 
Jojo frowned and spoke “I wouldn’t recommend it. There’s people who’s on drugs living in the forest who’ll do anything to get their next high and even murder too.” 
Sam’s eyes narrowed and spoke “Drugs? I don’t think so. I saw that they mysteriously wound up in the hospital with bite wounds.”
Seeing Tina and Michael’s questioning look. Sam answered “I checked it online at the school library during my last class in high school and found that Port Monaco maybe a rock and roll town but it’s the town with the most victims in the hospital.” 
Jojo stiffened and spoke “Someone blabbed to the tabloids for money.” 
Then she heard Raya calling for her and left to the kitchen. 
Michael handed Sam back the keys and got up and said “I’m going to town on my motorbike”. 
They heard Raya yell “Be back by one o'clock, Michael! It’s supposed to be a rain storm this afternoon.” 
Michael shrugged as he left the room, he heard Sam say “Don’t forget your helmet. I don’t want you to wind up like Claire.” 
“Yes Mom” Michael said teasingly to Sam as he left the house. 
Tina turned to Sam and spoke “I’m going to ask Jojo to let me ride a horse.” 
She left the dining room to the kitchen leaving Sam frowning. 

Sam got up and went to the TV room. He saw Grandfather watching racing cars on TV. Grandfather had a look on his face that he didn’t want to be disturbed so Sam wandered up the stairs to the loft towards the computer. He turned it on and the monitor stayed dead. He stared as the words “Virus Alert!” flashed on the monitor. Sam sighed and walked to the hallway where the bedrooms were. On a hunch, he pulled out the keys and tried them on one of the locked door. Then he heard someone coming up the stairs and pocketed them. It was Tina. 
Seeing Sam she spoke “Jojo says she can have me help take care of one of the horses but not ride one due to them being skittish towards new people” 
Sam asked her “Is that normal for horses?” 
Tina stood frowning, staring at Sam for a minute and shook her head and then went to her room with Sam following her. 
Sam spoke again “Isn’t that normal for a horse to accept people who ride them?” 
Tina annoyingly replied “I’m not a horse expert. Ok? I suspect it might be the skin walker gene I have which could make the horse nervous around me.” 
She grabbed a pair of jean overalls from the drawer and stared at Sam. 
“Do you mind?” she said, “I’m changing my clothes.” 
Sam sighed and left her room closing the door as Hocus streaked in the room and he heard Tina’s laughing examinations “Hocus! You silly cat!” 
Sam wandered down stairs to the TV room and went outside to the pool house. As he walked towards it a male he recognized as Daniel came striding out of the forest with a glare on his face that stopped in front of him. 
Sam spoke “You must be Daniel.” 
Daniel glared and then grabbed Sam as if pawing him. Sam twisted himself out of the grab and stood backing away. 
Daniel spoke “Give my keys back.” 
Sam spoke “What keys?” 
Daniel glared and answered “The keys in your back pocket of your jeans. I want them back.” 
Sam replied “I don’t know what you’re talking about.” 
Then he backed away as Daniel threw himself towards Sam grabbing him on the waist. Sam heard the keys jiggle out of his pocket and both reached for it at the same time knocking each other on the head. Sam gasped as he saw Daniel’s eyes glowed yellow and Daniel glared at him as his form changed into a black wolf. Sam reached for the keys but the wolf snapped at him. Growling the wolf grabbed the keys with his snout mouth and ran into the forest with Sam following him. Sam followed till the wolf was out of his sight and looked for tracks. He found the wolf’s tracks and came around a tree, while keeping the pool house in sight and saw Daniel lying on the ground and a white wolf was running away from Daniel with keys dangling in its mouth. Sam ran towards Daniel and could see that he had a bruise on his cheek. He watched as the bruise faded on Daniel’s cheek went away. Sam shook Daniel awake who glared at him and before Sam could talk, the male turned into a black wolf and ran away. 
Sam frowned and wondered to himself “What the fuck is going on here?” 
Then he walked towards the pool house. 

In the bushes the white wolf stood watching and then the form changed into a hooded figure dressed in all black. The figure turned and walked towards a tree growing out of a small hill and walked patting the ivies. Then Daniel came into sight as a black wolf changing out of his form. 
He spoke “Pack Leader, it wasn’t necessary to use force on me. We bumped heads and you know how-” 
As the figure held up a point finger as if shutting Daniel up, then proceeded to knock on the ivy till Daniel heard a hollow sound. The figure in black then pulled some ivy down and revealed a rusty moss covered door. Taking one of the keys the figure in black put the key in the keyhole and opened the door. Inside showed a hung figure corpse of a bald man in a tan suit of clothes. The figure stood watching the hung man. 
Daniel gasped “So that’s what happened to him.” 
The figure in black gestured with a nod of the head and Daniel went in pulling a dusty fallen chair near the corpse and put it in front of the man. He grabbed the ropes and yanked. The ropes fraying with age gave away as the corpse dropped in Daniel’s hands. Daniel saw a name tag came fluttering from the corpse. 
It read “Lawyer, Timothy Jones”. 
Daniel looked questioningly to Pack Leader, the figure in black. 
Pack Leader spoke a muffled voice “Put him where the trail walkers can find him. I’ll handle the rest.” 
Daniel obeyed and then walked away carrying the body over his shoulder. Pack Leader stood staring around the room then went out and closed the door locking it and moved the ivies to around the door. The figure howled a Human howl as a wolf came bounding out of the forest and changed its form to reveal Lone Eagle.
He spoke “Pack Leader, How long must you hide yourself? I saw Michael leave on a motorbike riding it towards town. He appeared to be wearing his helmet. I wouldn’t be surprised that he takes off the helmet because I did it before I blew out my knee.” 
Pack Leader shrugged and changed into a white wolf and bounded into the forest with Lone Eagle following in his wolf form. 

Chapter twenty one

Michael’s ride towards town was bumpy towards his standards. He drove by the accident sight to see it crawling with officers. 
He also saw a news crew came running towards him yelling “It’s Michael Ryan, the son of Claire Ryan! Hey! Stop!”
As he roared by them and went down the street, he passed by several houses and at a stop intersection he paused to see a couple, sitting outside a house glaring at him. The couple was a man and a woman with black hair and tan skin, who stood and looked at Michael as he looked to see their eyes glow yellow then he blinked his eyes and the couple went inside the house together. Michael shook his head and frowned as he drove by the intersection. He looked in the review mirror of his motor bike to see a news crew van driving behind him. 
He could hear the loudspeaker of the van saying “This is your local news station; we’re following Michael Ryan on motorbike.” 
“Fucking idiots” Michael thought “What the hell are they doing? I better lose them”. 
Then he drove towards the forest park where he rode on the grass by a tow truck blocking the drive way hauling a red sedan. Michael smiled of satisfaction as he heard fuck words from the news van aimed at the tow truck to get out of the way. Michael drove the motorbike down a trail hill and till he was out of sight and then he got off the bike and took off the helmet. He sighed and looked up at the sky. It was already mid morning judging by the sun but already clouds were forming still white. 
“I got plenty of time” he thought. 
As he looked to see a woman dressed in grey pant suit with a microphone and a cameraman holding a camera came from the top of the hill yelling “Michael Ryan, there’s ordinances that says you can’t ride your motorbike on the trails!” 
Michael dropped the helmet and got on the motorbike and drove up the hill towards them. 
The woman spoke towards the camera “This is Michael Ryan riding up the hill on his motorcycle without his helmet.” 
Michael road up the hill till his motorcycle almost reached the two then suddenly he turned the bike around spraying dirt at the news lady and then road down the trail. 
The news lady yelled sputtering “You fucking idiot! You could have gotten hurt!” 
As he went down the trail, the bike hit the helmet and then skidded towards the bushes with Michael yelling “Fuck it!” 
He drove away from the yelling news lady till he couldn’t hear her. As he tried to stop the bike the ground abruptly came to an end as Michael found himself air borne off a small hill with a tree growing out of it. He jumped from the bike and hit the rocks below as the bike hit the ground and roared away. Michael laid groaning and writhing in pain. He felt intense pain as if he broke a bone. He screamed out in pain howling. It didn’t come to Michael till later that his howls were wolf like.

In his pain haze Michael saw a white wolf came out of the bushes with several wolves. He could see the wolves turn into people but their features were fuzzy and he could hear voices talking faintly. Then he saw Lone Eagle holding out his hand and looking at Michael with some intense look on his face. 
Michael groaned out “Help me.” 
And grabbed Lone Eagle’s hand then he passed out. 

When he came too, Michael sneezed and shook himself violently. He was lying on a couch bed in what appeared to be a room. He sneezed again and felt a cool cloth put on his forehead. 
He heard a male voice spoke “Rest, Michael, the pain will go away.” 
Michael felt intense pain as if his body was shortening and fur was growing on him. His eyes sight turned purple and the figure in the room turned pink. Then he was in a wolf form yawning and stretching on the couch in pain. Then the pain went away as he returned to his Human form. 
Michael sighed and spoke weakly “What happened to me?”
Then the cloth was removed and he was lying on a couch in what appeared to be an office full of electronic equipment, complete with TV monitors and a man was staring at him. The man was wearing jeans, a beige shirt and a red plaid long sleeve shirt over the shirt. The man Michael recognized him, one of the couple who stood on the steps of a house glaring at him as he rode his motorbike. 
“Who are you?” Michael asked “And how did I get here?” 
The man spoke “The name is Silent Walker. You were brought here by Lone Eagle. No need to get up” as Michael struggled to get up with panic in his eyes. 
Silent Walker spoke again “Don’t worry I called Raya about you and she’ll tell the others and I’m actually a tribal healer.” 
While noticing Michael’s questioning look on his face, Michael asked “What happened to me?” 
 Silent Walker sighed and answered “You changed, due to that fall you had. It was the only way to heal you. You were suffering from internal injuries so your one of us now.” 
Michael lay down on the bed and frowned and spoke “What happened to my Mother Claire Ryan?” 
Silent Walker’s face frowned in a scowl and spoke “Please don’t mention that woman’s name in my presence. She’s not one of us and it’s not important.” 
Then he abruptly walked towards the desk in the corner, with a chair and sat down sideways to Michael. Michael sat up and felt dizziness. 
He sighed and lay down and asked “Who’s the woman that was with you?” 
Silent Walker spoke “She’s not important so get well okay?” 
Michael groaned and fell asleep. 

Chapter twenty two

Sam’s day was different from Michael’s. He walked towards the pool house and checked the doors but they were locked and so was the fence to the pool. Sam sighed and walked back to the house. 
He frowned and wondered thinking “Why would someone burn the pool house and Grandfather would build another on in its spot?” 
Then he walked to the porch and went inside the house. He walked toward the kitchen to see Raya on the phone with a serious expression on her face, and then she abruptly hung up. 
Sam asked her “Was that the hospital?” 
Startled Raya looked at him and answered “No, its Michael, he fell off his motorbike because of some news crew distracting him. No it’s just a few bumps and bruises. He’s at the doctors getting checked out.” 
Sam frowned and glared at her and then left the kitchen without a backwards glance. Raya sighed of relief and spoke some words in Romanian chanting. Then she left the kitchen to the TV room. 
She heard Sam telling Grandfather: “Raya tells me that Michael fell off his motorbike and has some bumps and bruises.” 
 Raya watched Grandfather reply “I hope he was wearing his helmet because it’s a town ordinance. Oh hi Raya.”
Sam looked to see Raya standing there with hands on her hips. 
Raya spoke “Don’t worry about Michael; he’s at the local doctors getting checked out, just to check for any other injuries.” 
Grandfather frowned and spoke “That’s fine with me.” 
He got up and hobbled with Sam’s assistance towards the front door and went to the rocker on the porch. Tina sat on the porch reading a book while throwing a ball for Nanook to chase. She looked up to see Grandfather and Sam entered the porch and went back to her book. Nanook came and dropped her ball in front of Sam who picked it up and threw it into the forest. Nanook ran after the throw. Then they heard her yelp and she came out of the forest with her tail between her legs. Sam got up as Daniel and Jojo came out of the forest. Sam noticed that Daniel had a stick in his hand which he tossed aside. Nanook went to the porch to sit next to Grandfather. Sam heard her whine as Daniel entered a corvette and drove away. Jojo stood watching the gang sitting on the porch. Sighing she pulled up Nanook’s ball from behind her and threw it in the forest. Nanook sat up on her haunches and plop her head on Grandfather’s lap. He stroked her head. 
Sam frowned and spoke “Michael fell off his motorbike because of some news crew distracting him. He according to Raya has a few bumps and bruises.” 
Tina looked up from her book and muttered “Motorbikes are nothing but trouble.” 
Jojo answered “Mother contacted me on my cell phone and told me that. I just sent Daniel to the local doctors to check this out.” 
Saying this she pulled out a cell phone from her back pocket and held it up. 
Nanook at the moment ran down the porch and pawed Jojo who exclaimed “Nanook, stop that!” 
Jojo dropped the cell phone and then Nanook picked it up and ran up the steps and dropped it at Sam’s feet. Sam picked it up and examined the cell phone. 
“Interesting device.” He said then he handed it back to Jojo who put in her back pocket of her jeans. He heard Nanook growl at Jojo who went inside the house as Grandfather stared at the forest. 
Sam asked “What are you thinking about, Grandfather?” 
Grandfather answered “I was thinking about Claire.” 
Sam spoke “Oh”. 

Daniel drove down the lane and slowed by caution tapes. He saw people there glaring at him. 
“Fucking druggies” he thought as he drove down the street towards an intersection. 
At the intersection he stopped and drove into a drive way of a white house. He got out of the car and sauntered towards the door, which opened revealing a woman dressed in purple sweat pants and a gray T-shirt, the woman’s black hair was up in a ponytail. 
Devices were in her ears he saw with recognition that she was deaf as she glared at Daniel, who signed in hand language while moving his mouth “I’m here for Michael.” 
Then she gestured to Daniel to come inside. He followed the woman inside the house. 

Inside in one of the rooms Michael lay groaning. He felt someone shake him and he woke up. 
Silent Walker stood and spoke “Daniel is here to take you home”
He gestured to Daniel standing there with a concerned look on his face. Michael saw his brown eyes turn gold for a minute then went back to brown. 
Michael groaning asked “He’s one of us?”
At Daniel’s nod, Silent Walker helped Michael out of the house towards the car. Once settled in the car Michael sighed and stared at Daniel who gunned the engine and pulled out of the driveway, then drove towards Grandfather’s house. 

At the house Tina looked up to see Daniel drive in the driveway with Michael looking sick. Grandfather sighed and watched as Sam went to help Daniel haul in Michael into the house with Tina following them. Grandfather got up and hobbled behind them as they went to the TV room and settled Michael on the couch. Grandfather went to an armchair and sat staring at Michael. Michael groaned out “I’m alright, Grandfather, just some bumps and bruises plus this awful headache.” 
Grandfather asked “Were you wearing your helmet?”
Michael sighed and noticing Daniel’s yellow eyed glare he answered “I don’t know. I can barely think straight with this awful headache.” 
Sam spoke “The headache must be because you took off your helmet.” 
Tina added “I don’t think you should be riding your motorbike for awhile Mike.” 
Michael looked at his sister and spoke “Believe me; I won’t be riding that thing for awhile.”
Grandfather spoke “You can take Claire’s bedroom. I don’t think she’ll be home for awhile due to the hospital stay.” 
Michael sighed and got up with Sam and Daniel’s help walked to Claire’s bedroom. The boys laid Michael down on the bed and he fell asleep. 
Sam grabbed Daniel’s shoulder, shook it off, and glared at Sam who spoke “You hit Nanook with a branch did you?” 
Daniel glared back and answered “So? You can’t prove it in this town.” 
Sam answered “The town’s controlled by skin walkers like you?” 
As he noticed Daniel’s eyes flared yellow and looked like he wanted to punch Sam when Tina wandered into the room. She frowned staring at Michael. 
“Poor Mike” she said “The motorbike according to Raya was found wrecked in a river. It smashed into a big boulder and it’s wrecked up.”
Daniel abruptly left the room slamming the door and Sam glared at him.
Tina noticing his glare asked “What’s going on?” 
Michael groaned out “Is Daniel gone?” 
Sam replied “Hell yes”
Michael sighed and spoke “I was followed by a fucking news crew who might put this event on TV.” 
Tina asked “What happened to you?” 
Michael answered “I fell off my bike off a hill and hit the ground hard” as an image of a biting white wolf came to his mind. 
Sam asked “Then what happened next?” 
Michael groaned as he felt a splitting headache come to him and he spoke “Owe my fucking head hurts. Once this shitty headache stops I’ll tell you the rest ok? So let me sleep."
Tina grabbed Sam’s arm and pulled him out of the room. They saw Grandfather in the TV room watching TV. 
 He looked up at them as Tina spoke “Mike is doing fine, except for a headache.” 
Grandfather sighed and answered “Ok, come here.” 
He gestured to Sam and Tina who came forward till they were close to Grandfather. 
Grandfather spoke whispering “Have you seen Michael’s eyes, the way he acted?”
Sam frowned and answered whispering “What do you mean his eyes?”
Grandfather looked toward the hallway to the kitchen and then looked at the duo and spoke “His eyes resembled one of a wolf when he looked at Daniel.”
Sam was about to speak but changed his mind and kept silent. 
Tina frowned and spoke whispering “You mean Mike did what? Wolf change into a skin walker?”
Grandfather asked her “How did you find out about skin walkers and Michael?”
Tina replied “On the car ride to home from school days ago with Mom. She saw my book about Wolves and told me outright about skin walking an ability to change into a wolf.”
Grandfather asked again “But about Michael?”
“I saw his eyes glow golden a bit when he looked at me” Tina whispered “as he lay down on the bed. I figured it out then with your talk.” 
Grandfather sighed and remarked loudly “Jojo, please check on Michael and see if he needs anything or not.” 
Tina and Sam turned to look at Jojo who stood there and spoke “Ok right away.” 
 The duo heard Grandfather mutter “Drat she might have heard everything with those ears of hers. Humph” as he turned on the TV to show car racing. 

Tina heard Nanook barking from outside went to the front door and let Nanook inside as the clouds in the sky appeared to darken. Sam wandered into the kitchen to watch Raya cook lunch. He asked “Why is the pool house locked?” 
Raya answered from the stove “It’s too cold for swimming.”
Sam sighed and heard Jojo walk into the kitchen. 
She spoke in Romanian “Michael is one of us now.” 
Raya spoke also in Romanian despite a glare from an annoyed Sam “Oh good, someone will have to introduce him to the Pack Leader.”
Jojo responded “I intended to once he feels better soon.” 
Raya spoke “I suggest we wait till Michael is up to walk in the forest, once the rain storm is over with.” 
As she prepared foods for the gang in the dining room Sam stalked towards the TV room and found Nanook sitting on her haunches in the sun room staring outside. Sam walked towards the sun room to see a white wolf sitting there on the edge of the forest watching. Sam groaned and stared at the wolf. The eyes of the wolf narrowed then the white wolf ran into the forest. 
Sam walked towards Grandfather as Raya came out of the kitchen saying “Lunch is ready. Sam help George to the dining room will you?” 
Sam sighed and then helped Grandfather out of the armchair down the hallway pass the kitchen towards the dining room. 

The sky became dark full of rain clouds and released the rain the clouds were holding after eating Sam wandered to Claire’s bedroom where Michael lay. He knocked on the door and heard a weak “Come in” said by Michael. 
Sam wandered in to see Michael sitting up in the bed staring at the walls. 
Sam spoke as he closed the door “Hi Mike, how are you feeling?” 
Michael replied “I’m doing ok but I still have a fucking headache” he cut himself off when he noticed Sam glaring at him. 
Michael added “What are you glaring at?”
Sam spoke “You skin walked did ya you fucker?”
Michael groaned out “How did you know that?”
Sam thought to himself “Better not mention Grandfather noticing his eyes.” 
He replied “I saw your eyes look like a wolf when you looked at Tina.” 
Michael sighed and replied “I guess I did. I don’t remember much of the accident.” 
Noticing Sam still glaring, Michael added “That’s the truth.” 
As they heard a knock on the door, Michael called out “Come in.” 
Jojo came in carrying a tray full of food which she set on Michael’s lap. Sam noticed her glare at him but kept his mouth shut. Then Jojo left the room closing the door. 
Sam sat on the armchair watching Michael eat the food. 
Michael stopped eating, swallowed some food and with fork raised asked Sam “Are you going to fucking stare at me eating?”
Sam answered “No, I’ll make like a tree and leave.”
He got up and left the room as Jojo came from the hallway towards him. 
“Skin walker” Sam muttered under his breath. 
Jojo annoyed asked “What did you just say?”
Sam replied “Nothing important for your fucking ears to hear. I was just muttering about Michael.”
Then he walked towards the TV room to go upstairs with Jojo glaring behind him with hands on her hips. 

Chapter twenty three

Night came with the end of the rains, as Sam lay on the bed in his room awake staring at the ceiling he wondered what made him ask Michael about skin walking.
He thought “It must be the Hunter gene speaking again.” 
Sam remembered his adoptive father telling him this saying “A Hunter must hunt to live” when he was ten years old. He heard scratching at his bedroom door and got up to open it and found Nanook sitting there with leash in her hand. 
“Oh you have to go.” He said as he snapped the leash on her collar.
Then he pulled on some red sweat top and pants and his sneakers while Nanook patiently waited. 
Then he let her pull him down the stairs towards the sun room. Sam stood frozen as a hooded figure in black stood on the porch illuminated in the light of the moon. Sam gripped Nanook’s leash that whined and opened the door. The figure turned and ran towards the forest. 
Sam called out “It’s alright, the dog won’t hurt you.” 
The figure kept running as Nanook strained on her leash. Sam walked outside grabbing a flashlight with him as Nanook pulled him towards the forest.

In the forest it was spooky and dark illuminated by the moon above and by Sam’s flash light. Sam sighed as Nanook went towards a tree and barked. Sam shined his flash light at Nanook’s direction and the flash light shined on a growling white wolf. Sam stood frozen staring at the white wolf who Grandfather called Ghost. He could see the wolf was totally white with yellow eyes and the eyes narrowed then the wolf bounded into the forest. Nanook strained on her leash and pulled Sam deeper into the forest with his flash light illuminating the way. Nanook led him to the pool house and barked at the door pawing it. Sam checked the door and found it locked. 
He told Nanook “The door is locked.” 
She howled and barked a racket. The porch light of the main house turned on. 
Grandfather came hobbling out and shouted “Sam! Quiet that dog! Will you? People are trying to sleep!” 
Then he limped back into the house and the porch light turned off. Sam sighed and pulled Nanook towards the main house. He heard her whine and bent to pet her sides as the hooded figure in black came around the tree with a thick stick in hand standing there. Sam stood up and pulled a barking Nanook towards the house as the hooded figure threatened with the stick shaking it at him and the dog. 

Inside Sam met a sleepy Tina wearing a bathrobe coming down the stairs with a plastic bag in her hand. 
He spoke “Tina, I saw a hooded figure in black threatening me with a stick.” 
Tina sighed and grabbed Nanook’s leash and spoke “It’s probably a druggie who was trying to get in to steal."
Then she took Nanook outside the front door for the dog to do her business. 
Sam followed them and spoke “I saw a white wolf again up close in the forest.” 
Tina replied “Must be Ghost the White wolf again.” 
Sam added “I think Ghost is trying to tell me something.” 
Tina sarcastically answered “I think it’s your imagination again.” 
Sam spoke “No I don’t think so at all.” 
He watched Nanook water the lawn and Tina pick up the scat of Nanook’s with a bag in hand. 
Then she held it out and asked “You mind throwing this in the garbage bin down the road?”
She gestured towards the road as Sam groaned. Tina handed the bag to him and sleepy hauled Nanook inside the house. 

Sam walked down the dirt road with flash light in hand. The forest was dark illuminated by the moon. He heard howls of wolves from beyond the forest. 
Sam sighed and muttered to himself “This is fucking ridiculous.” 
Carrying the bag he reached the end of the lane to see a big garbage bin sitting on the corner. Sam also could see yellow tapes outlining the accident scene of Claire’s. He opened the bin and threw the bag inside while looking behind him. Then he walked towards the house, he heard a twig snap behind him and turned around as a branch hit him in the face. Sam shook himself groggily and shined the flash light on the person to see it was the hooded figure in black who knocked the flash light out of his hands and then Sam blocked the branch from hitting him in the face with his arms. He ran towards the house and felt something hit him in the back and he fell towards the ground. 
Sam quickly rolled around to see the figure bring down the branch on his head as he fell unconscious he heard a muffled voice speak “You ruined everything, you fool.” 

When Sam came to, he found himself in a horse stall with a horse chewing on his hair. “Owe fuck.” he thought as he got up groggily and then went to the stall door. 
He found it locked and saw on the opposite side was the hooded figure in black standing there. 
Sam glared and asked “What the fuck do you want?” 
He heard a muffled voice speaking from the figure “Nothing, you shouldn’t have come to exist at all.”
Then the figure turned and left him banging on the stall door. 
In the darkness Sam grumbled and muttered “You shouldn’t have come to exist at all” he echoed. 
Then he felt his way around the small stall. The horse left him alone munching on the hay. Sam sighed and then went to a corner to sit down in the hay. He sat in the darkness sitting there thinking despite having a headache. 

Morning came with a scream that woke up Sam. He woke up to see Tina standing at the stall door staring at him. 
He got up and stomped out grumbling to Tina “The fucking druggie hit me with a branch and locked me in here.” 
Tina led the horse out with a halter and followed an angry Sam towards the coral with the other horses. Sam opened the gate and let Tina come through with the horse and closed it behind him. He leaned on the fence as Tina released the horse. 
She went to join Sam and asked “What did the druggie look like?”
“Some Gothic person all dressed in black with a hood covering the face” Sam answered. 
Tina was about to reply when they heard Jojo’s angry voice speaking from behind them “Sam where have you been and why did you sleep in the horse stall with Honeycomb?”
Sam grumbled and climbed the fence with Tina and then he reached Jojo at the fence and answered her question with “Some fucking druggie person hit me in the head with a branch and locked me in the horse stall.” 
Jojo asked “What did this druggie look like?”
Sam answered “Like some fucking shitty Goth person dressed in black with the face hidden by a hood” as he stomped by her towards the house with Tina following behind him. 
Jojo wandered towards the forest and came upon a white wolf who growled at her. 
She spoke “Ghost, what’s going on?” 
Ghost’s form changed into the figure in black who Jojo sighed and spoke “Pack Leader, what did Sam do?” 
A muffled voice answered her from Pack Leader “He and the dog caught me as I was about to go inside the house to visit Michael last night.” 
Jojo asked “Why leave Sam in the horse stall?”
Pack Leader replied “It was just a warning that’s all” as a black wolf came from the bushes changing into Daniel. 
“Pack Leader” Daniel said “Michael is up and awake inside the house.” 
Pack Leader spoke “Lead him to me, and I’ll handle the rest” as the form changed into Ghost. Then the wolf bounded away. Daniel nodded towards Jojo and went into his black wolf form and ran into the bushes. Jojo went towards the house. 

In the house Sam passed by a confused Grandfather while stomping upstairs to his room. 
Tina told Grandfather “I found Sam sleeping in Honeycomb’s stall. He was hit by some Gothic druggie who locked him in there.” 
Grandfather sighed and spoke “The druggie must desperate” as the front door banged open.
Jojo came in and Grandfather spoke “Tina, will you go in to the kitchen? I want to talk to Jojo alone for a minute.” 
Tina obeyed and walked towards the kitchen doors. Grandfather watched her leave as Jojo came in the room.
He called “Jojo come here.” 
Jojo came and spoke “Something I could do for you?”
Grandfather spoke annoyed “Tell your Pack Leader to control those minions of his especially around Sam.” 
Jojo glared at Grandfather and spoke “I don’t know what you’re talking about.” 
Then she turned on her heel as Grandfather spoke “Yes you do.”
Jojo stomped towards the kitchen and slammed the door. She found her Mother there with Tina petting Hocus the cat. The cat meowed and arched as Tina rubbed his back. 
Jojo angrily spoke in Romanian to her mother “George said quoting tell your Pack Leader to control those minions of his especially around Sam.” 
Raya replied also in Romanian “And what did you tell him?”
Jojo noticing Tina’s concentrating look on her face spoke “I told him I don’t know what you’re talking about. Where did he get the idea?”
Raya cooked the food on the stove and spoke “The Goddess has a way of things around here.” 
Jojo sighed and went to sit down at the small round kitchen table. 
She replied “George is getting suspicious.” 
Tina sat next to her on the chair. Hocus jumped from the island counter to jump onto Tina’s lap. The cat proceeded to purr loudly as Tina gave the cat scratches and rubs. 
Raya responded by saying in English “Goodness gracious the cat is being friendly with you.”
Tina spoke “I guess my skin walking gene hasn’t manufactured yet.” 
Raya went to Tina and kneeled in front of her speaking “Don’t worry about the skin walking gene, you won’t die from it. I promise you.” 
The kitchen door banged open and Michael came in, “When’s breakfast?” he asked. 
Raya got up and went to the stove and resumed cooking. 
Tina told Michael “I found Sam locked in Honeycomb’s stall. He says some Gothic weirdo knocked him out with a branch and locked him in the stall.”
Michael stiffened but kept his mouth shut when he noticed Jojo glaring at him. He saw her eyes flare yellow then she blinked her eyes and they went back to normal. 
Tina heard Hocus hiss and she stroked the cat who settled down on her lap. 
Michael spoke “Probably some druggie I guess wanted drugs hit Sam.”
With that comment he abruptly left the kitchen towards the TV room. In the TV room Michael stood watching Grandfather snoozing away. He wandered outside and saw Daniel walking from the forest. 
Daniel spoke “Pack Leader wants to see you, follow me.” 
Then Daniel walked up to Michael and whispered in his ear and then Michael changed into a wolf as Daniel did the same. The two went into the forest.

Chapter twenty four

In the forest Michael in a gray wolf form followed Daniel till they reached a river. Daniel took a drink from the river and gestured to Michael to do the same. Michael took a drink in his wolf form and swallowed the water. Then the two wolves walked following the river to a small waterfall and piles of rocks around with a small hill and a tree growing out of the hill. Daniel changed out of his wolf form and howled as Michael changed into his Human form. The bushes rattled startling Michael as two wolves came forward. One Michael saw was Ghost the white wolf the other was a gray wolf who changed form to reveal Lone Eagle to Michael’s surprise. Then the white wolf changed form to reveal a hooded figure in black. Michael saw that the figure was wearing black sneakers and loose black sweatpants with a bullet proof vest over the black sweatshirt and some kind of hood covered the entire face. 
Lone Eagle spoke “This is Pack Leader.” 
Gesturing to the hooded figure in black with his hand as Michael spoke “Hello.” 
He heard a muffled voice from Pack Leader speaking “Greetings Michael.”
Daniel noticed a confused look on Michael’s face explained “Pack Leader’s identity is only revealed to those who trust is earned.” 
Michael answered “I understand.” 
As he was about to say more is when they heard a faint bell ringing sound. 
Daniel spoke “Its Raya ringing the bell. She wants you back for breakfast, I’ll lead you back.”
Michael followed Daniel in a wolf form till they reached the edge of the forest leading to the house and then changed back to Human forms. Daniel bid Michael bye and walked away. Michael walked towards the house to Raya. 
Raya spoke “Oh you’ve seen Pack Leader.” 
Michael stared at her as she explained “It’s that look on your face that says it all. Poor Pack Leader still hasn’t shown anyone except Lone Eagle his identity.” 
Saying this Michael followed Raya into the house with a confused look on his face. 
He asked “How come?” 
Raya answered as they walked towards the kitchen “Embarrassment or something that would have made Pack Leader recognizable.” 

In the dining room Michael found Grandfather on the phone, and then he disconnected the phone. 
Sam and Tina sat on the benches watching Grandfather. 
Michael asked “Grandfather was that the hospital?”
Grandfather answered “Sit down, Michael.”
As Raya brought the food, Michael looked at Grandfather while waiting for the food to be served. 
“What’s going on?” Michael asked again “And excuse me for being nosy.” 
Grandfather spoke “Local druggies found a body hung in the trees, which the cops identify as Timothy Jones the realtor who sold the house to me before you kids were born.” 
Tina asked “Why did they call you?”
Grandfather answered “Because the cops are saying his body was found on the border of my lands” while sounding angry.
Sam spoke “So this is murder isn’t it?”
Grandfather angrily answered “No the cops are calling it suicide. They found a ladder next to the tree along with a note.” 
Sam replied “How long has Timothy been hanging?”
Grandfather glared and spoke “I ordered his body to be examined by the local coroner. Besides he was the father of Octaves Ryan.” 
The Trio gasped as Raya dropped a plate on the table. Jojo came from the kitchen hearing the racket.
Grandfather continued again “I had a DNA test done on your Father, before he died in the plane crash reveals that he was Timothy Jones’ son with an unknown woman.”
Raya stiffened. 
Grandfather continued “I also had his plane accident checked out. It appears that it was due to mechanical error related to lightening striking it so there’s nothing fishy about it.” 
Michael spoke “When will you find out about our unknown Grandmother?”
Grandfather answered “I’m having some leads checked out but don’t worry I’ll find her.” 
Raya excused herself from the table and then walked into the kitchen. She muttered a chanting spell and then found Jojo’s hand on her arm. Raya spoke something whispering in Jojo’s ear then Jojo nodded and left the kitchen towards outside. Raya composed herself and then went to the dining room. She found most of the food untouched. 
Raya spoke “Why is most of the food untouched?”
Grandfather spoke “I guess it must be the bad news about the death of Timothy Jones their other Grandfather.”
Raya harrumphed and then picked up the plates of uneaten food and spoke “I’ll see that you’ll have to eat it for dinner tonight.” 
Saying this she left the room carrying plates of uneaten foods. Michael felt Nanook nudge him with her snout and petted her on the head. Then Nanook followed him out of the dinning room towards the TV room. In the TV room Michael sighed and grabbed Nanook’s leash and clipped it on the dog. Then he took the dog outside the front towards the barn. He could sense himself being watched, and then Nanook barked. He stood and held Nanook’s collar as Pack Leader came from behind a tree and stood watching them. 
Pack Leader gestured and spoke “Please come with me and bring the dog.” 
Michael got up, nodded and followed Pack Leader with Nanook through the bushes past several trees till they reached the river. 
Pack Leader spoke “Jojo tells me that your Grandfather George Patricoly has found out the identity of your other Grandfather.” 
Nanook at the moment barked and another gray wolf came bounding out of the bushes towards them. 
The wolf changed into Jojo who spoke “I’ll take the dog with me to the house” as she took the leash from Michael, Nanook barked. 
Lone Eagle came out of the forest and spoke “State Troopers with tracking devices have been seen by patrols going in the forest. They appear to have dart guns with them and an antenna, a tracking device.” 
Pack Leader spoke “Jojo take Michael to the house, while we will watch the State Troopers.” 
Jojo obeyed and Michael followed her and the dog towards the house. 

On the way towards the house, Michael heard bushes rumbling as a group of eight State Troopers came with dart guns from out of the bushes. Jojo glared at them and handed Michael, Nanook’s leash. 
She spoke to the state troopers, “This land belongs to George Patricoly and this is his grandson Michael Ryan. What are you doing here?”
One of the State Troopers came forward and spoke “We have permission from George Patricoly to find and remove any wolves we come upon.” 
Michael recited “Without wolves to control the deer population, the deer will eat all of the grass and grow too numerous and cause havoc in crossing the roads with cars hitting them. Not to mention the deer will eat in people’s back yards. Also-“
He cut himself off when one of the State Troopers put his hand to his mouth and yawned while speaking “Orders are orders.” 
Saying this they left the duo with the dog walking further into the forest. 

At the house, Daniel came out of the bushes in his Human form with a worried expression on his face. Seeing Jojo, he went toward her and kissed her on the lips. Michael looked away with jealousy on his face. He led Nanook towards the house and went inside, was a State Trooper talking to Grandfather who was sitting in an armchair. They both went silent when they saw Michael come in with Nanook. 
Michael asked “Why are there people walking in the land with dart guns?”
Grandfather replied “Wolves killed one of my colts in the paddock some other day.” 
Michael didn’t know why but he felt like Grandfather was lying when he said this. He also noticed Sam sitting on the couch dressed with his hair partly damp. Michael glared at Sam and then released Nanook from the leash that went to sit at the fireplace. 
Sam waited as the State Trooper left the room before speaking “Michael, where’s Tina?” 
As she came in from the front door and spoke “Grandfather, there’s State Troopers combing the land.” 
Grandfather replied “I know I sent them to find any wolves they can and remove them.” 
Michael spoke “It’s because one of them killed a colt in the paddock.” 
Tina glared and spoke “Yeah right, I just came from the paddock and the horses are fine but skittish.” 
The Trio looked at Grandfather who got up and hobbled towards his room. 
Michael angrily stood in his way and spoke “Out with it Grandfather, what’s really going on?”
Grandfather spoke “One of the skin walker minions hit Sam and locked him in a horse stall. I won’t tolerate behavior like that towards Sam. The sweep is a warning to the skin walkers and you, Michael can tell your Pack Leader that.” 
Saying this he limped around Michael and stomped towards his room. The Trio heard his bedroom door slam. 
Tina spoke “Your Pack Leader? What did Grandfather meant by that?”
Michael sighed and spoke “I met the skin walkers’ Pack Leader today” while noticing Sam’s narrowed gaze. 
He added “The Pack Leader’s identity was hidden from me because they have yet to earn my trust.” 
Sam nodded his head in agreeing as his cat Hocus came and jumped on the couch. Sam gave Hocus some scratches as Tina picked up the cat. Hocus meowed as Nanook got up and barked. 
Tina spoke “Cut that out Nanook.” 
Nanook instead kept barking at the fireplace. Sam got up and proceeded to feel the wood with his hands. He felt nothing out of ordinary as he knocked on the fireplace and heard a hollow sound. 
Sam spoke “The fireplace is hollow.” 
Michael replied “Must be the chimney” as he went to sit on the couch with Tina holding Hocus. 
Sam spoke “I don’t think it’s the chimney. I think it’s something else.” 
As Michael sighed and asked “You think it’s some hidden passage?”
Sam answered “Yeah I think so” as Nanook pawed the fireplace with her paws. 
Sam stared at the fireplace and spoke “The house is three stories tall with a window for the attic and I’ve been exploring the house and I can’t find an entrance to the attic or that room with that shuttered window.” 
At that moment the doorbell rang, the Trio walked to the front door. 
Michael opened the door to see Officer Edward Larsen there who spoke “Hi kids, is your Grandfather around?”
The trio heard Grandfather’s bedroom door slam as he came limping towards the door. Grandfather angrily spoke “What’s going on?” as he went to the front door. 
Officer Larsen seeing him spoke again “We caught someone trespassing on your lands.” 
He gestured towards the car where his partner opened the door and hauled out a glaring Daniel. 
Grandfather spoke “Oh that’s Daniel, Jojo Ioniel’s boyfriend” as Jojo came to the door looking annoyed. 
She gasped when she saw Daniel in handcuffs and spoke “What’s my boyfriend doing in handcuffs?”
Officer Larsen replied “The State Troopers caught him walking on George Patricoly’s lands. He wouldn’t give us a legit reason why he was trespassing plus there was no ID on him. He kept insisting that he was Jojo Ioniel’s boyfriend.”
He gestured towards his partner who released Daniel who grumbled to himself while looking angry. 
Officer Larsen spoke again “Sorry for the trouble.” 
Then he turned to the squad car and with his partner got in and drove away. Grandfather harrumphed and limped back towards his bedroom. The gang heard his bedroom door slam. 
Jojo walked towards a grumbling Daniel and asked him “What happened?”
Daniel angrily spoke “I was walking towards my car which is parked on the street, and I had to cut through the lands to get to there just to avoid the news crew. Then the State Troopers did some surprise attack on me as I was walking around the bushes. Humph.” 
Jojo put an arm on his shoulder and the two walked down the driveway talking. Michael sighed and wandered inside the house with Tina still holding a meowing Hocus. Sam stood on the porch steps watching Jojo and Daniel whisper to each other while walking down the driveway. He went to sit on a rocker and sat watching Jojo and Daniel till they were out of sight. Sighing he got up and walked inside the house. 

Chapter twenty five

Inside the house Nanook was still pawing the fireplace with her paws. Michael grabbed her collar and her leash and hauled the dog outside as Sam came in. He noticed Tina had turned on the TV and was watching it. Hocus wounded himself around Sam’s legs, who bent to pet the cat. Then Sam wandered outside the backyard to see the State Troopers come out of the forest.
He heard one of them swear “Fuck it! We’ve been going around in a fucking circle!” 
Then the State Troopers walked around the house leaving Sam standing there watching them leave. As they disappeared out of sight he heard a wolf howl followed by several wolves howling. Then Sam walked towards the gravesites and stood staring at it. He could see some roses lying there that were fresh. 
Sam thought to himself “What happened to the Morgans anyway?”
He heard Raya call him from the back porch saying “Sam! Would you come inside? It’s not safe with the State Troopers hanging around.” 
Sam walked towards the house and at the porch he asked Raya “Why are there roses on the gravesite?” 
“Oh” Raya said “I put the roses there.” 
Sam noticed that she looked nervous saying this. He frowned and then followed Raya inside the house. 

Outside the front door, Michael stood holding Nanook on a leash. He walked towards the side of the house. He met the same State Troopers there, who one of them yawned in his presence. Michael sighed and looked at the house. On the third story was a shuttered window. Michael wasn’t sure what the window led but he let Nanook pull him down the dirt driveway towards the barn where he saw Jojo and Daniel kissing. Michael sighed with jealousy as Nanook bounded towards the pair. They stopped kissing to look at Michael walking towards them being led by Nanook. 
Jojo sighed and spoke “I’ll see you later Daniel” as Daniel turned and left walking down the dirt driveway. 
Michael asked Jojo “Do you have any idea why they arrested Daniel?”
Jojo answered “It must be what I told him, dressed as a punk rocker.” 
Michael replied “Oh,” as Nanook barked at the barn. 
They looked to see Pack Leader come out of the barn with Lone Eagle who both was talking became silent. 
Michael spoke “Did you know that the State Troopers arrested Daniel then let him go when Jojo identified him?”
He heard Pack Leader speak “Yes I know.” 
Lone Eagle frowned and spoke “Jojo did you tell him to wear his driver’s license ID?”
Jojo answered “Yes I did which Daniel promised me.”
Then Michael watched as Pack Leader and Lone Eagle left them to walk back into the barn closing the barn doors. 
Michael asked Jojo, “Why did your Mother say that Pack Leader only shown Lone Eagle his identity?”
“I don’t know” Jojo said “I do know that there’s a rumor among us that Pack Leader started hiding when one of the Humans attempt to betray Pack Leader.” 
Michael asked “Who was the Human who did this?”
Jojo frowned and spoke “I don’t know, maybe someone close to Pack Leader, who hurt Pack Leader badly.” 

Inside the barn in an unused stall sat on the piles of scattered hay was Lone Eagle with Pack Leader who took the hood off revealing a ski mask on the head and hiding the mouth and only showing the eyes. 
Lone Eagle spoke “Oh, which reminds me what happened to Coyote Wilson?”
Pack Leader spoke muffled “He was attacked because he attempted to betray me.” 
Lone Eagle asked “How did he betray you?”
“It was Sam the reason why he was going to betray me” said Pack Leader angrily.
Lone Eagle spoke “It explains Coyote Wilson was found in the river.” 
Pack Leader spoke “Yes poor Detective Wilson, his Father, I had him put in some mental asylum because the idiot was babbling about me being responsible for his son’s accident. Humph.”
Lone Eagle asked again “What about Timothy Jones the lawyer and realtor?” 
Pack Leader grumbled out “That idiotic fool was nosy enough to find the cabin due to some map which I had burned and he is hung as a result.” 
Then they heard the barn door open and the voices of the State Troopers speaking, “Check the barn!” 
Despite protests from Jojo saying “Don’t bother there’s just horses in here.” 
Pack Leader immediately put the hood on, in the stall and Lone Eagle covered Pack Leader with hay. Then Lone Eagle sat on the hay and as if mediating. 
He didn’t have long to wait because he heard the State Troopers exclaim “There’s a Native American in this stall!” 
Lone Eagle heard the stall door open and felt a poke from a State Trooper’s gun saying “Wake up Native American, who are you?” 
Lone Eagle opened his eyes and slowly pulled out his ID card from a chain around him and held it up for the State Trooper to look at. The other State Troopers piled around him to read the card. 
He heard one of them reading it “The card says Lone Eagle Horse Giver”. 
Lone Eagle heard another State Trooper say “What are you doing here Lone Eagle?” 
Lone Eagle replied “I help take care of the horses in the corral. I was mediating when you bothered me.” 
He heard a State Trooper answer “We’ll settle that with George Patricoly.” 
Then they grabbed Lone Eagle, cuffing him and hauled him out of the barn with a glaring Jojo and Michael standing there witnessing. The duo with the dog followed them towards the house.
 
At the house Grandfather sat on the rocking chair in the porch with Sam sitting on the steps. They both heard the commotion of the State Troopers leading a man who was dressed like a Native American while being followed by Michael and Jojo with a barking Nanook.
One of the State Troopers spoke to Grandfather “Do you know this man?”
Grandfather stared at Lone Eagle for a minute and spoke “Sorry I don’t know him.” 
One of the State Troopers handed him Lone Eagle’s Identification card and Grandfather read it out loud “Lone Eagle Horse Giver, Hmm sorry the name doesn’t sound familiar” while noticing Michael and Jojo’s glare at him. 
The same State Trooper spoke again “We found him in a stall in the barn mediating he says and Lone Eagle here claims to help take care of the horses in the corral.” 
Grandfather frowned and spoke “Sorry doesn’t ring any bells.” 
Jojo spoke “You don’t remember him, but he does help me with the horses in the corral.” 
Grandfather spoke again to Lone Eagle, “I’m sorry sir; I don’t remember you helping out with the horses before I hurt my leg, or after.” 
Grandfather watched as the State Troopers hauled Lone Eagle down the lane towards a squad car where they put him in it. 
Michael protested to Grandfather “He does help Jojo with the horses. I’ve seen him-” Grandfather cut him off with a wave of his hand. 
Grandfather spoke “It’s obvious that Lone Eagle is a skin walker judging by the looks of him.” 
Michael spoke again “Oh how do you know that? Plus isn’t it discrimination because of his skin color and the way he’s dressed?”
Grandfather answered “Yes I know, but he’s still a skin walker to me.” 
Grandfather got up and limped inside the house slamming the door. Michael followed with Nanook whining inside the house. Jojo stood with her hands on her hips and frowned. 
Sam asked her, “Was he really a skin walker?”
Jojo shook her head and spoke “How should the hell I know?” then stormed inside the house with Sam following her.

Chapter twenty six

Night came as Sam slept uneasily, as he felt like something was bothering him, so he got up and went to the window. Staring at his window was Ghost who walked around the house. Sam opened his door slowly and went out the hallway noisily. He didn’t notice Michael watching him from the adjoining bathroom nor does he noticed Michael follow him to the loft. At the stairs Sam strained to hear as the front door opened and closed. He was about to walk downstairs when he felt a tap on his shoulder and hand on his mouth. 
He heard Michael whisper “Shh it’s me, Michael, what’s going on?”
Sam whispered back “Ghost the skin walker has entered the house. I hope he won’t do any harm to Grandfather” as the two slowly tiptoed down the stairs. 
Then abruptly the front door banged open and close and they heard someone pounding on the porch. Sam ran towards the front door and turned on the light just to see Ghost running away. 
They heard Grandfather’s door open and him sleepily yell out “What’s the hell is going on there?!” 
Sam was about to speak when Michael called out “Oh it’s just a druggie trying to break in the house. We scared him off.” 
Then they heard Grandfather’s door slam shut and Sam asked Michael ‘Why couldn’t you let me tell the truth?”
Michael replied “I don’t know, it just came out.” 
He turned and tripped over a wrapped package with the words George Patricoly scrawled on it. 
Sam picked up the package and gave it a shake and heard nothing serious from it. He looked at Michael questioningly who took the package and then walked to Grandfather’s door and knocked. 
They heard Grandfather yell “What? I’m trying to sleep here!”
Michael spoke “The druggie was a messenger, left a package on the hallway addressed to you.” 
The door opened and Grandfather came out. 
He grabbed the package and gave it a shake, then frowned as he spoke “Michael, throw it out in the garbage outside. I refused to accept packages from the druggies.”
The boys heard him harrumph as he slammed the door in Michael’s face. 
Sam grabbed the package and was about to open it when Michael stopped him by saying “You don’t know what’s in there.” 
Sighing Sam thrust the package to Michael and spoke “Excuse me for being nosy. You go throw it out in the dumpster near the end of the street. I did that last time with Nanook’s shit.” 
Saying this he left Michael standing there and he heard Sam walk up the stairs. 
Michael sighed and then was about to open the package when he got an image of a white wolf with snow around the wolf in his head saying “Don’t open it.” 
Michael sighed and then got the same image as he was about to open the package again. Grumbling he slowly opened the door to see Daniel standing there who grabbed the package and ran into the night. 
Michael shook his head and muttered to himself “This is getting weirder and weirder. Ugh, I’m going to bed.” 
He met a sleepy Tina on the stairs who asked him “What’s going on?” 
Michael answered “Nothing to worry about” while noticing Tina’s glare he added “Don’t worry about it. Go back to bed.” 
Then he walked by Tina who stood with hands on her hips and spoke to herself “Boys, go figure.” 
 
In the morning the Trio was talking about the night visitor at breakfast in the dining room. 
Sam spoke “I think Ghost is a skin walker” 
As he looked at Grandfather who glared and spoke “It figures that whoever tried to catch Ghost has been catching some hoodlum.”
Michael kicked Sam in the shin as he was about to say something. 
Sam looked at Michael who asked “Who is the hoodlum they have been catching?”
Grandfather answered “Someone who witnesses haven’t yet to come forward identifying the hoodlum” as he glared at Michael. 
Michael sighed and Sam spoke despite a kick in the shin by Michael “What did this hoodlum look like?” 
Grandfather replied “No witnesses have come forward admitting that except you Sam.” 
Tina asked “When will the State Troopers stop searching the lands?”
Grandfather answered firmly “As long as their needed.” 
Then he limped towards the living room with Jojo helping him. Raya gathered the plates of no foods and Tina went to help her by carrying the plates of leftover foods. 
Sam grumbled “Mike, why are you fucking kicking me?”
Michael answered “Because you have a fucking big mouth.” 
Sam replied to that remark “Oh really, I bet you your fucking Pack Leader, that Ghost was that black hoodlum who knocked me out and left me in the barn.” 
Michael responded sarcastically “Yeah right” as they glared at each other. 
Tina came back from the kitchen and jokingly spoke “Guys, are you going to sit there having some staring contest?”
Michael got up and spoke “No, not really.” 
Then he left the dining room and Tina with Sam heard the front door bang shut. 
Tina asked Sam “What’s with Mike anyway?”

Michael sat on the porch steps staring in space as State Troopers came from the bushes grumbling. 
“This is ridiculous!” he heard one of them yelled followed by another saying “Let’s stop and go for coffee instead.” 
Michael heard them walk away down the driveway towards the accident site. Frowning he got up and walked following them when he was abruptly grabbed by behind and yanked into the forest. He felt a hand clamp over his mouth and the familiar muffled voice of Pack Leader speaking “Don’t, there’s news people there and their really nosy.” 
Michael was let go and turned to look at Pack Leader speaking “What happened to you to be covered up?”
Pack Leader answered “Because a Human betrayed me and we’ll leave it at that.” 
Michael watched as Pack Leader’s form changed into a white wolf that bounded away. 
Sighing Michael walked towards the house to see Sam standing there glaring on the porch steps. 
“The State Troopers have called off the search.” He said to Michael. 
Michael spoke “Oh, too bad.” 
Sam asked “Why is your Pack Leader’s identity hidden?”
Michael got an image of a stalking white wolf apparently snarling in his minds eye followed by the wolf speaking “Don’t tell him that.” 
Michael replied “How I should know?”
Sam spoke “Yeah right” and went inside the house. 
Michael groaned and went to sit on the porch steps.  
He put his head in his hands and thought to himself “A Human betrayal?” 

At the town’s police station Officer Larsen was at his desk typing a report on his computer when the door banged opened. He looked up to see a frowning man dressed in Native American outfit being hauled inside by State Troopers. 
Larsen stood up from his desk as one of the State Trooper came to him and spoke “Lone Eagle Horse Giver is his name and book him for trespassing on private lands belonging to George Patricoly.” 
Larsen obeyed and soon the man was released from the cuffs and behind bars in a cell next to his desk. 
Larsen asked the State Trooper with black hair with streaks of grey in it and pale skin whose name plate read “Johnson” was standing there outside the bars of the cell watching Lone Eagle “What’s going on?’
The State Trooper Johnson spoke with eyes narrowed “George Patricoly called us to track a wolf on his property and remove it, but so far the wolf has been evasive. We found signs of more than one wolf. Plus thanks to some news crews, we got people from animal rights groups protesting the removal outside” with a jerk of his head, Larsen followed Johnson to the window that led outside where protesters with waving signs stood. 
“Ugh” Larsen spoke “Great, the boss is going to have me for lunch.” 
He noticed Johnson staring at him and at his name plate that read Sergeant Larsen, Boss. 
Larsen spoke “I have reports to type, excuse me.” 
Then he abruptly walked towards his desk watched by Johnson with narrowed eyes and went to his computer. He heard the front door of the police station open and closed as Johnson left the Police Station. Larsen shook his head and grabbed the phone. 
He dialed a number and waited as a male voice spoke “Hello?”
Larsen spoke “Larsen here, we got a problem.” 

Silent Walker put the phone down with a scowl on his face. He heard a rap on the door to his office and looked to see his female cousin Cheyenne deaf and silent standing there watching him. 
He hand signed “There’s a State Trooper named Johnson, who is suspicious. He might be a problem.” 
She nodded and signed “What are we going to do if he’s a Rogue?”
Silent Walker hand signed back “That remains to be seen but he’ll be watched.” 

Chapter twenty seven

Night came as Pack Leader left the barn towards the house. Pack Leader stood there watching the house and walked slowly around the perimeter. Reaching the graves, Pack Leader kneeled and did some muttering chant. Then Pack Leader slowly got up and changed form to Ghost. Ghost went to sit facing a window, above, watching and waiting. 

Inside Sam couldn’t sleep, he tossed and turned then he got up in his pajamas towards the window and looked. Outside sat Ghost, who was staring at his window as Sam sighed and stood staring at Ghost. Then he yawned and went back to bed to sleep. In his sleep he dreamed that he was walking in a forest full of snow in his pajamas. Sam felt no coldness but the heat coming from the tips of his toes to his head as he walked barefoot in the snow. He saw some tracks of a wolf and followed it towards a clearing which he stood hidden behind a tree. In the clearing a woman came walking dressed in white clothes with her black hair pulled up in a ponytail. Sam gasped for he recognized the woman to be Brittany Morgan from the photo. He stood watching silently as the woman went behind a tree holding long knife in her hand. Sam could see her eyes narrow with concentration as she pulled on a hood covering her head and kneeled hugging the tree under its fallen limbs. Then Sam saw a movement out of his eyes to see a figure an older version of him self complete with long blonde hair pulled back came crashing out of the forest dressed in jeans, boots, with a brown jacket.
“Coyote Wilson” Sam thought from his hiding place.
The male, Coyote Wilson put his hands to mouth and yelled “Brittany! Where are you?!”
Sam could only watch as Coyote stomped near the tree where Brittany hid. Brittany erupted from her hiding place throwing the knife at Coyote’s chest. Sam could only watch with horror as Coyote staggered staring at a glaring Brittany with the knife in his chest then he fell towards the ground and lay still. Sam watched as Brittany pulled the knife from Coyote’s chest and went to a tree and wiped the blood off the knife with leaves. Then she stomped away in the snow dragging Coyote’s body. Sam felt him self following the two till they reached a river where Brittany threw in Coyote’s body and then walked away. 

Sam awoke with a start gasping as sweat covered his brow. He frowned as the light of the new day shined in the window. Checking the time, Sam saw that it was around eleven in the morning. Groaning he got up and got dressed exchanging his pajamas to his jeans shorts, tank top and plaid shirt over the tank top. Sam sighed and plopped on his sneakers after putting on socks. Then he went to the door of his room to downstairs. Downstairs he heard humming from the kitchen and went to the kitchen to see Raya at the stove cooking away. 
“Sam” she said without looking from the stove, “It’s about time you got up.” 
Sam asked “Where’s everybody?”
Raya answered “Oh George is in his room, while Tina is with Jojo at the horses corral. Michael is hanging around somewhere.”
Sam sighed and went to the table to sit and he stared out the window. He frowned as he saw Ghost sitting in the edges of the forests staring at him. 
He didn’t notice Raya turn around and see Sam staring out the window, seeing Ghost the white wolf. Raya took a plate of foods and set it on the table in front of Sam who picked up a fork and absent mind began to eat while staring out the window. 
Sam spoke after swallowing a mouthful of food, “What’s with Ghost the white wolf anyway? I keep seeing Ghost sitting under my window staring during the night several times.”
Raya sighed and sat next to Sam in a chair and sat staring out the window. Ghost outside at that moment turned and walked away into the forest.
Raya heard Sam mutter “Weird dream.”
Raya asked “Sam, did you have any strange dreams?’
Sam asked while eating bites of food “What strange dreams?’
Raya choose her words carefully as she spoke “Legend is that Ghost communicates to people by dreams.” 
Sam frowned and said “Just one weird dream I had last night of a woman stabbing a guy and throwing his body in a river, Humph.”
Raya choked on a gasp and asked carefully “Can you identify the woman and the victim?”
Sam spoke “The man said one name ‘Brittany’ and the man reminded me of myself which was an older version of me actually.” 
He didn’t notice Raya put her hands on her head and leaned on her elbows on the table while staring at Sam. 
Sam drank from a cup and once finished the cup, spoke “Thanks for the food, Raya. I’ll go look around and see if I could find Mike.” 
He got up and wandered out of the kitchen. Raya stood up and picked up the plate with the cup and walked towards the dish washer. She hummed to herself and heard Grandfather come limping in the kitchen. Raya looked to see Grandfather with a glare on his face.
“You’re the missing Grandmother who I’ve been seeking.” He said with accusation in his voice.
Raya calmly spoke “Prove it, George.” 
She watched as Grandfather pulled a folded paper from his pocket and thrust it at her. She took it and saw that the paper was an official document on DNA tests. She read the results to see that the tests between her, Michael and Tina were similar. 
Frowning Raya sarcastically spoke “So I’m related to the kids, doesn’t mean I’m this missing Grandmother.” 
Noticing Grandfather’s glare she added “Did you check to see if Timothy Jones Senior had any other relatives, alive?”
Grandfather limped towards her and snatched the paper out of her hand and limped out of the kitchen slamming the double doors. 

Sam wandered outside to see Michael sitting on the steps throwing a ball for Nanook to chase. He sat down next to Michael watching him. 
Michael noticing Sam’s stare asked “What ya staring at?”
Sam replied “I had a dream last night of Brittany Morgan and my father, Coyote Wilson.” 
Michael spoke “Go on. What was your dream about?”
Sam leaned forward and whispered the contents of his dream to Michael who stared at him with shock.
“Weird” Michael said, “I just think something fucking funny is going on here.” 
Sam added “Raya told me that there’s a legend that Ghost can communicate to people through dreams and I bet that was it.”
Michael heard Nanook whining and heard a car come in the driveway. Sam and Michael both looked to see a police car came in the driveway. They both watched as a man with grey streaks in his black hair, in a tan police uniform got out of the car with a glare on his face. 
The man spoke to Sam and Michael “The name’s State Trooper Johnson. Is your Grandfather around?”
They both heard the front door slam to see Grandfather came limping outside with an annoyed look on his face. 
Grandfather spoke “Something I could do for you Officer?”
Johnson spoke “I’m State Trooper Johnson. May I discus something with you in private?”
Grandfather gestured towards the back end of the porch. Johnson walked up the stairs towards the back end of the porch on the other side of the house. Michael sat watching them talk as Sam narrowed his eyes as Grandfather and Johnson both whispered with their backs to the two. The two watched as Grandfather threw one of his hands up in the air as he whispered to Johnson. Then they saw as Johnson patted Grandfather on the shoulder and then walked away towards the two. Johnson gave Michael and Sam a nod of his head before walking to his car and driving away. They both saw Grandfather stood banging his cane on the porch grumbling to self. Then Grandfather limped over to them and stood with anger in his face. 
“Well” he said to the two “Somebody bribed and a prisoner is free.” 
He limped inside the house slamming the door with a confused Sam watching him. 
Michael spoke “Lone Eagle Horse Giver, I bet is who he’s talking about.” 
Sam looked at Michael and spoke “Must be then, it must be Pack Leader who did that.” 
Michael answered “I don’t know if it’s Pack Leader who did that or not.” 
Sam spoke “Oh come on. The town is run by fucking people like you.” 
Michael asked “What makes you think of that shit?”
“I got this idea from Daniel” Sam said and added “I think it was one of the wolves that forced Claire off the road, Mike.” 
Michael gasped “Sam! What the fuck?!”
Sam answered “I think it was because of the bottle of wine Nanook found next to a wolf print.” 
Michael gasped “Bottle of wine?’
Sam added “It was Daniel who erased the wolf print with his shoes and I bet you that someone made Claire crash and then dumped some of the contents of the wine bottle down her throat.” 
Michael gave a grunt sound and then Nanook barked as a car came in the driveway. The two could see it was Daniel who came out of the corvette closing the door. They heard Nanook growling.
“Greetings,’ Daniel spoke “have you seen Jojo?”
 Sam spoke “At the horse corral with Tina.” 
 Daniel gave a mock bow and walked towards the barn. 

At the horse corral Jojo and Tina were chatting while leaning on the fence. 
Tina asked Jojo “How old were you when you changed?”
Jojo asked “Changed?”
Tina replied “You know, changed into a wolf form like what happened to Mike.” 
Jojo spoke “Uh, I don’t like talking about that.”
Tina pressed “How come? This happened to Mike.” 
Jojo was suddenly grabbed by behind and Tina looked to see Daniel turn her around and kissed Jojo on the lips. 
Tina spoke laughingly “Get a room you two.” 
Daniel placed a kiss on Jojo’s lips then let her go and stood facing Tina. 
“Greetings” Daniel said “How are the horses?”
Tina giggled and spoke “The horses are doing fine today.” 
Jojo spoke “Come on Tina let’s go to the house and see what Mother cooked for lunch.” 
The three walked from the horse corral towards the house. 

On the way to the house, Tina asked Daniel “When are you going to propose to her?’
Daniel gulped and stammered “I don’t know.” 
Jojo spoke “I think it depends on how this relationship continues. We just met at the beginning of June.” 
Tina spoke “Oh. I see so it’s too soon to tell right?”
Daniel nodded his head as Jojo replied “Yes.”
