They heard Nanook barking and followed the barking towards the house where Michael was there with Sam sitting on the porch steps. 
Michael seeing Daniel with Jojo and Tina, growled to Nanook “Sit!”
Nanook sat next to the Michael as he heard her growl aimed at Daniel. Sam sat watching the three reach the porch steps. 
Tina spoke “About time you were up, Sam. I tried to wake you up in time for breakfast, but you kept on sleeping, ignoring me.”
Sam nodded his head and stood watching Daniel, Jojo and Tina enter the house. He heard Michael groan and looked at him. 
Michael groaned out “Oh why, oh why do I feel a fucking feeling for Jojo when she has a boyfriend?”
Sam frowned and sat next to Michael and spoke “It must be your shitty hormones acting again.” 
Michael grumbled and got up with Nanook following him into the house. Sam sat on the porch steps. He felt a feeling of being watched and shuddered at that feeling. Then he got up and walked inside the house. Out of the bushes Ghost came out and stood watching Sam leave. Then Ghost walked into the forest. 

Inside the house the group sat at the dining room table eating lunch as Raya exclaimed “Sam, I just fed you and you’re still hungry?”
Sam spoke “I guess I’m hungrier than I thought.” 
Daniel spoke “So what’s new with Claire?”
That brought the cheery mood around the table to somber. 
Daniel noticing the somber moods on his companions’ faces spoke again “Sorry I had to bring that up.” 
Grandfather spoke “Well, the news on Claire is still the same according to the hospital who called an hour ago.” 
Michael and Tina both frowned. Michael could hear Nanook whimpering and he reached a hand and rubbed the dog’s head. Nanook barked and Hocus the cat came jumping on the table. 
Raya spoke “Get that cat off the table before he eats the food.” 
Sam groaned, reached for the cat and pulled Hocus off the table. He left the dining room with Nanook following. 
Tina spoke “Excuse me.” 
Then she got up from the table to follow Sam holding Hocus with Nanook following behind them. 
Raya frowned and spoke “Oh well, so Daniel are you wearing your driver’s license?”
Daniel answered by pulling a wallet out of the back of his ripped blue jeans and opened the wallet showing his drivers’ license. 
“I got it done this morning” he said. 
Jojo spoke “About time.” 
Grandfather harrumphed as he slowly got up and limped off. They heard Sam came in the dining room with a questioning look on his face. 
He asked “What did I miss?”
Michael answered “Daniel got his driver’s license done.”
“Oh” said Sam who went to help Raya clear the table. 
Michael watched as Jojo with Daniel left the dining room then he picked up some plates and left to the kitchen. 
In the kitchen Raya spoke to Sam “Did you have any strange dreams, Sam?”
Michael heard Sam replied as he walked into the kitchen “Just that weird dream of Brittany stabbing my Father whatever that means.”
Raya hummed to herself as she bent to put the dishes in the dishwasher. Michael followed her example and helped her to put dishes in the dishwasher. 
Michael broke the silence by speaking “What happened to your Father anyway?”
Sam spoke “I don’t know but I’ve heard my adoptive parents mention him in terms like he survived.”
Raya asked “Survived what?”
Sam replied, “Probably what I dreamed.” 
Michael shockingly asked “Your Father survived a knife wound and a near drowning?”
Sam sighed and sat at the kitchen table with Hocus sitting there hissing as Nanook sat next to the table eying Hocus. 
Sam spoke “My adoptive parents over the years told me that my Mother is locked up because she tried to kill my Father.”
Michael and Raya both gasped and they looked at each other with shock on their faces then at Sam who stared at them with narrowed eyes. 
“What’s going on?” he asked them. 
Raya sighed and spoke “Sorry but I’m surprised with what you told me” as Michael echoed the same comment. 
Hocus at the moment hissed out a meow as the three looked to see a white wolf running from the kitchen window to the forest beyond. 
Sam spoke “What’s with Ghost anyway?’
Raya and Michael exchanged glances and nodded their heads in a silent agreement as Sam kept looking out the window. 
Then Sam spoke “I keep seeing Ghost around too much.” 
Raya went to the phone and dialed a number as Michael went to join Sam looking out the window. 
They both heard Raya speaking Romanian to someone on the phone and turned to watch Raya talk while hearing her mention the words, “Brittany Morgan”, “Coyote Wilson” 
Raya hung up the phone and spoke to the two “Just asked some of my sources to check out some information anyway. It’s possible that your Mother might be alive.” 
Sam shrugged and went to look out the window as Michael sat down giving the cat some body scratches. Hocus purred loudly as Nanook whined. 
Raya went to the dog and petted Nanook’s head. The three sat in silence lost in thought. Then they heard the kitchen door slam as Tina came in. 
“What’s with the frown faces?” Tina asked “Plus I met this Officer Johnson, some State Trooper wandering around the horses corral claiming he was looking for something. Guy gave me the creeps with his eyes, Ugh.” 
Raya frowned and an “Ooh” escaped from her as the teens looked at her with confusion on their faces. 
Sam asked “Did you call Officer Johnson?”
Raya sighed and spoke “That I admit, No, I called some police officers in the state department to check out Sam’s Mother.” 
She walked over to a sitting Sam and tousled with his blonde hair. 
Sam spoke “Tina, my adoptive parents mentioned to me over the years that my biological Mother was locked up for trying to kill my Father.”
Tina sighed and asked “I’m missing something am I?”
Sam related the events of his strange dream to Tina who stared open mouth.
“Ouch!” Tina exclaimed and added “So sorry to hear of that.” 
Sam spoke “Yeah.”
Michael sighed and got up to wander out of the kitchen. Tina, Sam and Raya heard the back door slam. Sam looked outside the window to see Michael walking towards the gravesites then walked into the forests. 
Sam spoke out loud “Jeez, lucky you Mike. You get to run in the forests without a care and I have to watch myself.”
Tina and Raya exchanged glances as Sam stood up and left the kitchen. Hocus jumped from the table to the blocky kitchen island in the middle of the kitchen. Nanook gave a bark at Hocus who arched and hissed at Nanook. 
“Fucking damn cat” Tina said “Always torturing Nanook.” 
Raya spoke “Please watch your language. It’s in Nanook’s nature to chase Hocus. She sees Hocus as a prey.”
Tina spoke “Well-”
At that moment she was interrupted by the phone ringing, Raya went to get it. She frowned hearing the contents and then hung up. Tina stared as Raya closed her eyes and muttered something in Romanian.
Tina asked “What’s going on?”
Raya replied “Trouble and danger for us all.” 

Chapter twenty eight

The heat of summer came in the night as Ghost wandered into the forest walking silently and alert. Ghost sat down on its stomach and closed its eyes. In a dream, Ghost changed the form to the hooded Pack Leader with long knife in hand facing the bushes covered with snow. Slowly a man with long blond hair, wearing green hunting army clothes came out with an identical knife in hand stood. 
Pack Leader spoke firmly “You’re not wanted around here.”
The man narrowed his blue eyes, stood his ground and spoke “Or you’ll what? You can’t harm me anymore like you did once, Brittany.” 
He smiled as Pack Leader gasped out “That name is no longer me, Coyote” 
Coyote spoke “I managed to survive you throwing me in the river but I had to hide myself from you. Poor you thinking I was dead.”
He smiled at Pack Leader who growled “I haven’t forgiven you for taking our son away and hiding him from me.” 
Coyote frowned and spoke “It was necessary for our son’s welfare. The others would have killed him.” 
Pack Leader growled sniffing the cold snowy air “Too bad, you should leave before the others arrive.” 
Coyote spoke “Oh really? The others can’t harm me.” 
Then he backed away with knife in hand and disappeared into the snowy bushes. Pack Leader put the knife away and changed form to Ghost who woke up and ran into the bushes towards a river. Ghost sat at the river growling then walked towards the forest. 

In the forest Pack Leader abruptly changed form as another figure came charging and jumped to the side in a Human form to see the figure who was dressed in black with some half mask covering the part of the face with the mouth peering out. 
“Longbow” Pack Leader growled “The others won’t tolerate you.” 
The masked figure in black said a male voice snarled “Oh they will, Brittany.” 
Pack Leader hauled off the hood and ski mask revealing a face pale from not being under the sun with brown eyes and long black wavy hair of a woman who spoke “Prepare to fight Longbow” as she held out a long knife.
Longbow held out a knife identical to Brittany’s. They parried knives flashing. 
Longbow smiled a menacing smile as he made a cut on Brittany’s left cheek. She growled at Longbow and attacked, which Longbow twisted to the side and knocked the knife out of Brittany’s hand and stuck the side of his knife at her throat. 
“Do you yield, Brittany?” He demanded. 
Brittany’s response was to spit at him, and he spoke “Very well, the others know of your son with Coyote and I suggest you yield or else.” 
Brittany held up her hands and waited for the knife to cut her throat. Longbow grabbed her hair and hauled her towards the edge of the forests with knife still at her throat. 
He spoke “As Pack Leader, I’m ordering you to change your form and get your son out of the house.” 
Brittany spat a fuck word at him and changed her form to Ghost who walked to the window of the house. Longbow howled some call of victory in his Human form. 

Sam lay on the bed sweating in the heat of the night. He was frowning as he stared at the ceiling then he got up and heard Nanook barking from the hallway. Getting up he felt a mild wave of dizziness as he got up to his bedroom door. Opening the door he saw Nanook who stopped barking and whined a sad sound. He followed Nanook outside his room to see Michael lying on the ground in the hallway, gripping his head as his body changed from Human to Wolf and back. 
“Mike” Sam ran to Michael and shook him. 
Michael moaned out “Pack Leader” then he gripped his head and changed to a gray wolf who snapped at Sam.
Sam backed away with Nanook growling at Michael in wolf form. 
Michael changed into his Human form and spoke “Go outside Sam.” 
Sam stiffened when he heard the order in a voice not Michael’s. 
Michael repeated the command and pointed to the hallway behind Sam who stood his ground and walked to his room with Nanook following him, slamming the door, locking it behind him.
He grumbled to himself “What’s gotten in Mike anyway?”
Then he heard pounding on the door as Nanook growled. Sam went to the window and looked to see Ghost sitting there. He sighed as Ghost turned and bounded away. 
The pounding on his door stopped then he lie on the bed and fell asleep. 

Brittany dragged herself with her cheek healing towards her cabin which was a small hill with ivy and a tree growing out of it. 
She reached for the keys at her sock and heard Longbow say “Looking for these?”
He thrust the rusted keys in her line of sight. She looked up at him to spit but received a whack on the back of her head from his other hand. 
She saw Longbow lean towards her with his mask still on his face speaking “You’ll learn to respect me like the others have” and he kissed her right cheek. 
Then he grabbed one of her hands and dropped the keys in her hand then walked away. Brittany snarled at his retreating back. She unlocked the door to the cabin and stepped inside. Groaning Brittany walked towards the dusty couch and lay curled in a ball. 
She moaned as she fell asleep, “Coyote, where are you?”

It was still hot as ever that Sam dragged himself from the bed to down stairs to the dining room. He saw Tina with Michael sitting there at the table while Sam heard Raya talking to Jojo from the kitchen. Their voices were too low to make out the conversation. Sam walked to the table and sat. He noticed Michael glaring at him. 
Sam spoke “What are you looking at Mike?’
Michael replied “Nothing.” 
Jojo came from the kitchen with her Mother carrying plates of foods. 
Sam asked Grandfather “How come you don’t have an air conditioner?”
Grandfather spoke “Don’t need one and don’t ask me to get a damned air conditioner.”
Sam groaned. 

The group ate the foods in silence. The phone rang and Raya went to get up to the wall and answer it. 
She spoke “Oh it’s for you George.” 
She handed the cordless to Grandfather who spoke “George Patricoly here.”
The group watched as his eyes narrowed and spoke with an angry tone “Who the hell is this?”
Grandfather abruptly slammed the phone down on the table, disconnecting it and grumbled out loud “Some druggie got this phone number from who knows where and is threatening me harm.” 
Shaking his head he got up from the table and limped towards the TV room. 
Jojo asked in Romanian “Mother, who was that really?”
Raya replied in Romanian “Georgina, Someone who’ll bring dread” as Raya went into the kitchen with Jojo following her.
Sam asked “Michael, do you remember what happened last night?”
Michael looked confused spoke “What, what happened last night?”
Sam sighed and said to Tina, “I found your brother Mike lying on the floor with an apparent headache.” 
At that moment he felt Michael kick him in the shin and glared at him who glared back. 
Tina spoke “It must be the heat because I had a bad headache last night too.”
Sam spoke “Oh really? Michael was saying Pack Leader before telling me to go outside.” 
Tina looked at Michael for confirmation, who said “Like Tina here said, I had a bad headache last night and I don’t remember much about what I said to you.” 
Sam spoke “Yeah right, you ordered me to go outside with some fucking creepy voice.” 
Michael asked “Creepy voice?”
Tina looked at Sam who added “Yeah your voice was strange like someone was talking through you.” 

At that moment the Trio heard the phone ring from the kitchen and heard Raya yell out “I’ll get it!” 
 Sam got up and walked into the kitchen with Michael and Tina following him. They stood in the kitchen with Jojo watching Raya on the phone with a range of emotions on her face. 
“Uh huh” she said and added “The kids are in the kitchen watching me. Yes Sam is here. You want to talk to him?”
Michael abruptly looked at Sam with a confused look on his face then back to Raya who spoke “Sam, the phone’s for you.” 
She held out the phone to Sam who took it and spoke to the receiver “Who is this?”
He heard a male voice on the line speak “Hello Sam, perhaps we’ll meet.” 
Sam again asked “Who is this?”
The male voice spoke “Someone who cares. A word of warning, you be careful of the wolves, their wild animals that aren’t to be trusted.”
The caller abruptly hung up and Sam handed the phone to Raya. 
Michael asked “Sam who was that anyway?”
Sam spoke “He didn’t give me a name.” 
He noticed Michael looking at him and added “Just some fucking shitty druggie bum wanting to scare me about the damned druggies hanging around here, Hmph.” 
Raya exclaimed “Sam, watch your language!” 
Tina added “I don’t think they’ll hang around here due to finding Timothy Jones’ body.”
Michael sighed and left the kitchen. Sam went to sit down at the table and petted Hocus who was rubbing his face against Sam’s face. 
He heard Tina asked Jojo “Can we go to the barn now?”
Sam looked to see Raya speak to Jojo in Romanian, and both Jojo with Tina left the kitchen. 
He watched as Raya went to put the dishes in the dishwasher while humming. 
Sam stood up but Raya stopped him by saying “I want to talk to you, Sam.” 
Sam sat down and watched Raya finish loading the dishwasher. She went to sit at the table as the dishwasher hummed washing the dishes. 
“All right I’ll tell you what you want to know” she said and added “Sam that was the new Pack Leader on the phone.” 
She saw Sam’s eyes widen with shock and added “He was warning you because of your heritage and the fact that you’re a minor, not old enough to cause trouble yet.” 
Sam asked “New pack leader? What happened to the former leader?”
Raya replied “The former leader was” she paused as the doorbell rang. 
She yelled “Sam and I will get the door!” 
She gestured to Sam to follow her and he followed through the TV room with an annoyed Grandfather, watching TV and glaring at them. The doorbell rang again. Reaching the door Raya peered through the door hole and muttered something in Romanian. 
Then she opened the door a crack and spoke loud enough for Sam to hear behind her “What can I do for you, Sir?” 
Sam peered behind Raya’s left side to see a tall man with long black hair pulled in a ponytail and tan skin stood above Raya wearing, blue jeans and tight fitting blue crew neck T-shirt. The man’s brown eyes narrowed when he saw Sam peering around Raya. 
Raya again asked “Hello Sir, who are you?”
The man replied “The name is Longbow. I’m here to see Sam Benson.” 
Raya gestured with her left hand to Sam and spoke “This is Sam Benson, something he could do for you?”
Longbow said with his eyes narrowing, which Sam noticed “Nothing, I just want to talk that’s all.” 
Raya exclaimed “Sam stop peering behind me and come out!”
Sam walked around Raya with a glare on his face and stood on the porch with Longbow as the front door shut behind him. 
Before Longbow could talk Sam asked “It was you on the phone.” 
Longbow folded his arms and stood facing Sam and said “Yes it was me-” 
Sam interrupted “Why?”
Longbow answered “Simply as a Leader of the Pack.” 
Sam grumbled out “You’re Pack Leader.” 
Longbow replied “Yes, the new Leader.”
He continued before Sam could talk “Be warned, you’ll be watched and don’t touch guns period” while pointing a finger at Sam then Longbow walked down the steps and changed his form to a grey wolf that ran away into the forest. 
“Don’t touch guns.” Sam echoed with a harrumph.
 Sam walked into the house gently closing the door. Sam walked into the living room and saw Grandfather watching him. 
“Who was that?” Grandfather asked him. 
Sam heard Raya came in the room speaking “Oh no one but a visitor who wanted to talk to Sam that’s all” then she walked to the kitchen.
Sam heard her talking to Jojo while in the kitchen. Grandfather harrumphed and averted his gaze back to the TV. Sam sat at the couch and felt Hocus jump on the couch to sit on his lap purring. He rubbed the cat’s back as Hocus purred. Sam heard whining from Nanook who sat at the couch on her hindquarters eying the cat. 

The front door opened and Tina came in with Michael. Sam seeing them got up moving Hocus from his lap, from the couch and went to the sun room. 
Sam gasped out loud “There’s a woman carrying flowers walking towards the gravesites.” 
Michael and Tina went to join him and stood watching the woman laid flowers of roses on the gravesites. Michael frowned seeing her clothes for they reminded him of the Pack Leader. Then she looked up and stared as if knowing she was being watched staring straight at them. 
Sam put his hand on the door to outside the sun room when Grandfather demanded “Where you going, Sam?”
“Just to see this woman, outside” Sam told him. 
Grandfather switched the TV off with the remote and swiveled the chair to face the Trio. 
Tina exclaimed “Oh! She’s coming here!”
The Trio went to the living room as the woman reached the sun room door and opened it. She walked inside and stood staring at the Trio with narrowed eyed looks making them uncomfortable before walking into the living room towards Grandfather to stand near him.
Grandfather spoke “Well, Brittany Morgan, long time I’ve seen you.”
He heard gasps from the Trio who were staring at her from the living room doorway.
Brittany Morgan spoke “Yes it’s been a long time I’ve been seen.”
Grandfather noticing the Trio, changed languages to a foreign language speaking “Was that you who was responsible for what happened to Claire?”
Brittany replied in the language “Yes.” 
She stood facing Grandfather in her black sweat pants with black shoes and a white tank top on her with her black sweatshirt wrapped around her waist. Her black hair was pulled in a ponytail and there was a bit of a scar on her left cheek.
Grandfather spoke knowing that the Trio wouldn’t understand his words “Who was Claire really?”
Brittany replied “One of us, who was told not to join herself with a Human.” 
Grandfather frowned and added “It figures about what happened to Claire. She’s currently locked up in an asylum. Don’t tell the kids that.” 
Brittany bristled who spoke “I was in an asylum when I had my son, fathered by Coyote.” 
Grandfather switched languages spoke in English “Sam, come here.” 
He gestured with his right hand to Sam who walked from the sun room to the living room. He stood watching Brittany with a confused look on his face. 
“Sam” Grandfather spoke “This is your biological Mother, Brittany Morgan. I believe you already know who your Father is.” 
Sam, as Michael and Tina gasped, said regaining his composure “Coyote Wilson is my father.” 
Grandfather answered “Yes, that’s true; your adoptive parents told you of your father did them?”
Sam noticed Brittany staring at him intensely said to her “Yes they mentioned my Father. Why did you give me up?”
Brittany with venom in her voice replied “I wasn’t given a choice.” 
She noticed Grandfather glaring at her and added “They accused me of starvation while I was carrying you.”
“Oh” said Sam. 
At that moment Grandfather ordered “Michael. Tina. Go help Jojo with her Mother in the kitchen will you?”
Michael sighed and grabbed Tina by the arms; together the two went into the kitchen. 
Grandfather asked “What happened to Coyote Wilson?’
Sam answered “I had a dream that Brittany” while noticing an intense look on Brittany’s face added “Mother attacked him with a knife-“
Brittany finished for him “And threw him in the river over a bridge-”
Grandfather interrupted her “Yet he survived did he?’
Brittany spoke “The attack was a warning, for him to leave the state. He refused to listen to me when I told Coyote to leave Connecticut” she paused. 
Grandfather spoke “Continue” as Sam stood next to her. 
Brittany continued while looking at Sam “I told him I couldn’t protect him from the others wanting to harm him. Coyote brushed my talk aside thinking the curse was over but I proved it by revealing my wolf form to him. Coyote told me that my people couldn’t harm him. I had to prove of his stupidity by attacking him. That was the last I’ve seen of him.”
Grandfather spoke firmly “He survived.” 
Brittany replied “Yes, there’s a story that there’s a hunter matching Coyote’s description around these parts, killing wolves.” 
Grandfather asked “And when was that?”
Brittany replied while looking at Sam “The story started the moment Coyote disappeared, which was about thirteen years ago.” 
Then the doorbell rang. 
Grandfather spoke “Brittany, go with Sam to the kitchen then” as Jojo came out of the kitchen with a questioning look on her face.
Brittany and Sam left to the kitchen as Grandfather ordered from his seat on the armchair “Jojo, answer the door will you?”
He watched as Jojo left the room. 
As the doorbell rang again, Jojo opened the door to her surprise to see a State Trooper standing there. 
The State Trooper spoke “Is George Patricoly around? I’m State Trooper Johnson.” 
Jojo politely spoke “Follow me.” 
She led the State Trooper towards the living room where Grandfather sat in the armchair watching. 
Jojo silently left the two alone, to the kitchen. In the kitchen, Brittany peered out of one of the two windows of the kitchen door watching Grandfather speaking to the State Trooper. 
Tina spoke peering out another window of the kitchen door “Ugh, it’s that creepy State Trooper with that weird look in his eyes.” 
Raya spoke from the kitchen stove “It’s not nice to judge people creepy by the looks in their eyes.” 
Tina protested “He does seem creepy-” 
Brittany interrupted “That State Trooper has killed wolves before according to witnesses among the pack.” 
Michael sat down at the kitchen table as Sam asked “What are you talking about?”
Brittany snarled out “I’ve seen this fool kill some renegade wolves.” 
At that moment Raya cleared her throat and Brittany continued “The others have seen him do the same to other wolves captured.” 
Michael asked “Who is he really?”
Brittany looked at him with muscular arms folded and spoke “Appears to be someone who has an agenda against wolves.” 
Then she went to the kitchen window and stood looking out the window. Sam stood next to her and looked to see a line of wolves of several shades of black, white and gray standing at the outskirts of the forest.
“What’s going on?” he whispered to his Mother.
Brittany sighed and whispered back “I don’t know.”
Michael exclaimed besides the two “Hey! There are wolves standing outside!”
Jojo and Tina looked to see the wolves turn around and disappear into the forest.
Michael asked “What brought them out?” 
Grandfather came into the kitchen limping with one hand on his cane with State Trooper Johnson following behind him. 
“Raya Ioniel” Grandfather spoke “this is State Trooper Johnson.”
Raya wiped her hands on the dish cloth from a pocket of her flowered dress and held out her hand to the State Trooper who shook hands with her. 
Grandfather pointed to the Trio with Jojo and Brittany introducing each person. 
Johnson interrupted before Grandfather could introduce Brittany by speaking “Ah the famous, Brittany Morgan. You look different from your pictures.”
Brittany kept her arms folded and nodded her head in greeting to Johnson. 
Grandfather added “State Trooper Johnson is here to make sure nothing funny happens around here if you know what I mean.” 
Raya frowned but kept her mouth shut as Grandfather and Johnson left the kitchen. Brittany gestured to Sam to follow her out of the kitchen. Sam got up and followed her out of the kitchen towards the sun room. They both heard the front door bang close as they both went outside towards the graves. 
Sam broke the silence by saying “I heard what happened to Mark” as he noticed her stiffen. 
Sam continued “Sorry I brought that up. What happened to Luke?”
Brittany replied “Luke. I haven’t seen him in awhile.” 
“Oh” said Sam who frowned. 
Brittany spoke “Come” and Sam followed her into the forest.
In the forest they walked in silence till they reached a small hill with a tree growing out of it. Sam gasped as Brittany pulled the ivies from the sides of the hill revealing a door. 
“My cabin” She said as she pulled out a set of keys and unlocked the door. 
Sam walked inside to see the cabin and looked around. He blinked his eyes as Brittany turned on the lights of the cabin with a switch. He noticed a couch facing the door on one wall with the fireplace besides it, went to the couch. There was a door next to it and a loft with a metal ladder on the other side of the room. 
Brittany noticing his interest spoke “You were conceived there on that couch” as she closed the door.
She stood and watched as Sam wandered around the cabin looking around. Then they heard a knock on the door. Brittany went to the door and opened it a crack. Sam sat on the arm of the couch facing the door. 
Brittany stared at Longbow standing behind the door facing her. 
Longbow spoke in a foreign language “Why did you bring him here?”
Brittany instead of answering pushed the door as if attempting to slam it in Longbow’s face that easily blocked the door with his hand. He pushed the door open wider with his hand and walked inside. 
Brittany walked towards the fireplace as Longbow spoke again in the language “As your Pack Leader, don’t turn your back on me.” 
Brittany replied in the foreign language “He’s my son.”
Longbow continued speaking in the foreign language “I don’t appreciate you bringing Sam here.” 
Brittany spoke in the language “Sam is still my son.” 
Longbow glared and advanced towards Brittany with a feral gleam in his eyes speaking “Why haven’t you taken another male as a mate?”
Brittany answered “I don’t want to” as Longbow reached her and gripped her shoulders. 
Out of the corners of his eyes, Longbow saw Sam stand up with a scowl on his face. 
Longbow spoke in English “I’m claiming your Mother, as my mate, any objections?”
Sam harrumphed and kept his mouth shut as Brittany spoke in English “Claiming me for what? I already been claimed by-“
Longbow finished by saying in English “By a Human, hmm?”
Brittany backed one foot back but Longbow kept his grip on her shoulders and lowered his head to her head. 
He whispered to her “Poor Coyote, doesn’t know what’s he’s missing.” 
Longbow felt Brittany jerk as he plopped his hands on her cheeks and lowered his face some more till his lips touched Brittany’s closed mouth and kissed her fully on the lips despite Sam heard growling noises behind them. 

Chapter twenty nine

Elsewhere in another part of the State of Connecticut, during the night, a man was lying on a medical bed asleep with bars around the bed wearing a hospital gown. He jerked his eyes open and with wild feral looks on his face while feeling cloth restraints on his muscular arms as he sat up. There was a shock of long blonde hair that fell around his face bare of a mustache and beard. The man then with great strength from a muscular physique easily ripped the cloth bonds around his arms and stood up growling. He stood in a hospital gown while looking around the room. Light of the moon shined from a window as monitors beeped from the four beds in the room. The man felt objects on his arms with wires attached to the monitors. He zealously tore them off as a small alarm went off. The man stood as a door to the room opened and a woman, a nurse came in the room. 
“Oh, you’re out of your coma” she said as she went to a phone by the side of the room and dialed a number. 
The man stood sneering as he watched her talk on the phone “I just thought I’ll let you know that he’s awake from the coma.” 
She paused and continued “Of course, I’ll let you know of-“
She cut herself off when the man stalked towards her with a wild look on his face growling. 
She spoke again “I think I have to go now.” 
Then she hung up the phone and darted towards the door as the man grabbed her from behind. 
The woman spoke “Please let me go.” 
The man glared at her while noticing the panic in her voice. He pushed her aside from the door and grabbed the handle of the door and twisted it opening the door. Then the man abruptly turned around as the woman attacked him with a syringe in hand. She groaned as he grabbed her wrist of her hand, holding the syringe, twisting the wrist, that the wrist brought pain to the woman. The woman stared at the man’s angry feral gaze as he took the syringe and stabbed the woman with it on her shoulder. The woman groaned again as she felt the drug take effect then the man let her go. He walked towards the door and opened it. Outside was a hallway where another nurse, a male stood with a syringe in his hand. 
The male nurse spoke “Go back to your bed.” 
The man stood as if calculating the male nurse then stalked towards him with a feral look in his eyes and face. His lip curled up in a sneering growl. The nurse stared at the man and dropped the syringe and ran down the hallway. The nurse as he ran felt something like a small pain hit him from behind and the nurse fell towards the ground feeling the effects of the drug. The man walked slowly as reached the male nurse he took the syringe from the nurse’s body and kept walking. Doors on his sides stood open as the man heard beeps from monitors beeping away. The man reached the end of the hallway and stood watching a nurse in an office with her back to him. The man seeing an exit sign above a door walked towards it. 
He heard a shout from the female nurse yelling “Hey! You’re not authorized to leave till the doctor checks you out!”
The man felt a hand on his arm and looked at the nurse with a glare of again a feral gleam in his eyes while holding the syringe in his other hand. The nurse stiffened and let go of his arm. She backed away and ran towards the office. The man stood, dropping the syringe, and walked into exit entrance finding it was a stairwell to up and down and entered it slowly going down. Reaching the end of the stairwell down several sets of stairs ending at a door with another exit sign above he put his ear on the door and heard silence. Then he opened the door and stood in the parking lot light illuminated barely with bushes surrounding the entrance with a wide open space next to it with lines and beyond that were a row of trees. The man sniffed the air and smiled to himself then slowly walked shadowing the building. He ducked behind the bushes, when something he recognized to be a car came by with multicolored lights flashing with the words “Wolfville” on it. As he eyed the car through the bushes the man felt something feeling he never felt before. He knelt in the bushes watching as the car came and sat between one of the lines. The flashing stopped and the car went silent. Then a figure came out of the car with a light in hand. The figure crept towards the exit towards the building where the man left. The man edged himself back towards the exit and waited as the figure came forward towards his position with a light sweeping from the area. The figure reached the door and opened it when the man attacked from behind silently pushing the figure on the back towards the doorway. The figure fell towards the ground and rolled to face the man, who hit him with his fists on the face. Then the man shined the light, the figure, dropped to see a man with gray in his hair with an old look on his face. His clothes were of black pants, black shoes, and a black top with items on them. The man proceeded to strip the figure of his clothes and hooked on the items like they were familiar to him. The man sighed and grabbed the light the figure dropped then turned it off. The man noticed a blue string around the old man’s left wrist, taking the string he pulled his long hair back into a messy ponytail. 
He heard a voice coming from one of the boxy items on his waist speaking “Report, Wilson, did you find the patient, over?”
The man walked towards the car and got in then turned the engine on. He saw besides the driver’s seat on the dashboard was a small folded open flat object with words on it. The words were in English which the man recognized. The man’s eyes read the words and then he put a hand to his head and groaned. 
Sighing he pulled the rearview mirror and looked at himself as he again heard the voice coming from the box on his hip speaking “Report, Wilson, did you find the patient, over?”
With a flick of a switch the man turned the box off and it went silent. Then he adjusted the rearview mirror and the side mirrors before he backed the car and drove off into the night.

Brittany lay on the sofa bed, as the moon barely shined its rays through the ivy covered windows, with Longbow besides her. She remembered after Longbow kissed her, Daniel came knocking on the cabin door and came in the cabin with a weird look on his face as he saw the two. Longbow, Brittany remembered to herself, practically ordered Daniel to bring Sam back to the house. 
Sam left the cabin glaring at Longbow saying “Don’t hurt my mother.” 
Longbow spoke “I won’t” then he pulled the sofa apart to show the bed part of the sofa and stood staring at Brittany with a golden gleam in his eyes and spoke again some foreign words that made Brittany move her feet towards him. Brittany closed her eyes remembering what happened next that brought her to be lying on the sofa bed lying next to Longbow he using her for oral sex and refraining from entering her despite her pleas of wanting it. 
She shifted to get up and felt Longbow’s hand on her arm and his voice speaking in his familiar foreign language “Where do you think your going, Brittany?”
She answered in the dialect not looking at Longbow “Just to shower.” 
Longbow spoke opening his eyes to stare at Brittany’s form “I’m not done with you yet.” 
Then Brittany sighed and once again felt Longbow pull her towards him and she knew what was coming next, closed her eyes.

Chapter thirty 

Grandfather Patricoly lay on his bed asleep with the light of dawn peering through the shades of his open windows when his phone rang. He groaned hearing the ringing of the phone. 
Reaching the phone he spoke “George Patricoly speaking.” 
A voice on the line spoke “State Trooper Johnson speaking. The patient you expressed interest in, has woken up and escaped. There’s one problem.” 
Grandfather spoke “What’s the problem?”
He heard the State Trooper’s reply and hung up the phone with a scowl on his face. Then Grandfather lay on the bed staring at the ceiling thinking. He remembered years ago, walking in the snow without a limp carrying some rope in his hand, before he hurt his leg, walking towards the river in the forest. At the river Grandfather stood watching the water flow under the ice till something caught his eyes. He stared with shock to see a man with blonde hair came floating by. Grandfather tied the rope around a tree and himself then threw himself into the waist high water towards the floating man. The ice was cold to the touch and reaching the man, Grandfather pulled him towards himself and with one hand pulled on the rope towards the shore while grunting of effort. At the shore Grandfather panted and then untied the rope from the tree. Grandfather heard the man groan out “Brittany” and hauled the man through the forest towards a busy road. There he laid the man on the ground and waved his arms at the cars who drove pass. 

Grandfather sighed at the memory. He frowned again at learning the man’s identity when his alarm buzzed eight am. Sighing Grandfather got up and got dressed. Then he grabbed his cane and limped outside his room towards the TV room to sit and wait. He didn’t have to wait long, for the Trio came downstairs together. 
Grandfather spoke “Good morning kids.” 
He saw Michael gave a look to Sam, grabbed his sister’s arm and went into the kitchen. 
Sam asked “what’s going on?’
Grandfather replied “Do you know how I got this limp?”
Sam answered “From hurting your leg.” 
Grandfather sighed and spoke “I got this limp from rescuing your Father from an icy river years ago.”
Sam stared with shock on his face and spoke “Uh, what happened to my Father?”
Grandfather replied “The attack that happened to your Father made him enough to be the Hunter who hunted and shot some wolves.” 
Noticing the confused and shocked look on Sam’s face Grandfather continued “Your Father, starting thirteen years ago, hunted with terror for a short time period of a month hunting some wolves who were actually skin walkers that led him to a trap. The trap, I’m unsure of the details put him in a coma on an off. On and off means your Father would wake up for who knows how long then fall back into a coma.”
He paused to let Sam take stock of the words then continued speaking “I received a phone call earlier today about your Father.”
At that moment he was interrupted by the doorbell ringing. 
Grandfather spoke “Sam, get the door will you?”
 Sam walked towards the front door and peered through the door hole. 
He made a sound of disgust and opened the door to face State Trooper Johnson who spoke “Is George Patricoly around?”
Sam spoke with disgust “Follow me” and he led the State Trooper towards the living room where Grandfather sat in his swivel armchair.
State Trooper Johnson spoke “Did you tell him about his Father?”
Grandfather spoke while noticing Sam’s glare “I did but I was going to tell him about what happened last night-”
Sam interrupted “What happened last night?”
State Trooper Johnson gestured with his hand towards Grandfather who spoke “Your Father woke up from his coma again but this time he escaped the facility where he was being held. There was a problem with your Father when he escaped.” 
Noticing Sam looking at him intensively, Grandfather continued “Your Father was acting not human like which is a concern.” 
Sam asked “How not Human like?”
Johnson answered for Grandfather “Cameras in the facility show him growling towards the nurses and attacking them when they tried to restrain him. Another problem was he failed to recognize your Grandfather, his Father who was attacked when your Father escaped.”
Sam gasped out “Grandfather?”
Grandfather spoke “Your Grandfather Douglas Wilson was called to the scene during the night and your Father attacked him. It appears that your Father has suffered from memory loss or he wouldn’t have attacked your Grandfather” while hearing Sam groan.
Johnson spoke “Cameras show that Coyote Wilson drove away in the facility security car which was tracked.”
Grandfather stared at Johnson and asked “Was tracked?”
Johnson put his hat in his hands and spoke “I came here to tell you that the security car was found on a back road in Drakeville, early as four am, with a yet to identified man lying inside it. Apparently the victim stopped the car and Coyote Wilson attacked the victim and stole his car. The victim is in a local hospital in a coma. There’s no identification on the victim so we’re running his picture and prints.”
Sam groaned out “Oh suppose my Father’s coming here?”
Grandfather spoke “It’s possible, but things are different while your Father was in a coma. He may be disoriented, not recognizing things the way they were.” 
Johnson spoke “I have men staking out Douglas’s house here in Port Monaco in case he should try to come by there.” 
Grandfather asked “Is the house the same one that he used to live in or a different one?”
Sam heard Johnson speak “No the house Douglas used to live in was sold to one of the Ioniels, the owner’s Raya Ioniel, which is also being watched discreetly.” 
Grandfather nodded as the front door banged open and Raya came in the room. 
She put her hands on her hips and spoke with annoyance “Why is there an odd car in front of my house?”
Grandfather answered “I assume you know the former owner of the house?”
Raya gasped “You mean that his son’s out of the hospital?”
“Escaped is more like it” said Johnson.
Raya asked “Escaped?”
Her eyes widened as Sam told her the whole story with Grandfather’s approval. 
Raya muttered in Romanian and then said in English “You think the Hunter plans to come here?”
Grandfather nodded his head. 
Raya added “Hence the car in front of my house?”
Johnson nodded his head in agreement.
Raya harrumphed then walked towards the kitchen double doors, which fell open to reveal Michael and Tina falling towards the floor.  
Raya exclaimed “Michael! Tina! It’s not nice to eavesdrop!”
Michael and Tina sheepishly walked into the kitchen with a glaring Raya behind them.
Johnson spoke “Suppose she tells her wolf friends this?”
Sam heard the disgust in Johnson’s voice as Grandfather spoke “It doesn’t matter. This information on Coyote will get out eventually.”
Sam stared at Johnson with a glaring look on his face. 
Grandfather spoke again “Sam, go in the kitchen will you?”
Sam sighed and walked to the kitchen and entered it. 

In the kitchen Michael and Tina who were sitting at the table stared at him as he came in. 
Sam spoke “Just news on my Father.”
He sat down and watched Raya cook breakfast. 
Sam sensed Michael and Tina still staring at him added “Raya do I have to tell them?”
Raya spoke with her back to the Trio facing the stove “Judging by the way they were hanging onto the door it seems that they heard everything.”
Michael spoke “I heard about your Father escaping from a facility and acting wildly.” 
Raya spoke “Not wildly, but revengeful.” 
Tina asked “What are you talking about Raya? What do you mean revengeful?”
Raya continued “Coyote Wilson tried to defeat them by acting like a Human. You heard that they led him to a trap which put him in a coma on and off. His wild behavior suggests that he’s thinking like them.”
Sam groaned out “What about attacking his Father, my Grandfather?”
Raya frowned and answered “That’s interesting, considering that by attacking him, he put his Father into a hospital out of their hands. Believe me, they don’t like hospitals.”
Michael frowned and spoke “That’s weird, what’s with the line of wolves outside, bordering the forest?”
He gestured as Tina and Sam looked out the window to see what Michael saw. 
The Trio heard Raya mutter in Romanian, and spoke in English “They only do that if their worried about something.” 
Sam asked as the wolves disappeared into the forest “They know about my Father?”
Michael answered “It must be what Brittany told us about Johnson.” 
Tina shushed them as Grandfather came in the kitchen with Johnson followed by a streaking Hocus with Nanook chasing him, who jumped onto the table. 
Grandfather spoke “Michael, Tina, please don’t eavesdrop again. I won’t tolerate this.” 
Then he added “Sam, your Father will be found and helped.”
Then he limped out of the kitchen with Johnson who put his hat on his head winking at Sam.
Sam groaned out “Oh fuck it” as he reached to pet a purring Hocus. 
Raya spoke “Watch your language, Sam. It’s not nice to use swear words.” 
Michael ordered “Nanook! Come sit here.” 
Nanook obeyed and sat next to Michael as he rubbed her sides while the dog eyed Hocus. 
Tina spoke “Oh well, when’s breakfast?”
Raya replied “Soon. Go make yourself useful and set the table.”

In the dining room, the Trio set the table in silence and they sat at the table glumly waiting for Raya to finish cooking. Michael felt Nanook nose her snout on his lap and plopped a hand on her head despite it on his leg.
Raya came out of the kitchen to the dining room and spoke to the trio “Breakfast is ready, please tell George and help me with the foods.” 
Sam spoke “I’ll get Grandfather.” 
Then he walked off towards the TV room as Michael and Tina entered the kitchen with Raya and grabbed the food. They came out to see Sam helping Grandfather, sit at the head of the table. The food was eaten in silence. 
Tina broke the silence by speaking “Where’s Jojo?”
Michael spoke sarcastically “Probably with Daniel I bet.” 
Raya answered “Yes, she’s with Daniel and will be here soon to work with the horses in the corral.” 
Tina spoke “Goody, I guess helping her will give me something to do then.” 
The cordless phone next to Grandfather on the table rang. 
With a harrumph, the gang looked at Grandfather answering the phone and spoke “Hello George Patricoly here.” 
The Trio and Raya noticed his eyes narrow and he spoke “Who is this?”
Then he abruptly hung up the phone with a glare on his face. 
He spoke “Some male told me to tell Sam that your Mother is fine.” 
He stared at Sam who spoke “Oh” while feeling Michael kick him in the shin from under the table. 
Sam added “Is the guy I met the yesterday wanting to talk to me.”
Grandfather spoke “Well, what your Mother does isn’t my business but tell the guy to not to call here again, understand?”
Sam nodded and the gang continued eating in silence. Once again the phone rang and Grandfather reached to answer it. 
They watched as his face narrowed in a scowl as he spoke “How many times must I tell you to not call me on this number? Harrumph. The phone’s for you, Sam.”
He passed the phone to Michael who gave it to Sam. 
Sam spoke “Who is this?”
He heard Longbow’s familiar voice on the line speaking “Hello Sam, its Longbow. I thought I’ll let you know that your Mother is doing fine.” 
Sam spoke “Put my Mother on the phone.”
Longbow laughed and spoke “Fine.” 
Sam sighed as he heard his Mother’s gasping voice on the line speaking “Hello Sam, How are you?”
Sam replied “I’m doing fine” as he cut himself off when he saw Grandfather shakes his head while glaring a warning look at him. 
Sam continued “You ok? You sound like you’re gasping.” 
Longbow’s voice came back on the line speaking “Your Mother’s my mate, remember that.” Then the line went dead as Longbow hung up. 
Sam handed the phone back to Michael who handed it to Grandfather who spoke “What did he say?”
Sam felt Michael kick him in the shin and Sam spoke “Just a friend was letting me know that Mother is doing fine.” 
Grandfather spoke “Hmm was it him?”
Sam replied “Yes it was him.” 
The food was eaten in silence. 

Chapter thirty one

Sam wandered outside the back of the house holding onto Nanook’s leash. He felt a feeling of being watched but shook off the feeling. Nanook pulled him through the forests towards the barn. Sam heard humming from the barn. He came out to see Jojo pushing a wheelbarrow full of horse feed came out with a shovel on top of it. 
She stopped humming when she saw Sam and spoke “Good morning, Sam, what brings you out here?”
Sam asked her “What do you know of some guy named Longbow?”
Jojo instead of answering pushed the wheel barrow towards the grassy gated corral and with a shovel put some of the horse feed into a trough as Sam walked towards the fence and stood watching her shovel the horse feed into the trough. Sam heard Nanook growling and looked to see Daniel came walking towards them with a scowl on his face. 
Sam called out “What do you know of some guy named Longbow?”
He noticed a pained expression came onto Daniel’s face and stood staring at Daniel.

“Perhaps he likes her” said Jojo.

Lone Eagle stood with a frown on his face and spoke noticing Sam’s questioningly look “My case was dropped.”
Then he looked at Jojo and Daniel and added “I couldn’t help over hearing the conversation about Longbow.”

Jojo spoke “He’ll know that you told us.”

Sam asked “What’s going on?”
Lone Eagle replied “Sam, please get inside. It’s not safe out now.” 
Nanook at the moment barked and a wolf came from the bushes and sat staring at the four. Sam watched as Lone Eagle, Jojo and Daniel changed forms to wolves that ran away with the lone wolf. 
Sam frowned and thought “Something’s going on” then he pulled Nanook towards the house and went inside.

At Brittany’s cabin, Longbow stood, holding the phone, with a scowl on his face. He saw Brittany sitting on the couch wearing her former Pack Leader uniform, minus the ski mask and hood, watching him. 
Longbow spoke in foreign language “The Hunter has escaped.”
Then he hung up the phone and went outside the cabin with Brittany following him with her ponytail head bowed. The two walked towards a clearing and stood waiting as wolves of all sizes and with colors of white, grey and black came from all directions surrounding the duo.

The wolves abruptly sat down on their haunches facing Longbow who spoke again in wolf language “You all heard of what happened. The Hunter has escaped to hunt again.”
Brittany groaned thinking “Coyote.”

Longbow spoke gesturing to Brittany “This is Brittany Morgan, the mother of the Hunter’s son. The son” he continued despite grumbling among the wolves “is a teenage boy, who cannot harm us. Yet the boy will be watched.” 
One of the wolves changed form which Brittany recognized to be Lone Eagle stood up and spoke “The teenage boy maybe a clue to defeating the Hunter.” 
The other wolves nodded their heads in agreement which Longbow spoke “Several Humans are aware of the boy’s heritage and are watching him as we speak. It is believed that the Humans have the technology to do their watching and they are aware of us. These Humans have been responsible for keeping the Hunter alive.” 
He paused to let the wolves take stock of his words then continued “This time we’ll take down the Hunter should he attempts to harm us. Are you with me?”
He looked around the sea of wolf faces who growled their agreements then he added “Go.” 
Then the wolves disappeared into the bushes as Lone Eagle stood watching the two.

Lone Eagle answered “I have reason to believe that the Hunter would seek Brittany and bring harm to her.”

Brittany spoke “It won’t. The Hunter was put here just to kill off renegades who harm people without the curse passing onto them.” 
Lone Eagle scowled and spoke “Yes I know but I’m worried about your son. What will the Hunter do if he finds out about Sam?”

Brittany echoed questioningly “Ah interesting?”

Brittany’s lip curled in a snarl while speaking “If you threatened Sam harm.”

She walked through the bushes to the house and was walking towards it through a clearing, when a wolf came and blocked her way growling. 
Recognizing the wolf, Brittany grumbled out “Longbow, I hate it when you do that.”
Longbow in wolf form advanced towards her still growling while snapping his jaws. Brittany harrumphed and walked around the wolf, when Longbow changed form and stood in his human form glaring at her, blocking her way. 
Brittany exclaimed “What do you want? You can’t keep me from seeing my son!”

Brittany charged at him who he grabbed her arms, spinning her around and pushed her to a kneel position with her back to him while holding her arms at a painful angle behind her.

She changed her form to Ghost who snapped at Longbow’s wolf form. Longbow in wolf form snapped back and gestured with his head towards the forest. Chapter thirty two
