Sam opened the door and let Michael come inside. Michael, Sam noticed had the same pained look as Jojo, Daniel and Lone Eagle.
Sam asked “How’s Tina?”
Tina came in from the kitchen answered “I’m doing fine, why?”
Sam sighed and walked into the kitchen followed by Michael and Tina. 
In the kitchen he told them “I saw Lone Eagle, Jojo and Daniel had a pained look on their faces like Mike did.” 
Michael replied “Something bad happened” while noticing Sam’s narrowed gaze added “like a death in the family.” 
Tina spoke “Oh I see.” 
Sam sarcastically spoke “Yeah right.” 
Michael sighed and spoke “I can’t say because Pack Leader won’t let me.” 
Sam grumbled out “Pack Leader is Longbow.” 
He noticed Michael stare at him with a weird look added “Longbow revealed himself to me the other day. He warned me that I’ll be watched and told me not to touch guns.”
Tina asked changing the subject “Hey Mike, how does it feel to change? I keep asking Jojo but she keeps clamming up and won’t tell me.” 
Michael answered “I think she doesn’t know how to explain it like I can’t either.” 
Tina stared at him as Sam asked “Can’t, how come?”
Michael sighed as an image of a charging grey wolf came to his minds eye, as he sat down and spoke “It’s impossible to explain the change.” 
Sam sat down next to Michael; spoke “Tina, when you change you’ll be able to know what Mike is talking about.” 
Tina sat next to the boys and spoke “I asked Jojo how old was she when she changed but she won’t tell me, harrumph. I can’t wait for my change to happen. This would be better than getting my period.” 
Both boys groaned out “Tina!”
Michael put his hands on his head and grumbled out “Women’s stuff, don’t need to hear that.”
Tina frowned and was about to talk when Raya came into the kitchen with a sad look on her face. 
Sam asked Raya “What’s wrong?”
She spoke noticing Michael look at her with his eyes golden spoke “Just some bad news that’s all.” 
Michael’s eyes turned back to normal as he asked “You mean like a death in the family?”
Raya replied sighing out “Yes, sort of like that.” 
Tina complained “Mike and Jojo won’t tell me what’s it’s like to change.” 
Michael glared at his sister as Raya answered Tina’s complaint “Believe me, it’s best for you to know for yourself." 
Humming in Romanian she walked to the dishwasher and started pulling out items. 
Tina spoke “Raya I’ll help you then.” 
She got up and went to help Raya put away the dishes in the cupboards as the boys sat at the table watching them. 
Raya spoke “Boys, are you going to sit there watching us, girls?”
Sam and Michael spoke unison “No” and then they both left the kitchen together. 

In the TV room Sam saw Grandfather watching TV with an intense look on his face like he didn’t want to be disturbed wandered the couch to sit. Hocus came and sat on his lap purring away. Sam gave the cat some rubs while Michael went to the TV and saw what Grandfather was watching. He made a face and joined Sam at the couch. 
Sam looked at him as Michael absent mind rubbed his head spoke “Motorbike races on TV, ugh.” 
They sat listening to the TV watching Grandfather watch the TV when a male voice boomed from the TV speaking “This is your local Connecticut news affiliate, reporting a security car from the Wolfville Asylum was found abandoned with a victim of a physical attack. The victim is a young male in his twenties found with no identification or clothes on him. If anyone recognizes him please call the number on the screen.” 
Sam felt Hocus move off, got up to look at the TV. He saw a male wearing a suit standing in front of a truck like vehicle with the words “Wolfville” on it. 
The male spoke “The local Wolfville hospital needs your help identifying a victim.” 
Sam stared as the screen flashed showing a male with brown hair with brown skin and eyes closed apparently lying on a hospital bed with monitors beeping. 
Then the TV flashed toward the newsman who spoke again “The victim, a male, was found inside the truck behind me apparently in the buff. The local Wolfville police are combing the area for clues. The local hospital has already sent for a DNA test but it’ll take awhile for them to identify who the victim is, who’s in a coma. To anyone who recognizes the victim, please call the number on the screen.”
The TV flashed some numbers then flashed back to motorbike racing. 
Sam went to sit down on the couch next to Michael who spoke “Don’t want to be in that guy’s shoes.” 
The TV flicked off and the boys looked at a glaring Grandfather who ordered “Michael, go to the kitchen.” 
Michael groaned out “Oh well” and walked to the kitchen. 
Grandfather and Sam heard the doors slam closed. 
Sam stood up and walked to stand besides Grandfather who whispered “I received a phone call earlier while you were out, from Johnson telling me that your Father’s fingerprints were all over the security car.”
Sam frowned and whispered “You mean my Father attacked that man?”
Grandfather nodded and whispered “I’m sorry but yes.” 
Sam’s face fell as he whispered “Then why would Father take the victim’s car and clothes?”
Grandfather whispered telling Sam “To gather information and to blend in, like a Hunter would when learning about his new world.” 
Sam groaned out in a whisper “What else do you know of my Father?”
Grandfather whispered “Not much, just information that’ll come when it comes.” 
Saying this Grandfather flicked on the TV with a remote and once again Sam saw the intense look on his face went to the couch to sit down. Hocus came by and rubbed his head against Sam’s leg, who bent down to rub the cat’s head. Sam heard a content meow from Hocus and sighed as he sat staring at the fireplace.
He heard Raya come into the room clearing her throat. 
Grandfather turned off the TV as he and Sam looked at her who spoke “Lunch is ready. Sam, please go help George, to the dining room.” 
She turned and entered the kitchen as Sam got up and went to help Grandfather out of the chair that leaned onto him towards the dining room. In the dining room, Sam helped Grandfather sit at the head of the table. The group ate in silence which was shattered by the shrill ringing of the cordless phone next to Grandfather on the table. 
Grandfather answered the phone speaking “Hello, George Patricoly speaking.”
The others continued eating while eavesdropping on Grandfather’s one sided conversation.
“Hmm,” said Grandfather “Yes I know I’m aware of that.” 
He paused and continued “Thank you for informing me.” 
Then he disconnected the phone as Raya asked him “Was that news on Sam’s Father?” 
Grandfather bristled out “Just some sources, seeking information.” 
Raya narrowed her eyes and spoke “Sources?”
Grandfather spoke “Since when are you nosy, Raya?”
Raya answered sputtering in Romanian which Grandfather replied “In English, Raya. I’m not fluent in Romanian and you know that.” 
Raya spoke “I heard the news of a victim needing identification from the loudness of your TV, George.” 
Grandfather spoke “I can’t help it that I’m old, your hearing is one of the things that goes when you get older, kids.” 
Michael, Tina and Sam at that remark groaned together. 
Raya angrily spoke “When are you going to tell them that you discovered my DNA matches them?”
Michael, Tina and Sam gasped out together “What?”
Grandfather replied “Your DNA makes you a relative of Michael and Tina, but I still haven’t proven that your Timothy Jones’ mother.” 
Michael groaned out “Aw man, I took a liking to Jojo.” 
Grandfather spoke to that remark “Yes, you and Jojo are relatives but remains to be determined of whether your cousins or not.” 
Raya spoke “I can assure you that I’m not Timothy Jones’ mother but Georgina is my daughter.” 
Grandfather glared at her, as Raya glared back. 
Tina broke the stand off by saying “How come we have to be the last to hear of this?”
Raya snapped temper rising “You’re not the last to hear of this. There are others who have brought charges against me and my family.” 
She continued before Grandfather could speak “Charges of causing the ability to change into a wolf, charges of witchery, and other charges too. You name it, my family has suffered that.” 
Grandfather spoke in a calm voice “I’m just wondering why.” 
Raya spoke “Because we believe in an old Earthly like religion called Wicca where the Goddess runs supreme and that we were Gypsies from Romania who were treated inappropriately which we came over to the USA for better treatment.” 
“Oh my” said Grandfather who added “I’m sorry I should have asked my sources about this sometime.” 
Raya harrumphed and then grabbed her plate empty of food and stomped into the kitchen. The double doors slammed banging in and out.
Grandfather got up and limped towards the TV room and the trio heard the loudness of the TV go on. 
Sam rubbed his head and muttered out loud “Jeez that went well” then he got up and grabbed his empty plate and walked into the kitchen. 
Michael gestured to Tina and whispered “Raya’s one of us, so ask her.” 
Tina nodded her head to get Michael’s meaning and grabbed her plate empty plate and went into the kitchen with Michael following her and Nanook behind him. 

In the kitchen the trio stood watching Raya open and slams the cupboard doors banging them out of anger. 
Raya pulled open the dishwasher and spoke facing the trio “Put your dishes in here before I’m tempted to break them over George’s head.” 
The trio obeyed then them watching Raya stomp out of the kitchen and followed her outside the front door. Outside the Trio sat in different rocking chairs as Raya walked down the driveway muttering in her Romanian chanting to herself. Soon Raya disappeared out of sight as the trio sat in silence. 
Tina broke the silence by speaking “Well I’m going to the horse corral to find Jojo. I might as well help her with the horses.” 
She got up and walked the direction towards the horse corral. 
Sam turned to Michael who stretched speaking “I need a change of scenery. I might as well go help Tina with Jojo.” 
Then he got up from the porch and jogged off towards the direction where Tina went. 
Sam grumbled out “Where does that leave me?”
He went inside to see Nanook holding her leash in her mouth. She whined to Sam who took the leash and clipped on her collar. Sam opened the door, grabbed a plastic bag as Nanook joyfully bounded out. They proceeded to walk down the lane towards the end of the driveway where the Sam saw once again the yellow police tape lines outlining Claire’s accident site. 
Sam sighed as he let Nanook sniff around the scene then he saw her squat and groaned out “Nanook.” 
He stood waiting as Nanook did her business, which he picked up with the plastic bag and threw the bag with contents, in the large garbage bin, sitting next to the entrance of the driveway.  Sighing Sam pulled Nanook into the forests towards the barn, reaching a clearing Nanook barked as a grey wolf came slinking from the bushes. 
The wolf changed form to reveal Lone Eagle who spoke “Greetings, Sam.” 
Sam returned the greeting sarcastically “Greetings, Lone Eagle.” 
Lone Eagle asked “Over the years as you grew up, you ever feel like being watched from time to time?”
Sam gasped out “How did you know that?”
Lone Eagle replied lowering his voice which Sam strained to hear “Just to tell you, there are Humans aware of us and you who are watching with any means.” 
Sam frowned and was about to speak when Nanook barked again as the bushes rumbled showing Ghost and a grey wolf. Sam gaped at Ghost who changed form to show his Mother standing there as the grey wolf changed form to reveal Longbow. 
Longbow spoke “What nonsense are you telling Sam, Lone Eagle?”
Lone Eagle bowed to Longbow and spoke “Just the truth.” 
Longbow scowled at Lone Eagle who changed into a wolf that slinked away with tail between the legs. 
Longbow spoke “Whatever Lone Eagle told you are nonsense.” 
Sam noticed his Mother roll her eyes at that remark but spoke “What happened to my Father really? Grandfather says-“
Longbow cut him off by speaking harshly “Don’t ask about your Father in my presence again.” 
Brittany spoke staring at Sam “He deserves to know before someone else tells him.”
Longbow growled out “Fine, your Father hunted us with terror, killing most of us.”
Sam spoke “Grandfather says you got him in some kind of a trap.” 
Brittany explained “The trap was corralling him like a horse with a wounded me as bait into a cave. He believed that killing me would end us.” 
Longbow chimed in “He’s wrong, dead wrong.” 
Brittany added ignoring Longbow’s remark, “Well, Humans can’t see in the dark as we can so it was easy to” while noticing Sam’s frown she added “to disable him and he was put into a coma from our ambush.” 
Sam asked “What happened next?”
Brittany answered “He was brought to a truck and abandoned on some back road.”
Sam spoke “Like what happened to that guy on the news.” 
He noticed the surprised look on his Mother’s face continued “The news said a man was attacked and left in a security car to some asylum on some back road in Wolfville.” 
Longbow growled out “It’s the work of the Hunter, reminding us of his existence.” 
Brittany asked “The man on the news, did he not have any clothes or identification on him?”
Sam replied, with eyes narrowing as Nanook whined, “No clothes or identification on him like the news said, happened to my Father didn’t it?” 
Brittany nodded her head and added “Yes. It took his Father, your Grandfather, three years to find him in an asylum and identify him.” 
Sam frowned speaking “Have you been keeping news on my Father?”
Brittany replied to the question “I’ve tried but the Humans, who are aware of us, have been moving him from place to place just to keep him alive.” 
They heard a wolf howl followed by several wolves howl. Sam noticed Longbow narrow his eyes as Brittany sighed. 
Sam asked “What’s going on?”
Longbow spoke “Look up in the sky; it’s going to rain soon, so get inside.” 
Sam looked up to see the dark clouds of the rain come and he looked to see Longbow with Brittany walk into the bushes in their wolf forms. Walking towards the horse corral, he met Michael and Tina walking towards the house. 
Sam told the two “It’s going to rain.”
Michael nodded as Tina looked worried spoke “Weird weather.” 
The rain fell as the trio reached the house with a loud boom of thunder and lightening. Sam had to restrain Nanook who barked wildly as they went to the porch. 
At the porch, Sam spoke “I wonder what really happened to my Father?”
Michael spoke “Scuttlebutt is your Mom got him in a cave and they knocked him out.”
Noticing Sam’s surprised expression on his face, Michael continued “Lone Eagle told me what happened to your Father.” 
Thunder and Lightening boomed again Sam wondered out loud “I wonder where’s my Father went to?”

Chapter thirty three

As the rain fell, a man sat in a car driving through the rain with forests on the side of the roads. He passed by a police car sitting at the side of the road. The police car turned on its sirens and lights and followed the car till the man stopped the car. The police car shined a large light onto the man’s car. In the car the man’s lips curled in a snarl, as his eyes narrowed in a glare as a memory came. In the memory, he was in a dark forest with a gun long as his arm complete with a flashlight taped to it shining the way of where he was going in the darkness. He swept the forest looking for something. He smiled when he saw blood laying on the ground which he followed the trail towards a cave entrance. Reaching the cave entrance he slipped inside. Inside he followed the trail of blood till he saw a white wolf with blood out of its sides and raised the gun to fire. The man groaned remembering what happened next as figures in black came and jumped on his back pushing him down to the ground. The man sighed remembering the fists hitting him that knocked him out. With a snarl the man touched the gun at his right side and was pulling it when he noticed something shiny besides the folded object with words on it, which he stole from the security car. He saw the shiny thing which he recognized to be a police badge. The man growled and pushed the gun back in its holster and picked up the badge as he stared at the road in front of him. The man unlocked the door and waited as he peered through the rearview mirror, he saw a figure leave the police car and waited as the figure came to the window and knocked. 
The man opened the window a crack and waited as the cop spoke with impatience “Your drivers’ license and car vehicle license please.” 
The man rolled the window down some more as the cop shifted in the pouring rain and showed him the badge. 
The cop groaned out seeing the badge “I’m sorry sir, but you were speeding in the rain. I have to give you a ticket anyway.” 
The man pulled the badge away and made a motion of reaching for the dashboard when he pushed on the car door opening it. The car door slammed hard into the cop who fell backwards towards the ground. The man pulled out the gun and aimed behind him at the light besides the car and it shattered putting them in the semi darkness. Then the man closed the door and drove the car away. 
“Soon” he thought, “I’ll find you” as he drove the car in the rain. 
As he drove away two large all black buses with large antennas on top of them, drove up. One stopped and figures ran out while the other bus drove to follow the man’s car. The man drove speeding as the rain stopped and the showed the setting sun in the sky above him. When it was nighttime with the stars out the man abruptly stopped the car seeing a wolf standing in the side of the road. Snarling he pulled out the gun and held it to him as the wolf, he saw, went to jump onto the car hood and sit. The man stared at the wolf that suddenly made a barking sound. The man blinked his eyes to see the wolf turn out to be a dog sitting on the warmth of the hood. The man was about to holster his gun when a vehicle pulled up behind the car. He saw it was a large traveler bus with a large antenna on top of it. The man glared at the dog and turned to watch as a figure got out of the bus and walked towards his car as he held the gun. He flinched as a flashlight shined onto him from the figure outside his car. The figure he saw through the bus headlights was male wearing jeans, sneakers, and a hooded red sweatshirt. The male put the flashlight under his arm, knocked on the window and had a folder in his left hand. The man put the gun away and rolled the window down a bit to let the male push in the folder. Then the man put on the car overhead lights and read the contents of the folder. He held up a headshot picture of a man and compared it to himself by looking in the rearview mirror. With a growling sneer the man opened the car door and stood next to the male who was shorter than him, he saw was in his early twenties. The dog at the moment got up from the car and ran into the forest. 
The male spoke “Come.” 
The man followed the male towards the bus and the door of the bus slid open leading to stairs, to the bus driver. The driver, who sat watching them enter, had red hair pulled back in a thick braid with beard and was wearing a tan uniform. The young male pulled apart some curtains behind the driver and entered with the man following him. Inside to the man’s surprise were on his left all kinds of electronic equipment with monitors on the wall. On his right were booths with maps on the walls with a large map of Connecticut there. In front paces away facing him were a door that led to the back of the bus. The man saw four people young as the male who stared at him with awe in their eyes. He saw two males dressed like the young male but with head pieces on their heads sitting in front of the monitors. The others he growled were females who were dressed like the young male. They were standing behind the two males. The young male cleared his throat and they stopped looking to look at the monitors at the walls. 
The young male spoke to the man “The name is Jack.” 
Then Jack introduced the group by speaking and pointing at each person “The driver’s Olav. This is Jennifer, Liam, Kent, and Kelly.” 
He paused as the man pushed the file towards Jack who took it. Jack went to a booth and pulled out a drawer under the booth and stuffed the file with the other files. Then Jack stood and watched as the man went to the booth and sat down with interest in the monitors. 
Jack spoke “We’re tracking you by satellite, Coyote.”
The man at the sound of the name Coyote jerked to stare at Jack who continued “You’re implanted with a homing device, for your safety.” 
Jack paused seeing the narrowed gaze of the man, Coyote’s eyes who stared at him with a feral look. 
Jennifer, who was standing, swung her long blonde hair out of her face to face Coyote spoke “We’re part of an organization that is aware of the skin walkers and is monitoring them, sometimes by satellite.” 
She paused when she heard a snarling like growl come from Coyote sitting at the booth. 
Jack sat down and reached a hand across the table and spoke “We are aware of what the skin walkers did to you.” 
Jack paused as Coyote stared at him with the same feral gleam in his eyes. 
He continued “Your son is being watched for his safety.” 
Coyote spoke his words for the first time snarling out “Where is he, my son?”
Jack sighed and spoke choosing his words carefully “In Port Monaco.” 
Coyote glared at him and spoke “With those skin walkers!”
Jack trying to calm Coyote said “They haven’t harmed him.” 
Coyote growled out “Yet.” 
Jack was about to speak when Olav from the drivers’ seat spoke out “You should tell him the truth about the skin walkers.”
Jack sighed again and told Coyote “Killing Brittany Morgan” as Coyote growled at the name, Jack continued speaking ignoring the growl “Won’t solve a thing to stop the skin walkers, but your son would be upset about that.” 
Coyote heard Jennifer speak “Your son is aware of his parentage, which is you and Brittany Morgan.” 
Coyote turned to glare at her which Jennifer turned around to face the monitors. 
Coyote demanded “Who told him this?”
Liam spoke from the monitors “His adoptive parents all three of them told him that.” 
Coyote asked with eyes narrowed “Three?”
Liam replied sighing “Yes three, at first were his adoptive parents Alex and Taylor Benson who told him of you, then George Patricoly who he resides with told him of his parentage.” 
Coyote growled as Jack asked “You want something to eat?”
Coyote turned to look at Jack, who reached besides him and opened a small door of a box in the counter labeled “Hunter Food” which cold air hissed out. Coyote watched as Jack pulled out a box and got up towards a large box next to the maps. He watched as Jack pressed a switch and the box opened a large door sideways. 
“A Microwave” Coyote spoke out loud.
Jack replied “Yes.” 
He opened the box and put the tray into the microwave and pressed some dial switches. The microwave hummed cooking the food. Coyote sighed as he felt the feeling of hunger wash over him. He saw Jack watching him as the food cooked in the microwave. Coyote watched the microwave as he heard a ding sound and the humming stopped. Jack opened the microwave door and took the tray with food to place it in front of Coyote. Coyote stared at the food as Jack handed him some silverware and sat across from him. Coyote slowly ate the food as Jack sat watching him. 
Coyote felt his familiar strength returning as he ate and he watched as Jack spoke “There’s something we of this group would like you to do.”
He didn't comment a response only listened to Jack's words as he ate the food. 

Chapter thirty five

Michael and Sam sat on the porch with Grandfather behind them in the rocking chair. It was barely noon and the heat of the day was soon being felt. Nanook sat at Michael’s feet panting away. A car came in the driveway as the teens and Grandfather saw a man got out. The man they saw had on black pants, with a black t-shirt top despite the upcoming heat; the man didn’t appear to be sweating. He had two hand guns in identical holsters on his sides near his upper muscular arms and his long blonde sun colored hair was pulled back. 
“Creepy” said Michael when he saw the man look at them with narrowed blue eyes. 
Grandfather ordered, “Michael, take Nanook and leave.” 
Michael sighing got up and clipped on the leash on Nanook’s collar. They both went down the steps and walked towards the barn without a glance. The man reached the steps and stood in front of Sam looking at him with an interested look in his face. 
Sam heard Grandfather speak “Sam, meet your Father, Coyote Wilson.” 
Sam gasped as the man nodded indicating that he was Coyote Wilson himself. 

Michael walked towards the barn to meet Jojo at the corral shoveling horse feed from a wheelbarrow assisted by Brittany as Tina sat on the fence.
Michael spoke “Some creepy guy came and Grandfather told me to leave.” 
Brittany stopped shoveling to speak “What did this guy look like?”
Michael answered giving the guy’s description which made Brittany gasp out “What!”
She dropped the shovel and darted towards the house through the bushes as Jojo changed form to a grey wolf that howled as Tina jumped down from the fence.
Michael heard the howling message say “Hunter’s here! Repeat, Hunter’s here!”

Brittany stomped towards the house, went around a tree, and was met by Longbow who blocked her way. 
She angrily spoke “Get out of my way.” 
Longbow asked “Are you challenging me?”
Brittany replied “The Father of my son is here and-“
Longbow interrupted “You’re not meeting him when you’re angry.” 
Brittany walked around him but Longbow grabbed her which made her angrier as her eyes turned golden and she growled out wolf language while changing her form, “Let me go, you fool.” 
Longbow still held her while changing his form too and spoke in wolf language “Your meeting with him will be on our terms, when you are calmer.”

Raya hummed to herself in the kitchen standing over a pot of spaghetti while in the kitchen. She heard the kitchen double doors slam, turned around and gasped as she saw the man standing with Grandfather and Sam. 
Grandfather spoke “This is my cook, Raya Ioniel.” 
Raya stood watching the man stare at her with a bit of a glaring look. 
Grandfather continued “Raya, this is Coyote Wilson, Sam’s Father.” 
Raya stiffened hearing the name and kept her composure and spoke “Hello, Mister Wilson.”
Coyote spoke eyes narrowing “Please call me Coyote.” 
Raya nodded and then turned towards the stove as Grandfather ordered, “See that there’s enough for our guest here.” 
Raya replied “Will do.” 
Without turning around to face Grandfather as she heard the kitchen doors open and close slamming with a bang. 
Raya turned to look at the window and could see a line of wolves standing outlining the forest line. Raya sighed and muttered a chant in Romanian then went back to cooking the spaghetti as Tina came in the kitchen with a confused look on her face. 
Tina asked Raya “Coyote Wilson? Did you meet him yet? He’s out there in the living room talking to Grandfather with Sam.” 
“Yes I’ve met him” Raya answered and continued “Apparently he’s staying for lunch.” 
Tina frowned and went to the kitchen table to sit down as Hocus jumped on the table. Tina reached a hand and the cat went to the hand and rubbed his full body on the hand. Tina sighed and then the double doors open to reveal Jojo coming in the kitchen with a frown on her face. She spoke in Romanian “Mother, there’s trouble out there. I’ve met the Hunter.” 
Raya still facing the stove spoke in English “What troubles is that and in English please?” 
Jojo replied in English with Tina watching her “Trouble is the Hunter’s here, and Pack Leader, Longbow, had to restrain an angry Brittany.”
Tina gasped out “Sam’s Mother mad?”
Raya spoke “Apparently she has some anger towards Coyote.” 
Jojo added “Longbow has claimed Brittany as his mate which won’t go well with Coyote.” 
Tina chimed in asking “Mate? “
Jojo spoke ignoring Tina’s comment “It appears from the way Longbow restrained Brittany that he has some sort of hold on her.”
Raya frowned and spoke “Well the spaghetti is ready, so please tell the men and Michael.” 
At that moment they heard Nanook barking as Michael came in the kitchen speaking “Raya when’s lunch? Plus did you meet Sam’s Father Coyote Wilson?”
Raya spoke “Yes I’ve met Coyote and he’s staying for lunch. The spaghetti is ready, so alert the others will you? Girls, help me load the food in the dining room please.” 
Michael groaned and left the kitchen with Nanook trailing behind him. 

In the dining room the group chewed their food in silence. Coyote sat facing Grandfather at the other end of the table with Sam sitting at his right on the bench. 
Grandfather between bites broke the silence by saying “So Sam?”
Raya, Jojo, Tina and Michael looked up from eating to see Grandfather looking at Sam who was staring at his food lost in thought while chewing away. Michael elbowed Sam in the sides and Sam looked up as Michael gestured to Grandfather. Sam gulped his food and took a drink from a cup set in front of him.
“Yes Grandfather, uh George?” Sam asked while noticing his Father’s narrowed gaze. 
Grandfather spoke “Sam, please still call me Grandfather.” 
As Grandfather noticed Coyote staring at him, Sam spoke “Ok if you say so. So Dad how long is you staying in town?”
Coyote noticing Sam watching him, finished chewing a bite of food, took a drink of water and cleared his throat then he spoke “That remains to be determined, Sam.”
The phone rang shrilling its ringing from the wall next to the kitchen double doors. 
Raya got up and went to the phone and handed the cordless to Grandfather who spoke “George Patricoly here.” 
Grandfather paused and spoke “Ah, Pack Leader I presume?”
Grandfather saw Coyote’s eyes narrow in a glare as the others stared at Grandfather with a range of emotions on their faces. 
He heard the voice of Pack Leader speaking “Hmph, your getting wise aren’t you? Anyhow put the Hunter on the phone.” 
Grandfather replied “There’s no one here by that name.” 
Pack Leader’s voice speaking again sounding a little annoyed “The Hunter has a name, and it’s Coyote Wilson. Put him on the phone.” 
Grandfather sighed and asked “If I don’t? What will you do?”
Pack Leader answered “Brittany Morgan, what do you think I’ll do to her? She was Pack Leader, from the top to the bottom now. Put the Hunter on the phone.”
Grandfather’s eyes narrowed and spoke to the group “It appears Pack Leader wants to speak to you, Coyote.”
He passed the phone to Michael who passed it to Sam and handed the phone to Coyote who took the phone speaking “Hello?”
Sam sat watching a range of emotions on his Father’s face and saw his eyes narrow. Then Coyote held the phone from his ear and held it up with a questioning look on his face as a sound of moaning came from the phone was heard by all.
Coyote asked “How do you disconnect this phone?”
Then Coyote heard a male voice speak from the phone “Don’t disconnect yet.” 
Coyote put the phone to his ear and snarled out “Longbow.” 
Sam gasped to Michael whispering “I’ve never told him, your Pack Leader’s name.” 
Michael widens his eyes in shock as they both sat listening on Coyote’s conversation on the phone.
Coyote spoke “I recognized that sniveling voice of yours. What game are you playing as Pack Leader?” 
Coyote noticing the others watching and listening to his talk spoke “There are others watching and listening.” 
He paused and pulled the phone from his ear and spoke “Longbow wants to talk to you, George.” 
He handed the phone to Sam who passed it to Michael and handed the cordless to Grandfather who put the phone on his ear. 
Grandfather spoke “What do you want now?”
He heard the voice of Pack Leader, Longbow speaking “I’ll be careful if I were you. You wouldn’t want anything bad to happen now would you?”
Grandfather opened his mouth to retort a remark when he heard the dial tone and then pulled the phone from his ear while speaking “He hung up.” 
Then Grandfather put the phone on the table and he picked up his fork and resumed eating. The group copied him in silence. 

Longbow scowled as he held the cell phone and put it in the pocket of his jeans as he stood outside Brittany’s cabin. He went inside and heard the shower running from the bathroom in one corner of the cabin. Longbow stood watching the closed door with a smirk on his face. He walked towards the door to the bathroom and heard the shower turned off. Then he leaned next to the bathroom door and waited as Brittany came out dressed in a blue bathrobe that bared her lower legs and with her black hair wet. 
Longbow spoke in foreign language “You look sexy.” 
Brittany startled, saw him, groaned then pulled the bathrobe closer together by tightly tying the sash and she went to the ladder leading to the loft. 
She heard Longbow speak again in the language “Are you challenging me?” 
Brittany replied in the foreign language, yawning not meeting his eyes “No, I need to sleep and be rested before you let me meet Coyote.” 
Longbow spoke “Coyote? Interesting use of first name considering around here, he’s known as the Hunter.” 
Brittany sighed and raised a foot on the first rung when she heard Longbow speak again “Are you challenging me?”
Brittany spoke angrily “What is your problem? You’ve been using me as your love slave since the moment you defeated me and took leadership.” 
Longbow repeated his question speaking firmly “Are you challenging me?” 
Brittany glared at him and grabbed the ladder and started climbing up when she felt Longbow’s hands on her legs and she kicked at him. Longbow blocked both kicks with his arms and pulled her off the ladder as she struggled yelling “Leave me alone! I’m not your love slave anymore!”
She swung her fists at Longbow who easily blocked the arms and he twisted her till she was pined between him and the ladder with both arms behind her. 
Brittany struggled while hearing Longbow calmly speaking in her left ear “Admit it. You love him.” 
She felt one of his hands snake towards the sash holding the bathrobe and snarled out angrily “That’s not going to solve a thing.” 
She heard Longbow laugh and said “Perhaps I shouldn’t let you see him.” 
Brittany groaned as she felt the sash come undone and sighed as she stared at the ceiling thinking “Oh Coyote help me” as the bathrobe came off from her. 

Chapter thirty four

Coyote Wilson walked in the forest towards Brittany’s cabin. He stiffened when he heard howls of wolves from the forest around him. Growling to himself he walked till he reached Brittany’s cabin. At the cabin he knocked on the door and stood sideways from the door with arms at his sides and his hands were fisted. The door opened showing Brittany who was dressed in a blue bathrobe, stood staring at him as Coyote stared back at her.  
“Help me” her brown eyes appeared to say as Coyote spoke “Brittany.” 
Then abruptly the door opened wider showing a man in his late thirties, stood besides Brittany with a scowl on his face.
Coyote snarled out speaking with recognition in his voice “Longbow.”
Longbow spoke something to Brittany’s ear in which Coyote heard was in foreign language and she groaned as she backed up and he stepped out closing the door. The men stood glaring at each other with Coyote towering over Longbow by a head. 
Coyote noticed the triumphant look in Longbow’s eyes broke the silence by saying “How’s your family and brother, Longbow?”
The triumphant look in Longbow’s eyes died as Longbow sneered out “Are you threatening me?”
Instead of answering Coyote simply walked away from him and Longbow called out “Don’t turn your back to me, Hunter. It isn’t wise.” 
Coyote stopped and turned and spoke “Perhaps you’re not smart enough to find a better choice in mates.”
Longbow charged at Coyote who easily grabbed his arms and knocked Longbow onto the ground. 
Longbow lay glaring up at Coyote who spoke “I over stayed my welcome.” 
Then Coyote walked away as the bushes around them rumbled showing snarling wolves coming out who snapped at Coyote’s feet as he walked by them. Longbow got up and dusted himself and went inside the cabin. 

Inside Brittany lay curled on the couch bed asleep. She felt someone sit on the bed and stroke her hair. 
“Coyote” she spoke out loud and opened her eyes to see a glaring Longbow sitting next to her on the couch. 
Sighing Brittany closed her eyes and went back to sleep when she heard Longbow speak in a foreign language “Are you challenging me?”  
Brittany groaned out with her eyes closed in the same language “No.”
She felt the sash of the bathrobe open and she thought “Please, have Coyote or someone help me get out of this situation.” 

Coyote walked through the forest passing bushes and trees when he felt something wrong. He reached for his gun in the holster in his left arm and felt it gone. He looked around and turned around to see a young man with spike perm hair with ripped jeans and a ripped blue T-shirt standing there a few footfalls away holding his gun and it was pointed at Coyote. 
Coyote growled and spoke “The gun isn’t loaded.” 
The young man stood still aiming the gun at Coyote who held out a hand and spoke again “Give me the gun please.” 
Coyote heard rustling in the bushes off his left and saw a man with long black hair with a touch of grey in it, wearing tan pants with beaded trim and an identical top with also beaded trim.  The older man noticing recognition in Coyote’s eyes as Coyote saw him spoke “Daniel, give the man his gun back.” 
Coyote looked at the young man, Daniel and heard the older man speak again “Daniel! I said give the man his gun back now.”
Daniel sighed and handed the gun back to Coyote who holstered it. Coyote watched as Daniel turned and ran into the forest. Lone Eagle stood watching Coyote who turned his head to stare at him. 
Lone Eagle spoke “The name is-“
Coyote interrupted him by saying “I know who you are, I recognized you.” 
Lone Eagle spoke “I go by the name Lone Eagle now.” 
At that moment they heard a wolf howl followed by several wolves howling. 
Coyote saw a pained expression come on Lone Eagle’s face and then Lone Eagle spoke with pain in his voice “It’s best for you to get indoors now.” 
Then he turned and walked further into the forest. Coyote turned and walked towards the house. 

At the house he met Michael coming out. They both stood and stared then Michael gave a sigh as he walked away into the forest with Coyote watching him, and then Coyote went in the house. In the house Nanook came bouncing up to him which Coyote reached a hand and gave her head a rub then Nanook went to sit by Grandfather who was sitting in an arm chair watching him. Grandfather flicked the remote and the TV went off.
Coyote noticed Sam sitting on the couch frowning who asked “You saw my Mother?”
Coyote replied “I did with that fool Longbow.” 
Sam grimace hearing the venom in his father’s voice, and Grandfather replied “From what Sam tells me, Longbow is using her as his mate.” 
He frowned as Coyote glared at him. 
Coyote spoke “He’s using her psychologically, torturing her.”
Grandfather added “She according to this Longbow on the phone was Pack Leader.” 
Coyote agreed speaking “He’s right, she was Pack Leader.” 
Sam gasped out “Mike said that that Pack Leader’s identity was hidden from him.”
Coyote spoke sounding a little annoyed “Appears that there’s some battle for power in the skin walker pack hence the hidden identity.”
Noticing Sam’s confused look, Coyote continued “There seems to be some psychological battle between two Pack Leaders. There are several skin walkers I’ve seen are supporting Brittany and others supporting this fool, Longbow.” 
Grandfather remarked “Hence Longbow using her for mating issues.” 
Coyote spoke “He won’t stop till she surrenders to him and those supporting her.” 
Sam asked “What will happen now?”
Instead of answering Coyote pulled the gun from his left holster and pulled out a long finger object from his pocket and put it in the gun. Sam grimaced as he heard the gun cocking noise and put the gun back in its holster. Then he watched as his father did the same with the other gun on his right side. Sam gulped out a groan and frowned as he saw Coyote look at him. 
Coyote asked “Longbow showed himself to you?”
Sam nodded and answered “He also told me not to touch guns.” 
Grandfather chimed in “I have some people who are watching the situation in case it gets violent.” 
Coyote spoke “Good.” 
Then he went to the edge of the living room bordering the sun room to look out the window. Coyote heard the TV flicked on, heard his son come to stand next to him and felt a hand on his right arm from Sam. Coyote looked at him.
“Dad” Sam said “Will you help Mother?”
Coyote looked away to look out the window and spoke “It remains to be seen.” 

Outside Michael walked into the forest and changed form to a wolf. He was met by two other wolves which he recognized to be Jojo and Daniel. The three wolves walked towards a clearing next to Brittany’s cabin where other wolves were sitting around on their haunches talking away in their wolf language. Michael heard smattering of conversations focusing on Brittany and Longbow. He sat facing the cabin door as Longbow came out slamming the door. The wolves abruptly went silent. 
Longbow had anger on his face spoke in wolf language “You saw what the Hunter did.” 
Michael felt confusion roll inside him as Longbow continued speaking “The Hunter threatened my family with harm with his words.” 
Michael sensed anger from some of the wolves but felt disgust at the moment as Longbow added “Family is important and I believe the Hunter must be taken care of and his offspring.” 
The door to the cabin opened and Brittany came out yelling “You promised that you’ll leave my son alone!”
Longbow turned to glare at her and spoke “Traitor.” 
Michael saw her stare at Longbow and then she raised her right hand and brought it across Longbow’s face slapped him. His head of long hair in a braid jerked to the side as she brought her hand away again from the slap. Longbow held a hand up as he sensed the other wolves growling. Michael saw some of the wolves were off their haunches and were baring their teeth apparently at Brittany in anger. 
Longbow asked “Tell me something woman, how it feels to be a traitor?” 
Brittany gasped at him and yelled “You used me, you bastard!”
Longbow answered “So what? Go inside or I’ll have you escorted.” 
Michael watched as Longbow gestured with his hand and two of the wolves changed forms to be men about Longbow’s age with tan skin, short black styled hair and identical outfits as Longbow was wearing, jeans, black sneakers and a crew neck blue T-shirt who advanced on Brittany who growled eyes flaring golden yellow color. She charged at Longbow who ducked in a leg split as the two men jumped over him and attacked Brittany. Brittany used her fists and legs to fight off the men but Michael noticed the men were stronger subdued her. 
They grabbed both of her arms as Michael heard Longbow say as they hauled a struggling Brittany inside the cabin “Watch her, see that she doesn’t escape and tie her up.” 
Michael sensed Jojo and Daniel backing away from himself along with the other wolves as Longbow came walking up to him. 
Longbow ordered “Change your form, Michael, now!”
The words felt like a command that Michael was compelled to obey which he changed his form to one of a Human and stood frowning staring at Longbow not meeting his brown eyes. 
Longbow stood a head taller than Michael who stared at him and spoke “You’re new aren’t you? Speak now Michael.” 
Michael sighed and responded still not meeting Longbow’s eyes “What do you want me to say?”
Longbow answered “Your loyalty to the Pack, Michael.” 
Michael gulped and stood frowning as Longbow grabbed Michael’s chin and raised his head up to face his face. Michael averted his eyes to look at Longbow’s ear. 
He heard Longbow speak “Be loyal and don’t tell the Hunter about what was said here after all family is important isn’t it?”
Michael groaned recognizing the threat in Longbow’s words as his chin was let go and Longbow spoke “Go.” 
Michael watched as two wolves came forward to change forms to Jojo and Daniel who took his arms and pulled him away from the clearing. Michael let himself be pulled away as he looked over his shoulder, he could hear Longbow talking to the others issuing orders.

Brittany lay growling on the couch bed feeling angry. Her arms were tied to the edges of the couch handles and so were her legs at the other ends. Around her neck was a choke collar as she could see the two men who brought her inside watching her from their positions in the living room. The choke collar Brittany discovered hampered with her changing her form from Human to wolf. Her eyes flared yellow gold as Longbow came inside the cabin. 
He spoke “Leave us. Guard the outside should she try to escape.” 
The two men obeyed and left the cabin closing the door behind them.
Brittany growled at Longbow who stood staring at her then he went to her and whispered in her left ear in foreign language “I’ll free you from the chains but you must submit to my authority if you want your son to live.”
Brittany spat at him and spoke in the same language “Just who do you think you are? Some bastard who wants-“
Longbow interrupted her by speaking “Wants isn’t important, but your submittal for my authority. There are others out there who see you as their Pack Leader and have been refusing to submit to me.”
Brittany didn’t know why but she laughed and felt Longbow put a hand on her neck. 
Her laughter died as he spoke “Perhaps I should squeeze the life out of you and be done with it.” 
Brittany snarled out “But you won’t will you?”
Longbow spoke “Your right, I won’t.” 
Then his hand went to settle on her breast which Brittany glared at him while struggling with her bonds spoke “Get off.” 
Longbow laughed a small laugh and spoke “Oh no, Brittany, I’m not done with you yet.” 
Brittany rolled her eyes sky way to stare at the cabin’s ceiling as she felt Longbow’s hands on her and knew what was coming next. Once he was done, she was crying as he left her free from her bonds in the cabin. 
Brittany heard him speak to the guards outside the cabin with the door open “See that she doesn’t escape.” 
Brittany got up from the couch to see the door close. 
“Coyote” she said “Help me.” 

Chapter thirty five

Michael numbly let Jojo and Daniel pull him through the forest to the house where they let his arms go. 
He walked towards the house and heard Daniel say from behind him “Remember what Pack Leader said, Michael. Family is important.” 
Michael turned to watch the duo walk towards the direction of the barn and disappear in around a tree still walking towards the area. Sighing he walked into the house to be met by Nanook with a leash in her mouth. He grabbed the leash and a plastic bag hanging off a hook next to the door while clicking the leash on Nanook’s collar. He walked outside to let Nanook pull the leash while wandering around the house. Michael sighed again as he saw Coyote came walking towards him from the direction of the driveway lane. 
Longbow’s words “Family is important” echoed in Michael’s mind as he was led by Nanook towards Coyote who stood watching him. 
Coyote growled out as Nanook stopped to sniff his shoes and Michael stared at him not meeting his eyes “Longbow got to you didn’t he by threatening you?”
Instead of answering Michael shrugged as Nanook went to a tree with him following behind her and the dog squatted there. 
Coyote followed the two and stood next to Michael and spoke again “Alright, I understand why you don’t want to talk to me. Its Longbow isn’t it?”
An image of a grey wolf came to Michael’s mind and its teeth were bared growling as the words “Family is important” echoed in his mind. 
Coyote spoke “Your silence says that Longbow got to you and has threatened you with some harm to your family.” 
At that comment Michael looked up and stared at Coyote’s eyes that were narrowed staring back at Michael’s eyes. Then they heard a sound of a wolf howling followed by other sounds of wolves howling. Michael sighed and picked up Nanook’s scat with the plastic bag and pulled the dog towards around the house to the lane with Coyote following behind the two. Still sighing Michael walked down the lane to the end of the driveway towards the dumpster. He threw the bag with contents into the dumpster and then pulled Nanook by leash behind him towards the house. 
Coyote spoke “Interesting, considering your Grandfather asked me to stay for a several days.” 
He heard Michael gasp as he pulled Nanook towards the house and unclipped the leash at the doorway. 
Coyote watched as Nanook obeyed Michael’s command of “Inside now.” 
Michael from the top of the stairs of the porch turned to face Coyote who stood at the bottom of the steps and asked “Just what do you want?”
Coyote spoke “What do I want? Many, many answers to questions but they’ll have to wait.” 
Michael groaned and walked down the steps walking around Coyote when his left arm was grabbed in a vise like grip. Michael looked at Coyote who was staring at him with a weird intense look on his face with his hand gripping his arm. 
“Let me go” Michael said as he heard a wolf howl followed by wolves howling. 
Coyote ordered “Tell Longbow I still haven’t forgotten here.” 
Coyote pointed to his chest at the right side. Michael stared at Coyote questioningly who let go of his arm and walked inside the house slamming the screen door. Michael walked down the steps towards the direction of the barn muttering to self when he came upon several wolves standing in a clearing in front of him. 
“None of my business” Michael said out loud and turned only to be blocked by several wolves that came out of the bushes that he was surrounded by wolves. One of them changed form to Human who Michael recognized to be Lone Eagle who stood staring at Michael. 
Michael demanded “What? I didn’t tell him anything.” 
Lone Eagle answered “Calm down Michael, but he did scare you?”
Michael replied “If you’re talking about the Hunter, no.” 
Lone Eagle spoke “I’m surprised because the Hunter usually scares new ones.” 
Michael frowned as Lone Eagle added “Your newness hasn’t taken time to factor in you being scared of the Hunter.” 
Michael stared and spoke “I’m not afraid of the Hunter.” 
Lone Eagle was about to speak when a new voice spoke “You will be.” 
Michael recognized the voice belonging to Longbow who stood behind a row of wolves. 
“Scatter” Longbow said as the wolves disappeared with Lone Eagle changing form and went away till Michael was alone with Longbow. Michael stared at the ground not meeting Longbow’s eyes or looking at him.
“Come with me” Longbow ordered Michael who followed him towards the horse corral where Longbow stopped at the bushes to watch through it, Jojo and Daniel with Tina stood watching the horses in the corral from standing in front of a fence. They appeared to be talking in hush tones. 
Longbow broke the silence by speaking facing Michael who was watching the Trio hush talk “What did the Hunter say to you?”
Michael relayed what Coyote told him and added “He told me to tell you that he hasn’t forgotten here.” 
Michael pointed to the right side of his chest and heard a growl from Longbow. Michael bravely with a questioning look on his face looked at Longbow whose eyes were golden color glaring at something behind him. 
Longbow’s eyes went back to normal and his eyes looked at Michael with a smile and said “Just something bad that happened years ago. Don’t worry about it.” 
Michael bravely spoke “This will come out will it?”
Longbow snarled “Well, pray it won’t come out.” 
Michael spoke “The Hunter might wind up telling anyway.”
Longbow reached out a hand grabbing Michael by the hair and pulled him towards him and whispered in his left ear “Just hope the Hunter keeps his mouth shut. If I were you, I’ll drop the matter and don’t bother asking the Hunter this.” 
Michael felt himself pushed down towards the ground and heard Longbow walking away.
Groaning Michael picked up and walked towards the horses’ corral where his sister stood talking with Daniel and Jojo. At the corral the three were surprised to see Michael come out of the bushes walking towards them.
Tina asked “Mike, you alright?”
Michael replied “I don’t know.” 
Daniel remarked “He had a conversation with Pack Leader.” 
Michael leaned against the fence and spoke to his sister’s questioning gaze “Don’t ask, Tina.”
Tina pouted and frowned as Michael settled himself against the fence. 
She asked “How come no one tells me anything around here?”
No one answered her question and they stood in silence. 

Longbow stood hidden in the bushes watching the four with his familiar scowl on his face. He heard a twig snap and spun around to face Lone Eagle standing behind him with both his hands up in the air. 
Longbow’s eyes narrowed and he glared at Lone Eagle who pleaded “Sorry about that.” 
Longbow snarled asking “If it wasn’t for your knee you would have challenged me would you?”
Lone Eagle again pleaded with his hands still up “No, old age.” 
Longbow fisted his hands at his sides, stalking towards Lone Eagle and stood in front of the man and said “Don’t pretend this act. You loyalty is to Brittany and not to me.” 
Lone Eagle replied looking at Longbow “So? My loyalty is to myself.” 
Longbow remarked sneering “Loyalty to self? Hah! It’s to Brittany. I’ve heard you acting like her right hand man, giving off her orders when she was Pack Leader.” 
Lone Eagle spoke “Actions must be proven for loyalty to be-“
Longbow interrupted waving a fisted hand at Lone Eagle by speaking “Actions have been proven, Luke Morgan.” 
Lone Eagle gasped out “My name is Lone Eagle and not-“
Longbow interrupted again saying “You’re Luke Morgan. I will prove it by the bum knee you had is the same as Luke Morgan’s.” 
Longbow stood watching as Lone Eagle stood staring at him with shock on his face and continued “Don’t you think I know, Luke Morgan? Pretty soon that wife of yours will show herself and I’ll do what I did to Brittany to her.” 
Lone Eagle growled as his eyes flared golden color. Longbow smiled of satisfaction and walked towards Lone Eagle and stood shoulder to shoulder. 
Lone Eagle heard him whisper “I know Ariana Nicholas, your wife, for she’ll show herself to fight for you and your sister.”
Lone Eagle felt anger and restrained himself with his hands still up in the air. 
Longbow stood staring at him then he smiled and spoke “You wouldn’t want anything to happen to your children do you?” 
He smiled flashing his teeth as he heard a growl from Lone Eagle and added “That’s why you’re here alone with Brittany. Ariana has the kids stashed safe out of dangerous hands, hmm?”
Longbow twisted out of the way of Lone Eagle’s attack with fists flying. Lone Eagle groaned feeling Longbow’s knee connected with his stomach. Lone Eagle felt himself thrown on the ground and kicked in the sides. 
Lone Eagle groaned from the ground again with Longbow stood over him speaking “Don’t bother fighting me. I have a black belt degree in martial arts and some military training. I know your moves like the back of my hand.” 
Lone Eagle lay moaning as he heard Longbow walking away. 
He thought to himself “Poor Longbow. He doesn’t understand.” 
He slowly picked himself up and limped away changing his form to a wolf. 

Chapter thirty six

The phone rang shrilling its call. Raya went to the phone from the bench in the dining room. The group stopped their eating dinner and looked at Raya. 
She spoke “It’s for you Coyote.”
She went to hand the cordless to Coyote who spoke “Coyote Wilson here.” 
He heard the voice of Longbow speak “The time has arrived. Come to the cabin alone and unarmed or I’ll see that Brittany dies and so will your son.” 
Coyote snarled out for the others in the room to hear him “You’re not hurting her or my son.”
Raya put her hands on her hips with annoyance as the Trio gasped and Grandfather narrowed his eyes. 
Coyote heard Longbow laugh and spoke “Do what I said, come alone, unarmed and be at Brittany’s cabin at this time.” 
Coyote’s face turned into a glare as he heard Longbow rattle off a time then he took the phone and toss it to Raya who demanded “What did Pack Leader want?”
Coyote replied “Something personal happened and I need to be there at a certain time.”
He abruptly got up from the table and threw his napkin while walking away. Sam got up and followed him towards Claire’s bedroom on the first floor. 
He spoke “Dad, what’s going on?”
Instead of answering, his father took off his guns and holsters and then proceeded to take the bullet case out of the guns. Then he went to the closet and opened it to reveal an open safe with a dial combination. 
Sam repeated his question pleading “Dad, what’s going on?”
Sighing Coyote replied “They threatened to kill your Mother and you.”
He heard Sam gasp and continued “I have something that I think Longbow wants which will bargain for your lives.”
Coyote opened the safe and put the guns in the safe with the bullet cases.
He shut the case and swung the dial and turned to face Sam who spoke “Be safe Dad.”
Coyote walked to his son and patted him on the shoulder then left the room with Sam following him. He walked through the living room and left through the sun room. Sam stood watching him leave the house and disappear into the forest. 

In the forest, Coyote reached Brittany’s cabin where Brittany stood restrained by two men. Longbow who stood next to them with a long knife and Brittany’s mouth was covered by the two men.
“I’m unarmed.” Said Coyote who stood staring at the four as Longbow gave out a howl and the bushes rumbled behind Coyote showing growling wolves. 
Longbow spoke “Kneel, Hunter.” 
Coyote growled and spoke “I came like you asked so let her go.” 
Longbow smiled a smirk and spoke “I see you’re in no position to give demands.”
Coyote kneeled and spoke “If you don’t mind, I’ll take off my shirt so you’ll have an easy time knifing me.” 
He pulled off his black shirt without waiting for Longbow to reply. Coyote saw Brittany’s eyes widen when she saw the necklace with the shiny pendant he was wearing around his neck and the scar mark on his chest on the right side. 
Longbow dropped the long knife and yelled out “You bastard! You had it all the time!” 
Brittany watched as Longbow’s eyes flared golden as he changed his form to a wolf and attacked Coyote. Coyote grabbed the wolf by the head with both hands and swung the wolf over his head. Then Longbow changed form back to Human and charged at Coyote who easily grabbed the male and threw him on his side. 
Longbow got up and felt his head grabbed and the long knife on his neck followed by Lone Eagle’s voice speaking “Do you yield? Keep the position as Pack Leader. Luke Morgan says so. The Hunter and his son lives period.” 
Longbow growled as Coyote got up taking the necklace with pendant off his neck. He handed it to Longbow who snatched it out of his hand. Lone Eagle let go of Longbow as the two men let go of Brittany. Brittany picked up Coyote’s discarded shirt. She handed the shirt to Coyote who put it back on. Together the two of them walked towards the house with several wolves moving out of the way. They heard Longbow howl some haunting cry from behind them. The sun disappeared behind the horizon as they reached the house’s back porch. The stars started coming out as Sam came running out with Nanook barking behind. He went to Brittany, grabbed her in a hug as he felt Coyote put a hand on his back while Brittany hugged her son. 

Coyote stood next to Brittany in front of the bedroom door and spoke “You take the bed, I’ll take the couch.” 
He heard Brittany sighed as she entered the bedroom while Coyote went to the living room couch. He lay down asleep then felt a prick of a knife side pointing at his neck. 
He heard Longbow’s familiar voice speaking “Well, the Hunter unarmed.” 
Coyote stared eyes squinting in the darken room. He heard a yell and felt the knife leave his neck followed by a crash of furniture breaking. Coyote got up from the couch and stood listening to the fighting. 
He heard Longbow speak “Ah Brittany. I’m not done with you yet.” 
Followed by a thud then the lights in the room flared on and Coyote saw Longbow with knife in hand gripping his head. Brittany on the floor reached out with her legs and swung them hitting Longbow in the legs and he fell to the floor with a thud. Brittany, Coyote saw, got up and started kicking Longbow with her feet yelling in a foreign language. Coyote grabbed Brittany, restraining her. To his shock she yielded with some shudders of pleasure sensed from her and running through him as he gripped her tight across his body. 
Longbow got up and Coyote ordered “Get out Longbow.” 
They heard a step into the room from Grandfather who saw them and spoke “Thomas, what are you doing here?”
Longbow turned and spoke “Leave it old man.” 
Coyote heard the sound of affection in Longbow’s voice towards Grandfather whose eyes widen with shock added “Thomas, why aren’t you home in Wolfville?” 
Longbow spoke “Just leave it old man.” 
He left them. They heard the front door open and close with a bang. Coyote looked around to see the Trio standing at the top of the stairs watching the situation. There was a light switch next to them on the wall. 
Grandfather spoke “Well, this will wait till morning.” 
He limped off to his room. 
Coyote spoke to the Trio “Go to bed kids.” 
He heard Sam speak “Do you want the lights on or off?’
Coyote responded “Off!”
He felt the lights flick off as he released Brittany who went to sit on the couch. Coyote sat next to her and put a hand on her back. He felt her shake from his touch. Coyote put his arms around her, pulling her towards him. He heard her moan a sigh as he lay on the couch with her wrapped in his arms. Brittany sighed, while lying on Coyote who stroked her hair.
“It’s been a long time hasn’t it?” He said. 
Brittany spoke “Yes it has been a long time.” 
Coyote sensed her fell asleep and closed his eyes with his arms around her.

Morning shined her rays of light through the windows of the living room; Coyote opened his eyes with a start. He felt fur in his left hand and looked to see a white wolf curled in a ball asleep on him and his right hand near the snout. He could feel the air coming in from the wolf breathing in and out on his right hand. Coyote stared at the white wolf, frowning with his left hand on the wolf. Sighing he rubbed the fur under his left hand and stared at the wolf who gave off some sound while shifting to curl tighter in a ball. Coyote heard Grandfather come limping in the room. 
Grandfather seeing the white wolf on Coyote whispered “It figures.” 
He went to sit down and waited. Coyote saw the white wolf open its eyes and the head swiveled to look at him while changing its form to reveal Brittany. Brittany stared at Coyote who stared back at her with a neutral expression in his face. 
Sighing Brittany rose but Coyote held her and whispered “I’m fine with you being what you are.” 
Brittany stared at Coyote then she leaned down and gave him a kiss on the cheek before getting up to face Grandfather who spoke “You’re Ghost.” 
Brittany responded “Yes.” 
Coyote got up from the couch to stand next to her. 
Grandfather loudly spoke “Kids, stop hiding from behind the corner and come down.”
Coyote looked to see the teens come down the stairs from the loft and they went to stand in at the bottom of the stairs staring at Grandfather with a whining Nanook.
“What?” Grandfather said to the Trio. 
Michael spoke “Who’s Thomas?” 
Grandfather replied “Ah, your Pack Leader, is Thomas. I recognized his voice the moment he spoke to me.” 
The front door banged open and closed as Raya came in the room followed by Hocus. 
Michael firmly ordered Nanook while noticing her eye the cat “Sit, Stay!”
Raya asked “What’s going on?”
Brittany answered for Grandfather “He recognized Pack Leader by this name of Thomas.” 
Raya gasped and pointed to a picture frame on the wall with a glare at Grandfather. The picture frame the Trio noticed showed a younger Claire standing over two younger boys. They were standing in front of a Christmas tree with forced smiles on their faces.
Sighing Grandfather explained “Thomas is my son and Claire’s younger brother by a different Mother.” 
The others except Raya and Coyote gasped as Grandfather continued “There’s a second son named Sean who’s the youngest also by a different Mother.” 
Coyote spoke “It explains how Longbow got your phone number.”
Grandfather was about to speak when the doorbell rang. 
He ordered “Somebody answer the door.” 
Michael went to the door and peered in the peephole. 
He yelled “It’s State Trooper Johnson!”
Grandfather spoke “Let him in.”
Michael let in State Trooper Johnson came in carrying a video tape. He frowned when he noticed Brittany but looked shocked to see Coyote standing there with arms folded. 
“The Hunter” He said out loud “Pleased to meet you, Coyote Wilson. I’m State Trooper Johnson.” 
Coyote nodded his head and kept his arms folded while staring at the State Trooper with a neutral expression on his face. 
Raya muttered out loud “I’ll get breakfast ready. Come on kids.” 
She gestured to the Trio to follow her and they followed her into the kitchen. 
Grandfather ordered “Brittany, please leave us.”
Brittany kept her face neutral while she went to the kitchen. The men heard the doors slam behind her.
