Morning shined her rays on through the forests canopy. Going back to civilization meant leaving Brittany alone but during his off hours of work at the Port Monaco Police Station, he visited Brittany’s cabin leaving food, provisions and items anonymously. It was the month of July when he had time off to visit Brittany personally. He had heard rumors of Brittany being pregnant and denying it when she was asked along with oddly seemingly insane from people hearing her talking nonsense sentences from her seen around the town. 
“Brittany” he spoke to himself, “Why didn’t you tell me about the baby?”
Sighing he walked towards the door and knocked. 

Brittany awoke from the knock. She hauled herself from the rocker she was sitting in and waddled towards the door. Opening it a crack, she saw Coyote Wilson standing there in his police uniform.

Coyote grabbed the door and pulled it wider despite Brittany’s protests of “I’m fine, no need to bother me.” 
Coyote spoke “Don’t deny it, Brittany. You’re pregnant with my child.”
He heard Brittany gasp as she backed away from the door and he entered the cabin seeing her cover her abdomen with her hands. Brittany he heard gasped as he grabbed her hands and yanked her large sweat shirt off her, revealing a swollen abdomen with child. 
Sighing Coyote asked “Why didn’t you tell me?”
He sensed Brittany shiver has he put back on her sweat shirt covering her. 

Brittany shivered as he put back on her sweat shirt over her swollen abdomen. She felt him put a hand on her where their child lay kicking away. He put his other hand on her chin and forced her to look up at his face. 
Brittany averted her eyes as Coyote spoke “Look at me, Brittany. Why?” 
Brittany shivered again and spoke “The others won’t understand and would kill the baby.” 
Coyote spoke “Let me take the baby to safety, just to be raised. The baby will have my protection.” 
Brittany shook her head as panic came and spoke “No! I won’t let you take the baby like my parents were taken.” 

Coyote recognizing the panic in her wide eyes as she shook held her in a hug and whispered in her ear “Don’t worry, Brittany, I swear it that the baby will live and no one will take it.” 

Brittany sighed feeling Coyote’s arms wrapped around her. Sighing she leaned into Coyote’s arms and felt a prick of a needle shot in her arm. 

He pulled out the syringe hidden in his sleeve as Brittany sighed and leaned into his arms. He brought the syringe into her arm and felt her stiffen from his arms around her. 
He felt her sway from the drug as he spoke “I’m sorry, Brittany, I have to do this.” 
He gently lowered her to the floor as she went unconscious. 
Coyote pulled out his radio from his waist belt and spoke “Target’s out you can come now and get her.”
He went to the door and yanked it open standing outside waiting as bushes rumbled showing fellow police officers and two paramedics carrying a stretcher who entered the cabin with him following. He stood watching them hoist Brittany onto the stretcher and then lifted it up. He stared at Brittany seeing that she looked pale and had dark circles underneath her eyes while recalling to himself that she seemed to be on the thin side when he looked at her without her top on. He exhaled a breath as the paramedics carried her out which he followed closing the cabin door. He followed them through the forest to the road where an ambulance stood which they loaded her inside and then the vehicle drove away. He felt a hand on his shoulder looked with surprise to see his father Detective Wilson who was frowning. 
He stared at his father who spoke “Chances are she might be put in an asylum due to people’s reports about hearing her talking scattered talk to herself while out and about in town.”
He nodded his head for he had heard the reports himself from town’s people and seen how Brittany acted that she seemed a little out of it. 

When she came too, Brittany found herself arms strapped to a bed in a room with white all around. She lay there realizing what Coyote had done to her, sent her to an asylum. Looking down she saw that her abdomen was still swollen with child. There was a needle injecting clear stuff in her right arm. Brittany was wearing a white hospital gown.
“Coyote” she screamed “How could you do this to me?!”
 Then a door in front of the bed opened and an orderly of the asylum, covered in white came out complete with a mask. 
The orderly spoke in a feminine voice “Stop screaming or I’ll be forced to inject you with something.” 
Brittany glared at the woman in the white mask and spoke “Why am I here?”
The woman spoke “As if you don’t know, you tried to kill the baby. It was a good thing you were brought in here, because the baby and you were dying from starvation.” 
Brittany asked “Starvation? What are you talking about? I’ve been eating fine.” 
The woman sarcastically replied “Eating fine? Not according to the doctors. Your diet of foods wasn’t enough for the baby, Hmph.”
Brittany snarled out “Who brought me here and how long am I here for?”
The woman spoke “Who else but Officer Coyote Wilson brought you here.” 
Brittany glared at the woman who added, “The doctors have decided because your health towards the baby, it will be taken away and adopted, once they determined the well being of the baby.”
Brittany screamed “No! You’re not taking this baby away from me!”
The woman pulled out a syringe and injected something in Brittany’s arm then she turned and left the room as Brittany screamed ranting out her cries.

Peering out of a plastic window of the door, Coyote stood with shock on his face. He heard a step and looked to see his father Detective Wilson standing there next to him.
“I’m sorry” He heard his father say “About the baby. Don’t worry there’s a family waiting to adopt the baby.” 
Coyote spoke “Don’t be sorry, I love her well enough to care for the well being of the baby.” 
Coyote heard a rustle of paper as his father handed him a clipboard with paper on it. Coyote could barely see the words with his eyes blurring as he signed the agreement form signing away his rights as the father to the baby Brittany was carrying.
Detective Wilson spoke “Don’t worry about her, the asylum will take care of her then.”
Sighing Coyote walked away before his father could see the tears fall from his eyes.

Brittany lay racking from the pain of labor. She gritted her teeth trying not to groan out loud as the tremors of pain rocked through her. She heard a sound of a small alarm and looked to see the door open showing the orderly female with two other male orderlies. 
The female spoke “Ooh you’re in labor.”
She held out a syringe which Brittany growled at her. The female gestured towards the male orderlies who grabbed a struggling Brittany who screamed from pain. She barely felt the female prick her arm with the syringe. Then Brittany felt herself getting woozy and falling asleep as she felt the orderlies drag her from the room. 

Coyote stood staring out the window of the asylum his eyes not seeing the scenery. He heard a baby crying sound from behind him and slowly turned around to stare at his father Detective Wilson holding a wrapped bundle in his arms. His eyes riveted on the moving bundle and he as in a trance walked towards his father to hold out his hands who handed him the bundle he saw was a baby with a mop of blonde hair on the head. 
He heard his father speak “It’s a boy.”
Coyote stared at his son who opened his eyes and he saw brown eyes which to his relief reminded him of Brittany’s. His son scrunched up his face to wail a crying sound which he gently rocked the baby and sensed his son stop the wailing to close his eyes falling asleep. He heard a sound of the door open with a slam and looked up to see a woman with a mean look on her face while wearing clothing of one color walking into the room. 
He stared at the woman who walked to him with her hands up. 
His father spoke “Give her the baby, Coyote.” 
Coyote brought his attention to the baby which he kissed his son’s forehead and then handed the woman the baby who without a word left the room slamming the door behind her. He bowed his head and felt his father’s hand on his shoulder. 
He looked up to stare at his father as he spoke “I like to see Brittany.”
He saw a frown on his father’s face who spoke “That’s not possible. I’m told that they released her after giving birth to the baby.”
He felt annoyance arriving as he glared at his father who added “I’m sorry, Coyote.”
He nodded his head of understanding then felt his father’s hand on his arm pulling him which he didn’t resist to the pulling as he silently walked. 

Next thing Brittany recalled with distaste running through her she drowsily woke up from a bed to hear a baby crying before falling back to the darkness of sleep. Brittany woke up with a jerk to find herself lying on a grass covered ground with tall towering trees standing overhead which she recognized as a forest which she sat up to discover herself without any clothes on. Groaning Brittany felt herself fine along with a feeling of hunger. She stared at the ground to see deer tracks which she walked stumbling through the bushes following them. She groaned putting a hand to her forehead and then shifted form to a white wolf which her nose scented the deer in the forest which she followed quietly. She heard a raging river sound and followed it to see a deer a young male buck lapping at the water. Growling inwardly she snuck behind the deer who continued lapping then struck throwing her body onto its back knocking it to the ground and brought her teeth to the deer’s neck in a tight jaw crushing grip. She held on as the male buck struggled in her grip as she continued to bite bringing her jaws further into its neck till the deer stopped its struggling giving up its life. She released her hold on its neck and went to its side biting with fury at its nourishment while sating her hunger. She ate till she couldn’t take any more bites and then went to the river to lap up water which she drank her thirstiness away. Then her nose alerted her of a presence behind her which she spun around growling to see a group of wolves staring at her in a semi circle as a wolf stood up on its hind legs shifting form to a male Human with Native American looks on his face, and pulled back hair and clothes of animal skins. Brittany frowned staring at the male who seemed familiar but couldn’t place him. 
The male spoke “Show yourself Amula, we won’t harm you but we want to know who you are.” 
Brittany stiffened of shock as she remembered who the male was her younger brother Luke who was staring at her with no recognition on his frowning face. She pushed herself up and shifted form to a Human and saw Luke’s eyes widen staring at her. 
She stared at him with a frown as Luke spoke “Older sister, Brittany, it’s your younger brother Luke. What happened to you?”
She shrugged as Luke yanked off his long sleeve top and tossed it to her which she put on covering her to the knees like a short dress. 
Luke she stared at spoke “I heard around town that you were expecting a baby. What’s with that?”
She spoke with venom in her voice “Just some sick rumor to shame me and ruin my reputation said by some idiot.”
She narrowed her eyes as she saw Luke narrow his eyes and make a sign with his hand which she recognized said “Talk to me later in private.”
She added speaking “So Amula? What’s with the name and who are these wolves? I thought the curse of skin walking would be passed by shooting a wolf. What’s with that?”
She folded her arms staring at Luke who spoke “There’s no curse, Brittany. Skin walking is part of a humanoid race called Amula that has lived for years undetected as wolf and Human.” 
She frowned hearing that to stare at Luke who continued "I found out about this after meeting the Amula in the forest who told me of the Amula race like I'm telling you."
She spoke as Luke paused to narrow his eyes aimed at her "Well that's interesting so tell me everything related to this Amula species and help me get my life back will you?"
She saw Luke nod his head as he gestured her to walk with him into the forest in Human form which she obeyed listening to her brother detail everything.

Chapter forty 

Grandfather sat in the chair watching as the teens arrived in the house with Raya. He stared at the stairs absent mildly and switched off the TV.
Raya came in with a serious look in her face as she spoke “So?”
Grandfather replied “Their upstairs.” 
He added while noticing Sam put a foot on the stairs “Let them work it out and they’ll come down themselves when their ready.” 
Sam frowned as Raya ordered “Michael, Tina come in the kitchen with me now.” 
She ushered the siblings into the kitchen while Sam stood in front of Grandfather who spoke “Your parents are working things out upstairs.”
Sam nodded his head. Grandfather dismissed him with a wave of a hand. Sam went to the kitchen to see the others there. He sat down at the table with a frown leaning on his hand as Hocus jumped on the table and the cat rubbed his head on Sam’s hand. Sam gave the cat scratches absent mildly. The group in the kitchen heard the doors open as Brittany walked inside with a frown on her face. Sam got up to stand as Brittany walked over to him and gave him a hug. 
Sam asked “Mom, about Dad?” 
Brittany replied “Don’t worry, we worked something out.” 
They heard the doorbell ring sounding loudly in the house. The trio and Brittany left the kitchen to see Coyote arrive in the living room holding a large thick rectangular brown cardboard package. 
He spoke “That was the delivery truck with something addressed to me. I don’t remember ordering anything.” 
Grandfather spoke “I did order something for you, Coyote. So open the package.” 
Raya came out of the kitchen carrying scissors by the blades which she held up waving them. Coyote took the scissors and set the package down on the couch and sat as Raya stood with arms folded. The group watched as he attacked the package with the scissors and once open Coyote set the scissors down on the table next to the couch. He looked at Grandfather with a shocked look on his face then at the open package. Shaking his head Coyote pulled out a large metal grey box by the handle from the package wrapping along with an object the trio gasped as Brittany stiffened seeing it. Coyote held up the object which was a long grey arm length gun with a flashlight built into its features. 
Grandfather spoke “The gun, a hunter’s rifle was built on my orders and is set to your preferences, Coyote.” 
Coyote stared at the gun and he looked at the metal box. Coyote opened the metal box to see sets of large golden bullets which he picked up examining it with one hand.
Frowning he set the bullet down and examined the gun and spoke “I think this will do.” 
He heard nothing in response but noticed Raya giving Grandfather a glaring expression that reminded him of hatred and that the male didn't seem to notice the look instead was concentrating on staring at him. Coyote without a comment picked up the box and gun and took it into the sun room which he spied a hook on the wall above the windows and pulled a chair below it while putting the bullet's box on a table along with putting a bullet into the gun and then stood on the chair finding himself having to stand on tiptoes to reach the hook which he hung the gun and then once satisfied with his work put the chair away and walked into the living room finding the others had notice where he put the gun and bullets' box he finding himself not concerned about it. Coyote noticed Raya give Grandfather a glare and then walk into the kitchen slamming the doors as he eyed the others. He eyed Brittany who shook her head in some no gesture while closing her eyes and saw her open her eyes and walk out going outside shifting form into a white wolf that bounded away going into the forest out of sight. Coyote eyed the kids who in response walked by him and Grandfather without a word them having grimaces on their faces which he heard the front door bang loudly which he went and peered through the peephole to find them sitting on the porch. 
Coyote went to Grandfather and spoke "The wolves will retaliate against you for giving me the gun." 
He eyed Grandfather who spoke in response sounding sarcastic "I'm an old man there's nothing the Amula as the wolves call themselves officially can do against me. I know many things about the Amula and have put measures in place in case they take me out on a permanent basis due to making an agreement with people who have power to assure of those measures. Don't worry about the Amula and their reaction towards me giving you a gun. They won't do anything deadly against me for Amula don't kill Amula period." 
Coyote stiffened hearing Grandfather's words who flared wolf like eyes aimed at him before resuming Human looking brown eyes. He exhaled a breath as Grandfather without another comment turned on the TV with a click of a remote and appeared to be focused his attention onto it by the look on his face seemingly amuse by the sporting event of race cars blared onto it from what he heard. 
He sighed and without a word walked into the kitchen to find Raya standing with arms folded who gave him a glare and she spoke "Out! I'm busy cooking and don't need you and who else underfoot so leave! Take a walk in the forest while you're at it!"
Coyote found Raya's expression indicated that she didn't want to hear him talk obeyed to go out of the kitchen to go to the sun room which he exhaled a breath and went onto the porch to find a rocking chair and sat seemingly lengthy due to figuring out it was best to stay close to the house for awhile. 

Chapter forty two

The Trio sat at the stairs on the porch of the front of the house not talking to each other and they stiffened hearing siren sounds as a police car, a fire truck and an ambulance arrived with lights flashing. 
They stood up as Officer Larsen they saw got out of the car speaking “We got a nine one, one call from someone incoherent and tracked it to here.”
The Trio’s eyes widen as they yelled in unison “Grandfather!”

The Trio stood outside on the porch watching the paramedics hauled an unconscious Grandfather on a stretcher with an oxygen mask on his face and loaded him into the ambulance which drove away sirens sounding the medics not giving them a word on what was his medical condition was instead just carried him out into the ambulance and drove away as Officer Larsen stood watching. 
The teens eyed the officer who spoke "Don't worry he'll be fine once he gets checked out." 
Sam heard the sarcasm of Officer Larsen's voice tone figured that the medical condition had something to due with Amula retaliating for giving his Father a gun. He kept the thought to himself as Officer Larsen took leave via car with the fire truck following. He eyed Michael and Tina warily as both walked down the porch's steps and went into the forest together leaving him on the steps ignoring him while appearing to not be interested in talking to him. He sighed and figured that he'll wander around the forest himself. Sam walked in the forest in the sun when he heard a twig snap behind him and spun around as he was hit in the face. He groaned as he was hit again and fell to the ground. 

Coyote felt himself fed up with sitting in the rocking chair got up and walked into the forest wandering around till his senses urged him to go in a direction as if compelled which he followed till he heard a loud groan in the forest and followed the sound to see Sam lying on the ground looking like he had an injury to his face judging by the bruise and saw a black wolf bounding away into the bushes. 
He picked up his son and carried him to the house entering it as Raya met him in the living room exclaiming “Oh dear, Sam!” 
Coyote angrily spoke “Take care of him while I go handle the fool who did this.”
He went to the sun room grabbing a chair and stood on it on tiptoe grabbing his gun off the hook then stormed out of the house.

Longbow stood in the clearing in front of Brittany’s cabin as wolves arrived answering his summons. He stood with arms folded as a white wolf arrive changing form to Brittany who stood besides him with arms folded. Longbow frowned as he heard rustling in the bushes to see Coyote with gun in his hand arrived. 
Wolves stood on their feet from their haunches growling at Coyote who spoke in an angry tone “I found Sam lying on the ground, hurt judging by the looks of him and a wolf running away from him.”
Longbow heard Brittany gasp hearing Coyote’s words. Coyote, Longbow saw pointed his gun at him with a glare on his face and jerked as a gun shot was heard by the group. Longbow grabbed Brittany restraining her as Coyote dropped the gun and crumbled onto the ground closing his eyes. Behind him where Coyote once stood was Daniel with a handgun in his hand and an angry look on his face. 
Longbow spoke “Daniel.” 
Daniel spoke “He interrupted me as I was about to shoot Sam.” 

Brittany yanked herself out of Longbow’s grip and stormed towards Daniel yelling “Daniel, you idiot! Shooting people won’t solve things!”
She grabbed the gun from Daniel’s hand and tossed it into the bushes then picked up Coyote by the arms and proceeded to drag him towards the cabin. 
Longbow spoke “Brittany-“
She interrupted “You got a problem I should know about, Longbow?”

Brittany, Longbow saw gave him a glare as she dragged Coyote to the cabin door which she opened with one hand. Then picked up Coyote and dragged him into the cabin. Longbow flinched hearing the door slam behind her with a bang sound. 
He went to Daniel who picked up Coyote’s rifle and spoke “Give me the gun, Daniel.”
Longbow repeated his words with a hand out as Daniel stared at him with an angry look on his face. 
He calmly stared at Daniel who handed him Coyote’s rifle and Longbow ordered “The handgun Brittany threw in the bushes. Amula will get it for me.” 
One of the wolves stepped forwards and walked into the bushes and came out with the handgun in its mouth which Longbow took. 
Longbow spoke “New orders for the Amula, no one shoots the Hunter or attacks his son without my say so. You all understand?” 
He heard murmurs of agreements among the wolves and stared at Daniel whose eyes were staring at the ground. 
Longbow spoke “The orders involve you, Daniel. You understand?”
Daniel spoke “I understand.” 
Longbow stared at the sky which showed the fading sun going down the horizon and spoke “Scatter, go home and get some sleep. We’ll meet here again in the morning at my summons.” 
The wolves scattered as Daniel changed form into a black wolf running into the bushes. Longbow made a sound of disgust and with guns in hand walked into the forest leaving Brittany’s cabin. 

Chapter forty three

Brittany lay on the couch bed in her wolf form with Coyote lying next to her with his shirt off. She woke up hearing Coyote’s growl and opened her eyes shifting into her Human form. Frowning she stared at Coyote and gasped seeing his eyes open staring at the ceiling which were wolf eyes of golden yellow. She saw Coyote’s eyes turn to face hers and felt his hands on her pulling her towards him. Brittany kept herself still as Coyote placed a hand on her chin pulling her towards his face and stared as he kissed her on the lips. She stiffened feeling where his other hand went and realized what he wanted from her. 

Raya stood in the living room as Michael came in the house and saw him frowned seeing Sam lying on the couch groaning of pain. Tina came in from the front door and gasped seeing Sam who sat up seeing her. 
Raya spoke “Michael, escort Sam upstairs alone and stay with him just for the night. Call me if he needs any medical attention. I’ll be sleeping in the guest bedroom.”
Michael obeyed pulling Sam off the couch who stared at Tina as he was pulled up the stairs. 
Once the boys were out of earshot, Raya spoke “Tina, trust me when I say please lock your door to your bedroom and don’t come out till morning.” 
She saw Tina give her a confused look but nodded her head and went upstairs. 

Michael sat in the armchair in Sam’s room staring at Sam lying groaning on the bed with his eyes closed. He heard him give out a sharp groan and stood up as Sam opened his eyes. Michael put a hand on his mouth refraining himself from gasping out loud when he saw Sam’s eyes were a like a wolf’s golden yellow eyes as the teen shifted form into a grey wolf that shook its head before resuming its human position. Michael stared at Sam who closed his eyes and went still. He listened to Sam’s breathing and heard him breathing deeply as if he was asleep. Then Michael tiptoed towards the arm chair and sat staring at Sam sleeping on the bed with a frown. 

Morning shined rays of light from the sun as Brittany sat up from the bed with the sheet covering her. She stared at Coyote lying next to her sheet covering him from the chest down with his arms at the sides over it. Frowning Brittany looked at the side of the bed to see her clothes sprawled lying on the floor next to it. She got up picking up her clothes putting them on while staring at Coyote’s sleeping form. Brittany heard a small knock on the door and went to it opening it to face Longbow who stood with arms folded. 
Brittany folded her arms and spoke “What do you want Longbow?”
Longbow she saw leaned towards her appearing to sniff and he spoke “You reek of the Hunter, Brittany. Go take a shower.” 
Brittany repeated her question “What do you want Longbow?”
Longbow spoke “Nothing, just checking up on the Hunter’s status.”
She frowned as he bent to pick up a large canvas bag which he thrust at her while speaking “Something for the Hunter when he awakes. I’ll be calling for a meeting soon. I expect the Hunter healed enough to leave for the house by the time of the meeting. If he wants further medical attention, he’ll have to get it at the house.” 
Brittany nodded her head and entered the cabin carrying the canvas bag slamming the door behind her. She went to the kitchen with a frown while looking at Coyote jerking in his sleep. 

Coyote jerked his Human eyes awake as awareness filled his senses with a new feeling. He stared in the darkness of the cabin unseeing the contents and sat up hearing noises feeling disorient of his surroundings. Coyote groaned shaking his head. 
He heard Brittany’s voice speaking as it got nearer to him “Good your up, Coyote, here eat.” 
He felt a tray placed on his lap and stared unseeing her in the darkness as he felt food on a fork touch his mouth which he opened letting in the food. 
Coyote spoke after finishing the food “Daniel shot me from behind.” 
He heard Brittany gasp and added “I wasn’t unconscious as I lay on the ground with my eyes closed. I heard every word said and felt you dragging me into your cabin where I passed out.”
Coyote felt her put a cup full of liquid to his mouth which he drank drinking the whole contents. 
Once finished he continued speaking “The bullet wound, would you check it for me, Brittany? I don’t feel any pain.”
He felt the tray removed and heard a bang noise as it was set on the floor and sensed her hands touching his back. He sighed feeling her hands pull off the bandage on the right side of his back and felt her hands touch him rubbing the area. 
Coyote spoke “The bullet wound?”
He heard Brittany speak with a gasping tone “The bullet wound is all healed up with no scar.”
Coyote stared in the darkness as he realized what the awareness was and frowned.
He spoke “Interesting, I must have some Hunter healing power that healed me.” 
He heard Brittany say in his ear “I don’t know if the Hunter healing power like you said did that but it sure explains it. Are you well enough to get up and leave the cabin to the house? I think my work here is done.” 
Coyote spoke “I feel well enough and I want my clothes back.” 

The cabin door opened behind Longbow who turned around to see Brittany come out with Coyote. Longbow stood with arms folded among the wolves scattered in the clearing staring at Coyote with Daniel next to him. Longbow stiffened seeing Coyote’s Human eyes change to a wolf’s golden yellow eyes when seeing Daniel and looked at Brittany with a sharp look. He saw her look at him and he jerked his head at Coyote gesturing. Brittany he saw looked at Coyote and frowned seeing the Hunter’s eyes which blinked changing back to Human eyes that narrowed boring at Daniel. 
Longbow spoke “Take him to the house, Brittany.” 
He stood as Brittany took Coyote’s arm and pulled him out of the clearing. 

Chapter forty four
Night fallen, Longbow stood at the edge of the clearing surrounding the house watching the back door. He stiffened as a figure with a flashlight, light came out of the house and stood on the porch. Longbow moved himself behind a tree and peered out as the flashlight holder walked towards him hiding in the darkness making a straight beeline. He stood behind the tree as the light got nearer and walked around the tree. 
Longbow blinked his eyes of the flashlight glare and spoke loudly “Just as I suspected. I saw the way you walked towards me hiding in the darkness which shows that you can detect Amula.” 
He heard a gun weapon cock and added “You know who shot you. I’ll tell you Jojo brought Daniel to a healer after finding him in an easily detected by Amula, trap while complaining of a bad headache, which I examined. I saw your eyes change when you saw Daniel after leaving Brittany’s cabin. It appears that Daniel lost something when he shot you which you gained, Coyote.”
Longbow blinked his eyes as the flashlight lowered itself followed by the gun clicking sound and stared at Coyote with a glare on his face. 
Coyote spoke with anger in his voice “You will tell the others to not to harm Sam or Brittany.” 
Longbow spoke “Or you as well, I’ll be sure to do that tomorrow in the morning.” 
Longbow stared at Coyote who pointed a pointer finger at him and left him walking towards the house. 

Chapter forty four

Coyote walked in the forest as the sun shined its rays of light. His awareness feeling told him that Amula were in the forest hiding and watching him. He went around a tree and stood hearing a sound of a person walking in the forest. Coyote stalked the person silently and waited around a tree peering. His eyes narrowed seeing Daniel walking in the forest towards him unseeing him. Coyote waited as Daniel went around the tree he was hiding and struck grabbing the male by the throat with one hand. He thrust a struggling Daniel’s back onto a tree and lifted the male up off his feet above him. Coyote brought his fisted left hand into Daniel’s stomach hard that groaned loudly and stopped struggling. He let go of Daniel’s throat that fell onto a lying position on the ground groaning loudly. Coyote walked away further into the forest and reached a clearing. His awareness feeling told him Amula was in the bushes surrounding him. 
Coyote spoke “Come out, I’m not armed.” 
The bushes rumbled around him as wolves came out growling and snapping their teeth. He stood with hands fisted as he heard a loud howling sound and saw the wolves turn around running into the bushes leaving him alone. 

Sam came out of his bedroom followed by Michael. They went down the stairs. 
At the bottom Sam turned around and spoke “Tina, you skin walked.” 
Michael seeing Tina at the top of the stairs grabbed Nanook by the collar and held the dog as Tina’s form changed into a wolf then changed back to her Human form. The Trio went in the kitchen and froze seeing Claire Patricoly sitting at the table who looked at them with a confused look. 
Raya at the stove spoke “Claire, this is Michael, Tina and Sam. Their one of us and is staying with George.”
The trio raised their hands at the sound of their names. They stiffened seeing Claire’s eyes turn golden yellow wolf like then blinked back to Human eyes with no recognition in them aimed at them.
Claire got up and spoke “I want to see my brother.” 
Raya spoke with back to them “Go ahead, Claire, but remember drinking means no driving.” 
Claire spoke “I understand, Raya.” 
She left the kitchen without a glance at the Trio. They saw her form outside the window walking into the forest. 
Raya turned around to look at the Trio and spoke “Michael take Tina outside and introduce her to the Pack Leader.” 
Michael nodded his head and left the kitchen with Tina behind him. Sam went to the table and sat staring out the window. He saw Michael outside whispering in Tina’s ear and saw her nod her head as they both change forms into wolves which bounded into the forest. Sam sighed loudly. 

Longbow stood in front of Brittany’s cabin as wolves arrived along with Lone Eagle hauling a groaning Daniel. 
One of the wolves changed form to Jojo who exclaimed “Daniel!”
Daniel fell to his knees and laid on the ground with hand on his stomach groaning loudly as Jojo ran to him and kneeled next to him. 
Longbow stared at Lone Eagle who spoke “The Hunter ambushed him, I saw. He grabbed Daniel by the throat putting his back onto a tree, lifting him up above him and punched him in the stomach.” 
Longbow spoke “Daniel, change your form now.” 
Daniel obeyed changing into a black wolf lying on its side. 
Longbow added “Now change it back.” 
He stood as Daniel changed form and continued “How are your senses?”
Daniel stared at him and spoke in a groaning tone “Their fine.” 
Longbow spoke with sarcasm “Oh really? Case number one, you walked into a snare trap in your wolf form that was reeking, easily detected by Amula. I know this because I used the wolf form and I could smell the trap the same distance as the clearing. Case number two, Jojo told me that you acted like you didn’t detect her while howling away when she came upon you from behind in a Human form. Case number three, your still on the ground groaning from the Hunter’s punch which I know won’t bring down Amula.”

He ignored Brittany and walked into the forest sensing her following to his annoyance.

Besides George didn't deny the gun giving to Coyote in the presences of the kids, myself and Raya who all heard that claim."

Your father claims he had this gun ordered for Coyote set for his hunting standards which he said it in my presence of myself, Brittany and the kids, Sam, Michael and Tina."

He heard the firmness of Coyote's voice tone obeyed to watch Coyote go into the sun room which he followed watching the male put the gun on a hook on the wall high above from standing on a chair in tiptoes after slamming the box down onto a table then stood with arms folded giving him a glaring stare of accusation in his eyes. Chapter forty five

Lone Eagle came into the clearing where Longbow stood with Brittany and other wolves.

I managed to get Daniel out due to suspecting that the cage trap was set by those State Troopers who'll come check on it.”

Coyote stood on the front porch with his arms folded as he heard the door bang closed behind him followed by steps. He felt the familiar awareness feeling and placed a hand on his forehead groaning softly.

He heard Longbow continued speaking “Brittany told me, you haven’t been the same since Daniel shot you. I should tell you Daniel lost his ability to detect Amula along with his wolf senses.”
Coyote looked at Longbow with a glare on his face growling loudly as the male paused to fold his arms and added “The ability and the senses transferred to you. You’re angry about that which caused you to kill Daniel. Your words heard before you shot him were ‘You’ll pay for what you did to me.’”
Coyote lowered his arms eyes narrowed growling louder while glaring at Longbow who lowered his arms. 
Longbow spoke “Why fight it? Embrace the senses, for your one of us now.” 
Coyote felt his control snap as his hands shot out grabbing Longbow by the shirt raising him up and threw the man towards the house. Longbow’s back hit the house wall. 
Coyote advanced towards Longbow growling loudly as the male shook his head and spoke “Stop fighting it, Coyote. The senses are there to stay.” 
Coyote roared some growling sound grabbing Longbow with one hand on his neck raising him up above him. 
Coyote snarled as Longbow gagged out with hands on his arm “You can’t fight the senses forever. Sooner or later, you’ll accept it.”
Coyote brought his fist into Longbow’s stomach repeatedly punching him while growling angry. He heard the front door open followed by running footsteps and felt hands grabbed his punching hand. 
Coyote shook at the hands which kept an ironclad grip as he heard Brittany’s angry voice speaking “Stop it, Coyote! Let him go now!”
Coyote released Longbow who landed on the porch deck on his back groaning loudly. Coyote felt himself pulled down the porch steps by Brittany who took him speed walking through the forest till they reached the fence of the horse coral. Coyote looked at Brittany who let go of his hand and she hugged his form. He sighed feeling her arms around him with her form pressed into his front and he closed his eyes letting himself calm down. He rubbed his chin on the side of her head.
He heard her speak “You’ve changed ever since you shot Belen. You haven’t been the same since the shooting.”
Coyote spoke “I had a life with plans before that happened.” 
He sensed Brittany put her hands on his cheeks and opened his eyes to stare at her eyes. 
Brittany spoke “Yes, I know.” 
He heard growling sounds to see multiple wolves come into sight growling and snapping their jaws aimed at them. 
Coyote frowned as Brittany spoke loudly "Leave him alone!"
He heard unexpectedly "I didn't say that you could attack the Hunter in retaliation against him hurting me. I'm fine as expected from the punching so scatter and leave." 
He eyed Longbow standing nearby with arms folded as he eyed the wolves who didn't give a protest instead scattered into the forest as the male pointed a finger aimed at him and added "You'll accept us Amula one of these days, Hunter mark my words. That oath I don't care how will come true period even if I have to be the hand of doing it."

He felt Brittany hug him unexpectedly in response despite his mood as he sighed from the feel of her body pressing into his front and clamped his mouth shut to shut his eyes willing himself to relax from her hugging him. He kept himself relaxed enough as Brittany continued to hug him as his senses of Amula spying on them blared unexpectedly but ignored the feeling to let her hug him as he leaned the side of his chin on her head and sighing softly. 

Chapter forty six December/January 2003

Coyote walked into the forest of the night in the snow with gun in his hand. He paused to adjust the strap of his backpack wrapped on his back. He stood as the sky lit up with firelight illuminating the forest. Coyote looked up to see the sky full of fire along with shaking and booming noises. He frowned staring at the sky and as a tree tipped forward falling towards him. Coyote ran as the mess of tree branches landed onto him pining him onto the ground on his side. He groaned loudly as white smoke arrived through out the clearing blinding him followed by intense pressure pushing him into the ground. Coyote shook his head struggling to stay awake from the air that went thin. His eyes sight went blurry as blackness over took him. 

The sun shined as Longbow walked in the forest among the snow looking among trees that lay lying on their sides on the ground. He paused when he sensed something behind him and spun around with long knife ready. Longbow lowered the knife to face Nanook that whined wagging her tail. 
He sighed out “Nanook, where have you been, you silly dog?” 
Nanook walked up to him and with her mouth grabbed a fold of loose clothing and proceeded to pull him. Longbow allowed her to pull him through the forest till they reached a tree lying on the sides. Nanook let go of Longbow and pawed the tree branches barking excitedly. Longbow pulled apart the tree branches and stiffened seeing Coyote’s form lying there unconscious. He stood up and howled the summons call. Longbow waited as Nanook pawed the tree branches barking excitedly as wolves arrived. One of the wolves changed form to reveal Michael wearing animal skin clothing like Longbow who pulled out a rope and tied it around Nanook’s neck. 
Longbow spoke as he yanked up some of the tree branches revealing Coyote “Help the Hunter, and he won’t be so eager to kill one of us.”

Brittany wearing animal skin clothing stood with Sam wearing identical clothing among the teepees and huts as wolves and men arrived carrying a figure on as make shift stretcher. She gasped seeing it was Coyote and frowned putting a hand on Sam’s shoulder that swung his long blonde hair out of his face to look at her. The two watched as the men brought Coyote into a hut and came out. 
She frowned seeing Longbow walk up to her speaking “Nanook found him and pointed him to me. I’ll help him from death but the rest is up to you and him.” 
She stood with arms folded as Longbow went into the hut. 

Coyote stood on the middle of a bridge staring at a misty wall of clouds facing him at the end of the bridge. He turned to his side and looked at his reflection on the water. He saw wolf’s golden eyes where Human eyes were stared at him from his reflection as he sensed a presence and looked to see Longbow on the opposite side of the bridge. Snow fell lightly coating the ground behind Longbow staring at him with identical eyes.
Longbow spoke “What about Brittany and your son?”
Coyote stared at Longbow who held up a hand and frowned. He looked at the water then slowly walked towards Longbow and reaching the man he gripped his hand. Coyote allowed himself pulled off the bridge as blackness arrived. 

Longbow came out of the hut as night fell and he walked up to Brittany standing watching him. 
Longbow spoke “I’ve done what I can. Now it’s your turn, Brittany. Go to him and do what you have to do.” 

Brittany nodded her head walking away entering the hut. She stood staring at Coyote’s form lying on the animal skin covered ground with a blanket over him. Brittany sighed and got to work. 

Coyote felt an urge and jerked his eyes open unseeing in the darkness. He heard a gasp sound as he sensed a female presence and reached for her. Hands touched his arms as he reached for her face bringing his lips to hers and pulled her down towards him. 
Coyote spoke recognizing the female form as he broke of the kiss “Brittany.”
He heard her speak “Coyote.” 
 
The light of the sun shined showing a new day. Coyote lay on his side eyes closed as light shined through an opening on top of the hut. He felt fur in his arms and opened his eyes with a jerk to face a snout. Coyote stared at the features of the white wolf with recognition on his face. He removed his arm to lie on his back as the wolf lifted its head and changed form to Brittany. Coyote stared at where he was inside a hut with a frown. His eyes eyed the gun lying on a hook on the hut’s wall then his eyes went to Brittany staring at him. He sat up with long blonde hair around his face as she sat up and felt her hand on his shoulder. Coyote placed a hand on hers as she rubbed his cheek with her other hand. He sighed loudly as he sensed her let go and watched her lean over to pick up folded animal skin clothing with shoe moccasins which she placed on his lap. 
Coyote spoke “I’ll need food and drink, Brittany.”
He saw Brittany nod her head then watched her get up walking naked to a set of folded clothing and shoe moccasins which he saw her put on her form then continue to stare at her putting her hair back in a braid. He frowned as she left the hut swishing the blanket behind her. He sighed loudly. 

Sam stood outside watching the hut where his parents were and watched as his Mother came out pushing aside the cloth hanging in the hut doorway dressed in animal skin clothing. 
She walked through the snow lying on the ground towards him as he spoke “Mom, about Father?”
Brittany reaching him hugged him and spoke “He’ll be alright.” 

Inside the hut Coyote stared at the gun hanging on the hook while dressed in the animal skin clothing. He staring at the gun pulled his blonde hair back and braided a low braid which he tied with a string. He stood up and walked towards the gun. He reached it as Longbow arrived into the hut with Brittany behind him carrying a cup and a bowl. They stood watching him as he fiddled with the gun hearing a click sound as he yanked the bullet out of it. He bent down towards his back pack riffling through it. He pulled out a metal box and opened it to place the bullet into it among other bullets then straightened up to stare at Longbow with Brittany behind him. Coyote with a frown on his face stared as Brittany wordlessly stepped forwards and handed him the bowl which he took. He went to sit on a bench made out of sticks standing next to him. Coyote ate the food ravenously with Brittany sitting on the bench next to him as Longbow stood watching with arms folded. Once done he handed the bowl to Brittany who handed it to Longbow and she handed him the cup which he gulped down. He tossed the cup to Longbow who caught it and watched him leave the hut as he leaned back against the wall. He felt Brittany’s hand touch his cheek which he closed his eyes pushing his face into her hand. He felt her arm go around him followed by her forehead touching the side of his face in place of her hand. Coyote sighed as his hand touched Brittany’s hand touching his leg which he gripped. 

"That's enough of that story due to that its nighttime now!" said Jason with his golden Human eyes glaring at the humanoids with identical Human like golden eyes dubbed themselves Hayu gathered around an eater light that was giving off warmth and surrounded by rocks around it with dirt ground and logs as Brianna called them. 
He heard multiple groaning noises from the offsprings of the Hayu as he added "You Hayu were all over the place with various points of views leaving me annoyed. Plus what's with the weird wording rhyming with it and duck anyway? Can't you focus onto one point of view and use language I could get it what your point is?"
He glared at the Hayu's leader a male with long white hair with identical golden eyes while wearing all white colored gonoid skin clothing Brianna dubbed them animal and the color white while Hayu dubbed him by the name of Nikolas who shrugged in response before the male spoke "Offsprings its time for you to go to bed and get some sleep which is a must for Hayu and manoids to have so move it now."
Jason folded his black covered arms and gloves of his black outfit skin suit with a jacket attached and gloves attached to the sleeves while giving multiple groaning offspring a glare as they each got up and went into huts some following each other and some following an adult Hayu. He stretched out his legs stiff from sitting so long on the log listening to Hayu adults telling their story of what they dreamed about while asleep and felt a hand on his shoulder which he looked to see a female Humanoid with twin eyes as his while wearing an all blue dress draped onto her form and having long black hair he on introduction was dubbed Brianna who claimed to him that his facial appearance was twin to a male humanoid hybrid of gonoid species she had as a mate named Eric and had always stuck close to him as his declared by the Hayu said mate wherever he went around their camp and the surrounding forest for various duties involving hunting for food and gathering eater food for eaters to eat on when it involved cooking the food over them including warmth and light to see at nighttime. 
Jason exhaled a breath and eyed Brianna who spoke "Well the wording rhyming with it and duck back where I came from are not appropriate for offsprings to hear and considered really bad language words for people to use."
He heard Nikolas groan loudly which he eyed who without a comment towards him got up and walked away which he saw him going into a hut. 
He resumed eyeing Brianna who added "Which reminds me its time for you, Jason to go into our hut for sleeping which I believe you need the rest period." 
Jason shrugged off Brianna's hand off his shoulder and got up groaning loudly while unfolding his arms stretching them above his head along with thrusting out his sword weapon hidden in a pocket in his left arm to grip it in his left hand as Brianna said after seeing him flaunt that weapon around the Hayu in their camp for cutting up captured dead gonoids for eating along with chopping branches found on the ground into pieces for the eater to eat. He heard a familiar noise from Brianna who earlier told him it involved her throat clearing itself which was a Human trait for Humans to use whenever getting people's attention as he looked at her to see a glare on her face and saw her jab a finger in a direction towards their hut he saw where she aimed it at. 
He exhaled a breath and flicked his wrist getting his sword back into his arm and without a word towards Brianna made a beeline towards the hut she pointed at only to get her hand grabbing his right hand and yanking him towards another hut while he heard her grumbling loudly "Can't tell which hut is ours despite the differences of the tree barks on them designed as always." 
He groaned loudly as she stopped her grumbling and got him inside their hut which he eyed her with night vision of yellow while kneeling on the fur covered ground as Brianna stood in front of him removing her dress showing her clad in some tight fitting clothes covering her sensitive parts. 
He frowned eyeing Brianna while feeling the urge to mate hit him as she spoke while removing her clothes and shoes baring herself to him "That word rhyming with duck is also another word for mating which I'm not kidding on that so lie down and be pleasured. I'm in the mood and I don't give a care if your not." 
Jason didn't give out a protest lied his form down and eyed Brianna while thinking to himself "At least I'm getting what I've been seeking."
He kept his eyes open while eyeing Brianna due to pretty sure he knew what she had in mind with her wording and clothes removal feeling himself fine with what she had in mind towards him.

The End.
